TBV_1.1–1.2	atra īśvara kṛta jagat vādinaḥ prāhuḥ yuktam uktam sarvajña praṇītam śāsanam tad praṇīta tvāt ca tat pramāṇam iti idam tu ayuktam rāga dveśa ādikān śatrūn jitavantaḥ iti jināḥ sāmānya yoginaḥ eva īśvara vyatiriktāḥ etad lakṣaṇa yoginaḥ na punar śāsana ādi sarva jagat sraṣṭā īśvaraḥ tathā ca patañjaliḥ kleśa karma vipāka āśayaiḥ aparāmṛṣṭaḥ puruṣa viśeṣaḥ īśvaraḥ 
TBV_1.3–1.4	 iti anena sūtreṇa rāga ādi lakṣana kleṣa ṣatru rahita tvam sahajam īśvarasya pratipāditam na punar vipakṣa bhāvanā ādi abhyāsa vyāpārāt kleśa ādi kṣayaḥ tasya yena rāga ādīn sva vyāpāreṇa jitavantaḥ iti vacaḥ sārthakam tad viṣaya tvena syāt tathā ca anyaiḥ api uktam jñānam apratigham yasya aiśvaryam ca jagatpateḥ vairāgyam ca eva dharmaḥ ca saha siddham catuṣṭayam 
TBV_1.5–1.7	 iti āśaṅkya āha bhava jiṇāṇam iti bhavanti nāraka tiryak nara amara paryāya tvena utpadyante prāṇinaḥ asmin iti bhavaḥ saṃsāraḥ tad hetu tvāt rāda ādayaḥ atra bhava śabdena upacārāt vivakṣitāḥ tam jitavantaḥ iti jināḥ upacārśrayaṇe ca prayojanam na hi avikala kāraṇe rāga ādau adhvaste tad kāryasya saṃsārasya jayaḥ śakyaḥ vidhātum iti pratīpādanam bhava kāraṇa bhūta rāga ādi jaye ca upāyaḥ pratipāditaḥ prāk tad upāyena ca vipakṣa rāga ādi jaya dvāreṇa tad kārya bhūtasya bhavasya jayaḥ saṃbhavati na anyathā iti na hi upāya vyatirekeṇa upeya siddhiḥ anyathā upeyasya nirhetuka tvena deśa kāla svabhāva pratiniyamaḥ na syāt iti sarva prāṇinām īśvara tvam na vā kasyacid syāt pratipāditaḥ ca ayam arthaḥ nityam sattvam asattvam vāhetoḥ anya anapekṣaṇāt apekṣātaḥ hi bhāvānām kādācid ka tva saṃbhavaḥ ityādinā granthena dharma kīrtinā tat na rāga ādi kleśa vigamaḥ svabhāvataḥ eva īśvarasya iti yuktam 
TBV_2.1	 atra bṛhaspati mata anusārinaḥ svabhāva saṃsiddha jñāna ādi dharma kalāpa adhyāsitasya sthāṇoḥ abhāva pratipādaṇam jainena kurvata asmākam sāhāyyam anuṣṭhitam iti manvānāḥ prāhuḥ yuktam uktam yat svabhāva saṃsiddha jñāna ādi saṃpad samanvitasya īśvarasya abhāvaḥ nāraka tiryagna rāma rūpa pariṇati svabhāva tayā utpadyante prāninaḥ asmin iti etat ca ayuktam abhihitam para loka sadbhāve pramāṇa abhāvāt tathā hi para loka sadbhāvā vedakam pramāṇam pratyakṣam anumānam āgamaḥ vā jainena abhyupagamanīyaḥ anyasya pramāṇa tvena tena aniṣṭeḥ na ca atra etat vaktavyam bhavataḥ api kim tad pratikṣepakam pramāṇam yatas na asmābhiḥ tad pratikṣepaka pramāṇāt tad abhāvaḥ pratipādyate kintu para upanyasta pramāṇa paryanuyoga matram eva kriyate atas eva 
TBV_2.2–2.5	 sarvatra paryanuyoga parāṇi eva sūtrāni bṛhaspateḥ iti cārvākaiḥ abhihitam sa ca para upanyasta pramāṇa paryanuyogaḥ tad abhyupagamasya praśna ādi dvāreṇa vicāraṇā na punar sva siddha pramāṇa upanyāsaḥ yena atīndriya artha pratikṣepaka tvena pravarttamānam pramāṇam āśraya asiddha tva ādi doṣa duṣṭa tvena katham pravarttate iti asmān prati bhavatā api paryanuyogaḥ kriyeta atas eva para loka prasādhaka pramāṇa abhupa gamam pareṇa grāhayitvā tad abhyupagamasya anena prakāreṇa vicāraḥ kriyate tatra na tāvat para loka pratipādaka tvena cakṣuḥ ādi karaṇa vyāpāra samāsādita ātma lābham sannihita pratiniyata rūpa ādi viṣaya tvāt pratyakṣam pravarttate na api atīnriyam yogi pratyakṣam tatra pravarttate iti vaktum śakyam para loka ādi vat tasya api asiddheḥ 
TBV_2.6^1	 na api anumānam pratyakṣa pūrvakam tatra pravṛttim āsādayati pratyakṣa apravṛttau tad pūrvakasya anumānasya api tatra apraṛtteḥ atha yadi api pratyakṣa avagata pratibandha liṅga prabhavam anumānam na tatra pravarrtate tathā api sāmānyatas dṛṣṭam tatra pravarttiṣyate tat api na yuktam yatas tat api sāmānyatas dṛṣṭam avagata pratibandha liṅga udbhavam āhosvit anavagata pratibandha liṅga samuttham yadi anavagata pratibandha liṅga udbhavam iti pakṣaḥ sa na yuktaḥ tathābhūta liṅga prabhavasya sva viṣaya vyabhicāreṇa aśva darśana anantara udbhūta rājya ācpti vikalpasya iva apramāṇa tvāt 
TBV_2.6^2	 atha pratipanna saṃbandha liṅga prabhavam tat tatra pravarttate iti pakṣaḥ saḥ api na yuktaḥ pratibandha avagamasya eva tatra liṅgasya asaṃbhavāt tathā hi pratyakṣasya tatra liṅga saṃbandha avagama nimittasya abhāve anumānam liṅga saṃbandha grāhakam abhupagantavyam tatra yadi tat eva para loka sadbhāvā vedakam anumānam sva viṣaya abhimatena arthena ātma utpāda kaliṅga saṃbandha grāhakam tadā itaretara āśraya tva doṣaḥ atha anumāna antarāt gṛhīta pratibandhāt liṅgāt upajāyamānam tat viṣayam tat abhyupagamyate tadā anavasthā tathā sarvam api anumānam asmān pratyasiddham tathā hi bṛhaspati sūtram 
TBV_2.7–2.9	 anumānam apramāṇam iti anena pratijñāna pratipādaṇam kṛtam aniścita artha pratipādaka tvāt siddha pramāṇau= hāsa vat iti hetu dṛṣṭāntau abhyūhyau viṣaya vicāreṇa vā anumāna prāmāṇyam ayuktam dharma dharmyu bhaya svatantra sādhane shidha sādhyatā yatas atas viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ sādhyaḥ prameya viśeṣayām pramām kurvat pramāṇam pramāṇa tām aśnute itaretara avacchinnaḥ ca samudāyaḥ atra prameyaḥ tad apekṣayā ca pakṣa dharma tva ādīnām anyatamasya api rūpasya aprasiddhiḥ na hi samudāydharma tā hetoḥ na api samudāyena anvayaḥ vyatirekaḥ vā dharmi mātra apekṣayā parkṣa dharma tve sādhya dhama apekṣayā ca vyāptau gauṇa tā iti uktam ca 
TBV_2.10–2.12	 pramāṇasya agauṇa tvāt anumānāt artha niścayaḥ durlabhaḥ iti dharmi dharma tā grahaṇe api na gauṇa tā parihāraḥ pratīyamāna apekṣayā gauṇa mukhya vyavahārasya cintya tvāt samudāyaḥ ca pratīyate eka deśa āśrayaṇena api trairūpyam ayuktam vyāpti asiddheḥ na hi sattā mātreṇa āvinā bhāvaḥ gamakaḥ api tu avagataḥ anyathā ati prasaṅgāt sa ca sakala sapakṣa vipakṣa apratyakṣīkaraṇe durvijñānaḥ asarva vidā tat uktam 
TBV_2.13–2.17	 gomān iti eva martyena bhāvyam aśvavatā api kim iti deśa kāla avasthā bhedena ca bhāvānām nānā tva avagamāt anāśvāsaḥ tat uktam avasthā deśa kālānām ityādi āha ca avinā abhau= a sambandhasya grahītum aśakya tvāt yat ca sāmānyasya tad viṣayasya abhāvāt sva artha para artha bheda asambhavāt viruddha anumāna virodhayoḥ sarvatra 
TBV_2.18	 sambhavāt kvacid ca viruddhāvi abicāriṇaḥ ityādi dūṣaṇa jālam tat anudghoṣaṇīyam eva yatas aniścita artha pratipādaka tvāt anumānam apramāṇam iti anumāna apramāṇa tā pratipādane kṛte śeṣa dūṣaṇa jālasya mṛta māraṇaa kalpa tvāt tatas anumānasya apramāṇa tvāt atīndriya para loka sadbhāva pratipādane kutas tasya pravṛttiḥ 
TBV_2.19–2.21	 atha idam eva janma pūrva janma antaram antareṇa na yuktam iti janma antara lakṣaṇasya para lokasya siddhiḥ iṣyate tat kim iyam arthāpattiḥ atha anumānam vā na tāvat arthāpattiḥ tad lakṣaṇa abhāvāt dṛṣṭaḥ śrutaḥ vā anyathā na upapadyate iti hi tasya alakṣaṇam vicakṣaṇaiḥ iṣyate na tu janma antaram antareṇa na upapattimat idam janma iti siddham mātā pitṛ sāmagrī mātrakeṇa tasya upapatteḥ tad māṭra hetuka tve ca anya parikalpanāyām atiprasaṅgāt 
TBV_2.22	 atha prajñā medhā ādayaḥ janma ādau abhyāsa pūrvakāḥ dṛṣṭāḥ katham atad pūrvakāḥ bhaveyuḥ na vahni pūrvakaḥ dhūmaḥ tad pūrvaka tām antareṇa kadācid api bhavan upalabdhaḥ tat api asat avinā abhau= a sambandhasya deśa kāla vyāpti lakṣaṇasya pratyakṣeṇa pratipattum aśakteḥ sannihita mātra pratipatti nimittam hi pratyakṣam upalabhyate na hi sakala deśa kālayoḥ vinā vahnim asambhavaḥ eva dhūmasya iti pratyakṣatas pratītiḥ yuktāḥ atas na dhūmaḥ api vahni pūrvakaḥ sarvatra pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām siddhaḥ iti kutas tena dṛṣṭāntena janma antara svarūpa para loka sādhanam tasmāt kecid prajñā medhā ādayaḥ tathābhūta abhyāsa pūrvakāḥ kecid mātā pitṛ śarīra pūrvakāḥ iti na ca prajñā ādayaḥ śarīrataḥ vyatiricyamāna svabhāvāḥ saṃvedana viṣaya tām upayānti śarīram ca tad anvaya vyatireka anuvṛttimat eva dṛṣṭam iti katham anyathā vyavasthām arhati 
TBV_2.23^1	 atha pūrva upātta adṛṣṭam antareṇa katham mātā pitṛ vilakṣaṇam śarīram nanu etena eva vyabhicāraḥ dṛśyate na hi sarvadā kāraṇa anurūpam eva kāryam tena vilakṣaṇāt api mātā pitṛ śarīrāt yadi prajñā megha ādibhiḥ vilakṣaṇam tat apatyasya śarīram upajāyeta kadācid tad ākāra anukāri tat kaḥ eva atre virodhaḥ yathā kaścid śālūkāt eva śālūkaḥ gomayāt tathā kaścid upadeśāt vikalpaḥ kaścid tad ākāra padārtha darśanāt atha darśanāt api vikalpaḥ pūrva vikalpa vāsanām antareṇa katham bhavet 
TBV_2.23^2–2.25	 tarhi gomayāt api śālūkaḥ katham śālūkam antareṇa iti etat api praṣṭavyam tasmāt kārya kāraṇa bhāva mātram eva etat tatra ca niyama abhāvāt vijñānāt api mātā pitṛ śarīrāt vijñānam upajāyatām atha vā yathā vikalpāt vyavahitāt api vikalpaḥ upajāyate tathā vyavahitāt api mātā pitṛ śarīrataḥ eva iti na bhedam paśyāmaḥ yathā ca eka mātā pitṛ śarīrāt aneka apatya utpattiḥ tathā ekasmāt eva brahmaṇaḥ prajā utpattiḥ iti na jāti antara parigrahaḥ kasyacid iti na para loka siddhiḥ na hi mātā pitṛ sambandha mātram eva para lokaḥ tathā iṣṭau abhyupagaman virodhāt atha anādyantaḥ ātmā asti tam āśritya para lokaḥ sādhyate na hi eka anubha vitṛ vyatirekeṇa anusandhānam sambhavati bhinna anubhavitarī anusandhāna adṛṣṭeḥ tat api uktam para lokinaḥ abhāvāt para loka abhāvaḥ iti vacanāt 
TBV_2.26	 na hi anādi anantaḥ ātmā pratyakṣa pramāṇa prasiddhaḥ anumānena ca itaretara āśraya doṣa prasaṅgaḥ siddhe ātmani eka rūpeṇa anusandhāna vikalpasya avinābhūta tve ātma siddheḥ tad siddheḥ ca anusandhānasya tad avinābhūta tva siddiḥ iti itaretara āśraya sadbhāvāt na ekasya api siddiḥ na ca asiddam asiddhena sādhyate kim ca darśana anusandhānayoḥ pūrva apara bhāvinoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ pratyakṣa siddhiḥ tat kutas anusandhāna smaraṇāt ātma siddhiḥ api ca śarīra antargatasya jñāvasya abhūta tvena katham janma antara śarīra sañcāraḥ atha antara abhava śarīra santatyā sañcaraṇam ucyate tat api para lokāt na viśiṣyate sañcāraḥ ca na dṛṣṭaḥ jīvate iha janmani maraṇa samaye bhaviṣyati iti duradhigamam etat na para loka siddhiḥ atha vā siddhe api para loke pratiniyata karma phala saṃbandha asidhdeḥ vyartham eva anumānena para loka astitva sādhanam atha āgamāt pratiniyata karma phala sambandha siddhiḥ tathā sati para loka astitvam api āgamāt eva siddam iti kim anumāna prayāsena 
TBV_2.27–2.28	 na ca āgamāt api para loka siddhiḥ tasya prāmāṇya asiddheḥ na ca apramāṇa siddham para loka ādikam abhyupagantum yuktam tad abhāvasya api tathā abhyupagama prasaṅgāt tat na para loka sādhaka pramāṇa pratipādanam akṛtvā bhāva śabda vyutpattiḥ artha saṃsparśini abhidhātum yuktāḥ  ithā ādi śabda vyutpatti tulyā tu yadi kriyate tadā na asmābhiḥ api tad pratipādaka pramāṇa paryanuyoge manaḥ praṇidhīyate iti pūrva pakṣaḥ 
TBV_3.1	 atra ucyate yat uktam paryanuyoga mātram asmābhiḥ kriyate iti tatra vaktavyam paryanuyogaḥ api kriyamāṇaḥ kim pramāṇataḥ kriyate uta apramāṇataḥ yadi pramāṇataḥ tat ayuktam yatas tad kārī api pramāṇam kim pratyakṣatam uta anumāna ādi yadi pratyakṣam tat ayuktam pratyakṣasya avicāraka tvena paryanuyoga svarūpa vicāra racanā catura tvāt 
TBV_3.2^1	 na ca pratyakṣasya api pramāṇa tvam yuktam bhavat abhyupagamena tad lakṣaṇā sambhavāt tad asambhavaḥ ca svarūpa vyavasthāpaka dharmasya lakṣaṇa tvāt tatra pratyakṣasya prāmāṇya svarūpa vyavasthāpakaḥ dharmaḥ avisaṃvādi tva lakṣaṇaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ tat ca avisaṃvādi tvam pratyakṣa prāmāṇyena avinābhūtam abhyupagamyam anyathā bhūtāt tatas pratyakṣa prāmāṇya asiddheḥ siddhau vā yatas kutaścid yat kiñcid anabhimatam api sidhyet iti atiprasaṅgaḥ sa ca avinābhāvaḥ tasya kutaṣcid pramāṇāt avagantavyaḥ anavagata pratibandhāt artha antara pratipattau nālikera dvīpa vāsinaḥ api anavagata pratibandhāt dhūmāt dhūmadhvaja pratipattiḥ syāt avinā abhāva avagamaḥ ca akhila deśa kāla vyāptyā pramāṇataḥ abhyupagamanīyaḥ anyathā yasyām eva pratykṣavyaktau saṃvādi tva prāmāṇyayoḥ asau avagataḥ tasyām eva avisaṃvādi tvāt tat sidhyet na vyakti antare tatra tasya anavagamāt 
TBV_3.2^2	 na ca avagata lakṣya lakṣaṇa sambandha avyaktiḥ deśa akāla antaram anuvartate tasyāḥ pratyakṣa vyakteḥ tadā eva dhvaṃsāt vyakti antarān anugamāt anugame vā vyakti rūpa tā virahāt anugatasya sāmānya rūpa tvāt tasya ca bhavatā anabhyupagamāt abhyupagame vā na sāmānya lakṣaṇa anumāna aviṣaya abhāva pratipādanena tad pratikṣepaḥ yuktaḥ sa ca pramāṇataḥ pratyakṣe lakṣya lakṣaṇayoḥ vyāptyā vinā abhāva avagamaḥ yadi pratyakṣāt abhyupagamyate tat ayuktam pratyakṣasi sa sannihita sva viṣaya pratibhāsa mātraḥ eva bhavatā vyāpāra abhyupagamāt atha ekatra vyaktau pratyakṣeṇa tayoḥ avisaṃvādi tva prāmāṇyayoḥ avinā abhāva avagamāt anyatra api evambhūtam pratyakṣam pramāṇam iti pratyakṣeṇa api lakṣya lakṣaṇayoḥ vyāptyā pratibandha avagamaḥ tarhi anyatra api evambhūtam jñāna lakṣaṇam kāryam evambhūta jñāna kārya prabhavam iti tena eva katham na sarva upasaṃhāreṇa kārya lakṣaṇa hetoḥ sva sādhya avinā abhāva avagamaḥ 
TBV_3.2^3	 yena anumānam apramāṇam avinā abhau= a sambandhasya vyāptyā grahītum aśakya tvāt iti dūṣaṇam anumāna vādinam prati bhavatā sajyamānam śobhate kim ca avisasṃvādi tva lakṣaṇaḥ dharmaḥ pratyakṣa prāmāṇya lakṣya vyavasthāpakaḥ pratyakṣa pratibaddha tvena niśceyaḥ anyathā tatra eva tatas prāmāṇya lakṣaṇa lakṣya vyavasthā na syāt asambaddhasya kenacid saha pratyāsatti vipra karṣa abhāvāt tadvat anyatra api tatas tad vyavasthā prasaṅgaḥ tathā abhyupagame ca yathā saṃvādi tva lakṣaṇaḥ dharmaḥ lakṣyānavagame api pratyakṣa dharmi sambandhi tvena avagamyate tathā dhūmaḥ api parvata eka deśe anala anavagatau api pradeśa sambandhi tayā avagamyate iti katham samudāyaḥ sādhyaḥ tad apekṣayā ca pakṣa dharma tvam hetoḥ avagantavyam na ca pakṣa dharma tva apratipattau sādhya dharma anala viśiṣṭa tad pradeśa pratipattiḥ pratipattau vā pakṣa dharma tva ādi anusaraṇam vyartham tad pratipatteḥ prāk eva tad utpatteḥ 
TBV_3.2^4–3.4^1	 samudāyasi sa sādhya tvena upacārāt tad eka deśa dharmi dharma tva avagame api pakṣa dharma tva avagamāt adoṣe upacaritaṇ pakṣa dharma tvam hetoḥ syāt iti anumānasya gauṇa tva āpatteḥ pramāṇasya agauṇa tvāt anumānāt artha nirṇayaḥ durlabhaḥ iti ca udya avasaraḥ pratyakṣa prāmāṇya lakṣaṇe api kriyamāṇe asya sarvasya samāna tvena pratipādita tvāt yadā ca avisaṃvādi tva lakṣaṇa pratyakṣa prāmāṇya lakṣyayoḥ sarva upasaṃhāreṇa vyāptiḥ abhyupagamyate avisaṃvādi tva lakṣaṇaḥ ca prāmāṇya vyavasthāpakaḥ dharmaḥ tatra aṅgīkriyate pūrva ukta nyāyena tadā katham anumānām na abhyupagamyate pramāṇa tayā 
TBV_3.2^4–3.4^2	 tathā hi yat kiñcid dṛṣṭam tasya yatra avinābhāvaḥ tad vidaḥ tasya tat gamakam tatra iti etāvat mātram eva anumānasya api lakṣaṇam tat ca pratyakṣa prāmāṇya lakṣaṇam abhyupagacchatā abhyupagamyate devānām priyeṇa tathā prāmāṇyam api anumānasya abhyupagatam eva yatas yat eva avisaṃvādi tva lakṣaṇam pratyakṣasya prāmāṇyam anumānasā api tat eva tat uktam arthasya asambhave abhāvāt pratyakṣe api pramāṇa tā pratibaddhasyabhāvasya tad hetu tve samam dvayam iti artha asambhave abhāvaḥ pratyakṣasya samvāda svabhāvaḥ prāmāṇye nimittam sa ca sādhya artha abhāve abhāvinaḥ liṅgāt upajāyamānasya anumānasya api samānaḥ iti katham na tasya api prāmāṇya abhyupagamaḥ 
TBV_3.5^1	 kim ca ayam cārvākaḥ pratyakṣa eka pramāṇa vādī yadi parebhyaḥ pratyakṣa lakṣaṇam anavabudhyamānebhya s tat pratipādayati tadā teṣām jñāna sambandhi tvam kutas pramāṇāt avagacchati na tāvat pratyakṣāt para cetaḥ vṛttīnām pratyakṣātaḥ jñātum aśakya tvāt kim tarhi sva ātmani jñāna pūrvakau vyāpāra vyāhārau pramāṇataḥ niścitya pareṣu api tathābhūta tad darśanāt tad sambandhi tvam avabudhyate tatas tebhyaḥ tat pratipādayati tathā abhyupagame ca vyāpāra vyāhāra ādeḥ liṅgasya jñāna sambandhi tva lakṣaṇa sva sādhya avyabhicāri tvam pakṣa dharma tvam ca abhyupagatam bhavati iti katham anumāna utthāpakasya arthasya trairūpyam asiddham yena na asmābhiḥ anumāna pratikṣepaḥ kriyate kim tu tri lakṣaṇam yat anumāna vādibhiḥ liṅgam abhyupagatam tat na lakṣaṇa bhāj bhavati iti pratipādyate iti vacaḥ śobhām anubhavati pratyakṣa lakṣaṇa pratipādana artham para cetaḥ vṛtti parijñāna abhyupagame tri lakṣāṇa hetu abhyupagamasya avaśyaṃbhāvi tva pratipādanāt 
TBV_3.5^2	 atha vā asmābhiḥ pratyakṣam api pramāṇa tvena abhyupagamyate yena tad lakṣaṇa praṇayane avaśyaṃbhāvī anumāna prāmāṇya abhyupagamaḥ iti asmān prati bhavadbhiḥ pratipādyeta yat tu pratyakṣām eva ekam pramāṇam iti vacanam tat tāntrika lakṣaṇa alakṣita loka saṃvyavahāri pratyakṣa apekṣayā atas eva lakṣaṇa lakṣita pratyakṣa apūrvaka anumānasya anumānam apramāṇam ityādi grantha sandarbheṇa aprāmāṇya pratipādanam vidhīyate na punar gopālāt yajña loka vyavahāra racanā caturasya dhūma darśana mātra āvirbhūta anala pratipatti rūpasya na etat cāru tasya api mahānasa ādi dṛṣṭānta dharmi pravṛtta pramāṇa avagatasu asādhya pratibandha niścita sādhya dharmi dharma dhūma bala udbhūta tvena tāntrika lakṣaṇa lakṣita pratyakṣā pūrvaka tvasya vastutas pradarśita tvāt 
TBV_3.5^3	 etat pakṣa dharma tvam iyam ca asya dhūmasya vyāptiḥ iti sa aṅketika vyavahārasya gopāla ādi mūrkha lokā sambhavinaḥ akiñcitkara tvāt pratyakṣasya ca avisaṃvādi tvam prāmāṇi lakṣaṇam tat yathā sambhavati tathā paratas prāmāṇyam vyavasthāpayadbhiḥ siddham iti etat pada vyākhyāyām darśitam na punar ucyate tat sthitam etat na pratyakṣasi sa bhavat abhiprāyeṇa prāmāṇya vyavasthāpaka lakṣaṇa sambhavaḥ tad bhāve vā anumānasya api prāmāṇya prasiddhiḥ iti na pratyakṣam paryanuyoga vidhāyi 
TBV_3.6^1	 na api anumāna ādikam paryanuyoga kāri anumāna ādeḥ pramāṇa tvena anabhyupagamāt atha asmābhiḥ yadi api anumāna ādikam na pramāṇa tayā abhyupagamyate tathā api pareṇa tat pramāṇa tayā abhyupagatam iti tad prasiddhena tena parasya paryanuyogaḥ vidhīyate nanu parasya tat pramāṇatam prāmāṇya abhyupagama viṣayaḥ atha apramāṇataḥ yadi pramāṇataḥ tadā bhavataḥ api pramāṇa viṣayaḥ tat syāt na hi pramāṇataḥ abhyupagamaḥ kasyacid bhavati kasyacid na iti yuktam atha apramāṇataḥ anumāṇa ādikam pramāṇa tayā abhyupagamyate pareṇa tadā pramāṇena na tena paryanuyogaḥ yuktaḥ apramāṇasya para loka sādhana vat tad sādhaka pramāṇa paryanuyoge api asāmarthyāt atha tena pramāṇa lakṣaṇa aparijñānāt tad prāmāṇyam abhyupagatam iti tad siddhena eva tena para loka ādi sādhana abhimata pramāṇa paryanuyogaḥ kriyate nanu ajñānāt tat parasya praṃāṇa tvena abhimatam na ca ajñānāt anyathā tvena abhimanyanānam vastu tad sādhyām artha kriyām anurvartayati anyathā viṣa tvena ajñaiḥ manyamānam mahauṣadha ādikam api tān mārtayitu kāmena dīyamānam sva kārya karaṇa kṣamam syāt 
TBV_3.6^2	 atha vā asmābhiḥ para loka prasādhaka pramāṇa paryanuyogaḥ anumāna ādinā svatantra prasiddha prāmāṇyena para abhyupagamau agata prāmāṇyena vā kriyate kim tarhi yadi para loka ādikaḥ a tīndriyaḥ arthaḥ pareṇa abhyupagamyate tadā tad pratipādakam pramāṇam vaktavyam pramāṇa nibandhanā hi prameya vyavasthitiḥ tasya ca pramāṇasya tad lakṣaṇa ādi asambhavena tad viṣaya abhimatasya api abhāvaḥ iti evaṃvicāraṇā lakṣaṇaḥ paryanuyogaḥ kriyate iti na svatantra anumāna upanyāsa pakṣa dharmya siddhi ādi lakṣaṇa doṣa avakāśaḥ bṛhaspati mata anusāriṇām nanu evam api anayā bhaṅgyā bhavatā para loka ādi ati indriya artha prasādhaka pramāṇa paryanuyoge prasaṅga sādhana ākhyam anumānam tad viparyaya svarūpam ca sva vācā eva pratipāditam bhavati 
TBV_3.7^1	 tathā hi pramāṇa nibandhanā prameya vyavasthitiḥ iti evam vadatā prameya vyavasthā pramāṇa nimittā eva pratipāditā bhavati etat ca prasaṅga sādhanam tat ca vyāpya vyāpaka bhāve siddhe yatra vyāpya abhyupagamaḥ vyāpaka abhyupagamanāṇtarīyakaḥ pradarśyate iti evaṃlakṣaṇam tena prameya vyavasthā pramāṇa pravṛttyā vyāptā pramāṇataḥ bhavatā pradarśanīyāḥ anyathā pramāṇa pravṛttim antareṇa api prameya vyavasthā syāt tatas ca katham para loka ādi sādhaka pramāṇa paryanuyoge api para loka vyavasthā na bhavet vyāpya vyāpaka bhāva grāhaka pramāṇa abhyupagame ca katham kārya hetoḥ svabhāva hetoḥ vā para loka ādi prasādhaka tvena pravartamānasya pratikṣepaḥ vyāpti prasādhaka pramāṇa sadbhāve anumāna pravṛtteḥ anāyāsa siddha tvāt 
TBV_3.7^2	 pramāṇa abhāve tad nibandhanāyāḥ prameya vyavasthāyāḥ api abhāvaḥ iti prasaṅga viparyayaḥ sa ca vyāpaka abhāve vyāpyasya api abhāvaḥ iti evam bhūta vyāpaka anupalabdhi samudbhūta anumāna svarūpaḥ etat api prasaṅga viparyaya rūpam anumānam pramāṇataḥ vyāpya vyāpaka bhāva siddhau pravartate iti vyāpti prasādhakasya pramāṇasya tad prasāda labhyasya ca anumānasya prāmāṇye sva vācā eva bhavatā dattaḥ sva hastaḥ iti na anumāna ādi prāmāṇya pratipādane asmābhiḥ prayasyate atas yat uktam sarvatra paryanuyoga parāṇi eva sūtrāṇi bṛhaspateḥ iti tat abhidheya śūnyam iva lakṣyate ukta nyāyāt 
TBV_3.8	 yat tu uktam pratyakṣām sannihita viṣaya tvena cakṣuḥ ādi prabhavam para loka ādi grāhaka tvena na pravartate tat na siddha sādhanam yat ca uktam na api atīndriyam yogi pratyakṣam para loka vat tasya asiddheḥ iti tat vismaraṇa śīlasya bhavataḥ vacanam atīndriya artha pravṛtti pravaṇasya yogi pratyakṣasya anantaram eva pratipādita tvāt yat punar idam ucyate na api pratyakṣa apūrvakam anumānam tad abhave pravartate tat asaṅgatam pratyakṣeṇa hi sambandha grahaṇa pūrvam parokṣe pāvaka ādau yathā anumānam pravartamānam upakabhyate saḥ eva nyāyaḥ para loka sādhane api anumānasya kim iti adṛṣṭaḥ duṣṭaḥ vā tathā hi yat kāryam tat kārya antara udbhūtam yathā paṭa ādi lakṣaṇam kāryam kāryam ca idam janma iti bhavati atas hetoḥ para loka siddhiḥ tathā hi 
TBV_3.9–3.10^1	 nityam sattvam asattvam vāhetoḥ anya anapekṣaṇāt apekṣātaḥ hi bhāvānām kādācid ka tva sambhavaḥ iti na tāvat kāryatvam ihajanmanaḥ na siddham akārya tve hetu nirapekṣasya nityam sattva asattva prasaṅgāt atha svabhāvataḥ eva kādācid ka tvam padārthānām abhaviṣyati na hi kārya kāraṇa bhāva pūrvaka tvam pratyakṣataḥ upalabdham yena tad abhāvāt nivarteta pratyakṣataḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvasya eva asiddheḥ yadi evam bāhyena api arthena saha kārya kāraṇa bhāvasya asiddheḥ sva saṃvedana mātra tve sati advaitam vicārataḥ tasya api abhāve sarva śūnya tvam iti sakala vyavahāra uccheda prasaktiḥ 
TBV_3.10^2	 tasmāt yathā pratyakṣeṇa bāhya artha pratibaddha tvam ātmanaḥ pratīyate anyathā iha lokasya api aprasiddheḥ pratyakṣataḥ tad janya svabhāva tvānavagame tasya tad grāhaka tva asambhavāt tathā ca iha loka sādhana artham aṅgīkartavyam pratyakṣam sva arthena ātmanaḥ pratibandha sādhakam tathā para loka sādhana artham api tat eva sādhanam iti siddhaḥ para lokaḥ aanumānataḥ yathā ca bāhya artha pratibaddha tvam pratyakṣasya kādācid ka tvena sādhyate dhūmasya api vahni pratibaddha tvam tathā iha janmanaḥ api kādācid ka tvena janma antara pratibaddha tvam api tatas anala bāhya arthavat para loke api siddham anumānam 
TBV_3.11^1	 atha iha janma ādi bhūta mātā pitṛ sāmagrī mātrāt api utpatteḥ kādācid ka tvam yuktam eva iha janmanaḥ nanu evam pradeśa asamanantara pratyaya mātra sāmagrī viśeṣāt eva dhūma pratyakṣa saṃvedanayoḥ kādācid ka tvam iti na sidhyati vahni bāhya artha pratītiḥ iti sakala vyavahāra abhāvaḥ atha ākāra viśeṣāt eva ananyathātva sambhavinaḥ anala bāhya artha siddhiḥ tarhi iha janmanaḥ api prajñā medhā ādi ākāra viśeṣataḥ eva mātā pitṛ vyatirikta nija janma antara siddiḥ 
TBV_3.11^2	 tathā yathā ākāra viśeṣaḥ eva ayam taimirika ādi jñāna vyāvṛttaḥ pratyakṣasya bāhya artham antareṇa na bhavati iti niścīyate anyathā bāhya artha asiddheḥ bauddha abhimata saṃvedanā dvaitam eva iti punar api vyavahāra abhāvaḥ tathā iha janma ādi bhūta prajñā viśeṣāt iha janma viśeṣa ākāraḥ nija janma antara pratibaddhaḥ iti niścīyatām anumānataḥ atha pratyakṣam eva sa vikalpakam paramārthataḥ pratipattuḥ tatas param punar vastu dharmaiḥ ityādi mīmāṃsaka ādi prasiddham sādhakam vahni bāhi artha pūrvaka tvasya dhūma ja agrat puras vṛtti stambha ādi pratyayasya atra abhyupagame para loka vādinaḥ sva pakṣam anāyāsa siddham eva manyante na hi dṛṣṭe anupapannam iti nyāyāt 
TBV_3.12	 yathā iva hi niścaya rūpā mātā pitṛ janma pratibaddha tva siddiḥ tathā eva iha janma saṃskāra vyāvṛttāt iha janma prajñā ādya ākāra viśeṣāt nija janma antara pratibaddha tva siddhiḥ api pratyakṣa niścitā syāt iti na para loka kṣatiḥ na ca niścaya pratyayaḥ anabhyāsa daśāyām anumāna tām atikrāmati pūrvarūpa sādharmyāt tat tathā aprasādhitam na anumeya tām atipatati iti nyāvāt anvaya vyatireka pakṣa dharmatā anusaraṇasya anabhyāsa daśāyām upalabdheḥ abhyāsa daśāyām ca pakṣa dharma tva ādi anusaraṇasya anyatra api asaṃvedanāt siddam anumāna pratita tvam para lokasya 
TBV_3.13	 atha itaretara āśraya doṣāt anumānam na asti eva evaṃvidhe viṣaye iti ucyeta nanu evam sati sarva bheda abhāvataḥ vyavahāra ucchedaḥ iti tad ucchedam anabhyupagacchatā vyavahāra arthinā avaśyam anumānam abhyupagantavyam etena pratyakṣa pūrvakatva abhāve api anumānasya prāmāṇyam pratipāditam na ca anumāna pūrvaka tve api itaretara āśraya doṣa anuṣaṅgaḥ tasya eva itaretara āśraya doṣasya vyavahāra pravṛttitaḥ nirākaraṇāt 
TBV_3.14	 yat api uktam anumāna pūrvaka tve anavasthā prasaṅgāt na anumāna pravṛttiḥ iti tat api asaṅgatam evam hi sati pratyakṣa gṛhīte api arthe vipratipatti viṣaye na anumāna pravṛttim antareṇa tad nirāsaḥ iti bāhye arthe pratyakṣasya avyāpārāt punar api advaita āpatteḥ śūnyatā āpatteḥ vā vyavahāra ucchedaḥ iti vyavahāra balāt sā eva anavasthā parihriyate iti abhyupagama vādena ca etat uktam anyathā bāhya artha vyavasthāpanāya pratyakṣam pravartate tathā pradarśita hetoḥ vyāpti prasādhana artham keṣāṃcid matena nirvikalpam anyeṣām tu sa vikalpakam cakṣuḥ ādi karaṇa vyāpāra janyam apareṣām mānasam keṣāṃcid vyāvṛtti grahaṇa upayogi jñānam anyeṣām pratyakṣa anupalambha bala udbhūta āliṅga joha ākhyam parokṣam pramāṇam tatra vyāpriyate iti katham anumānena pratibandha grahaṇe anavasthā itaretara āśraya doṣa prasaktiḥ para loka vādinaḥ prati bhavatā preryeta 
TBV_3.15–3.16	 yat api uktam sarvam api anumānam asmān prati pramāṇa tvena asiddham ityādi tat api asaṅgatam yatas kim anumāna mātrasya aprānāṇyam bhavatā pratipādayitum abhipretam anumānam apramānam ityādi granthena atha tāntrika lakṣāṇa kṣepaḥ atīndriya artha anumāna pratikṣepaḥ vā na tāvat anumāna mātra pratiṣedhaḥ yuktaḥ loka vyavahāra uccheda prasaṅgāt yatas pratiyanti kovidāḥ kasyacid arthasya darśane niyamataḥ kiñcid artha antaram na tu sarvasmāt sarvasya avagamaḥ uktam ca anayena sva gṛhāt nirgataḥ bhūyas na tat āgantum arhati 
TBV_3.17^1	 athaḥ kiñcid dṛṣṭvā kasyacid avagame nimittam kalpanīyam tat ca niyata sāhacaryam avinābhāva śabda vācyam naiyāyika ādibhiḥ parikalpitam tad avagamaḥ ca pratyakṣa anupalambha sahāya mānasa pratyakṣataḥ pratīyate sāmānya dvāreṇa pratibandha avagamāt deśa ādi vyabhicāraḥ na bādhakaḥ na api vyakti ānantyam ubhayatra api sāmānyasya eka tvāt sāmānya ākṛṣṭa aśeṣa vyakti pratibhānām ca mānase pratyakṣe yathā śata saṅkhyāvat cedena śatam iti pratyaye viśeṣaṇa ākṛṣṭānām pūrva gṛhītānām śata saṅkhyā viṣaya padārthānām tathā hi ete śatam iti pratyayaḥ bhavati eva sāmānyasya ca sattvam anugata ābādhita pratyaya viṣaya tvena vyavasthāpitam tat evam niyata sāhacaryam artha antaram pratipādayat upalabdham sat pratipādayati upalambhaḥ ca avaśyam kvacid sthitasya sā eva pakṣa dharma tā tatas sambandha anusmṛtau tatas sādhya avagamaḥ 
TBV_3.17^2	 yaḥ tu pratibandham na upaiti tasya api katham na sarvasmāt sarva pratipattiḥ abhyupagame vā apratipanne api sambandhe pratipatti prasaṅgaḥ pramātṛ saṃskāra kārakāṇām pūrva darśanānām abhāvāt iti anuttaram sambandha apratipattau pramātṛ saṃskāra anupapatteḥ darśana jaḥ saṃskāraḥ api anabhivyaktaḥ sattā mātreṇa na pratipatti upayogī na ca smṛtim antareṇa tad sadbhāvaḥ api na ca anubhava pradhvaṃsa nibandhanā smṛtiḥ kvacid viṣaye saṃskāram antareṇa tad anupapatteḥ pradhvaṃsasya ca nirhetuka tva asambhavāt yatra api abhyaste viṣaye vastu antara darśanāt avyavadhānena vastu antara pratipattiḥ tatra api prākta na krama āśrayaṇena vastu antara avagamaḥ iyān tu viśeṣaḥ ekatra anabhyasta tvāt antarāle smṛti saṃvedanam anyatra abhyāsāt vidyamānāyāḥ api asaṃvittiḥ 
TBV_3.18	 kecid tu yogi pratyakṣam sambandhgrāhakam āhuḥ vyāpteḥ sakala ākṣepeṇa avagamāt tathā ca yatra yatra iti deśa kāla vikṣiptānām vyaktīnām anavabhāsā anupapattiḥ atas ekatra kṣeṇe yogi tvam pratibandha grāhiṇaḥ etat pūrvasmāt aviśiṣṭam tat loke artha antara darśanāt artha antara su dṛḍhaptati itau tārkikāṇām nimitta cintāyām pakṣa dharma tva ādi abhidhānam atas na tāntrika lakṣaṇa pratikṣepe api 
TBV_3.19	 utpanna pratītīnām astu prāmāṇyam utpādya pratītīnām tu atīndriya adṛṣṭa para loka sarva jña ādi anumānānām pratikṣepaḥ iti ced tat asat yadi anavagata sambandhān pratipattṝn adhikṛtya etat ucyate tadā dhūma ādiṣu api tulyam atha gṛhīta avinā abhāvānām api atīndriya para loka ādi pratibhāsā anutpatteḥ evam ucyate tat asat ye hi kārya viśeṣasya tad viśeṣeṇa gṛḥītauvinābhāvāḥ te tasmāt para loka ādi avagacchati eva atas na jñāyate kena viśeṣaṇa atīndriya artha anumāna pratikṣepaḥ sāhacaryā viśeṣe api vyāpya gatā niyata tā prayojikā na vyāpaka gatā atas samavyāptikānām api vyāpya mukhena eva pratipattiḥ niyata tā avagame ca artha antara pratipattau na bādhā na pratibandhaḥ ekasya rūpa bheda anupapatteḥ tatas na viśeṣa viruddha sambhavaḥ na api viruddha avyabhicāriṇaḥ iti yat uktam viruddha anumāna virodhayoḥ sarvatra sambhavāt kvacid ca viruddha avyabhicāriṇaḥ iti etat api apāstam avinā abhau= a sambandhasya grahītum aśakya tvāt avasthā deśa kāla ādi bhedāt iti adeḥ ca pūrva nītya anumāna pramāṇa tve anupapattiḥ 
TBV_3.20–3.23	 parokṣasya arthasya sāmānya ākāreṇa anyatas pratipattau loka pratītāyām bauddhaiḥ tu kārya kāraṇa bhāva ādi lakṣāṇaḥ pratibandhaḥ tad nimitta tvena kalpitaḥ tat uktam kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt vā svabhāvāt vā niyāmakāt avinā abhau= a niyamaḥ adarśanāt na na darśanāt ityādi tathā avaśyaṃbhāva niyamaḥ kaḥ parasya anyathā paraiḥ artha antara nimitte vā dharme vāsasi rāga vat iti ca 
TBV_3.24^1	 tathā hi kvacid parvata ādi deśe dhūmaḥ upalabhyamānaḥ yadi agnim antareṇa eva syāt tadā pāvaka dharma anuvṛttitaḥ tasya tad kārya tvam yat niścitam viśiṣṭa pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām tat eva na syāt iti ahetoḥ tasya asasttvāt kvacid api upalambhaḥ na syāt sarvadā sarvatra sarva ākāreṇa vā upalambhaḥ syāt ahetoḥ sarvadā sattvāt svabhāvaḥ ca yadi bhāva vyatirekeṇa syāt tatas bhāvasya niḥsvabhāva tva āpatteḥ svabhāvasya api abhāva āpattiḥ tad pratibandha sādhakam ca pramāṇam kārya hetoḥ viśiṣṭa pratyakṣa anupalambha śabda vācyam pratyakṣam eva sarvajña sādhaka hetu pratibandha niścaya prastāve pradarśitam 
TBV_3.24^2	 svabhāva hetoḥ tu kasyacid viparyaye bādhakam pramāṇam vyāpaka anupalabdhi svarūpam kasyacid tu viśiṣṭam pratykṣam abhyupagatam sarvathā sāmānya dvāreṇa vyaktīnām atadrūpa parāvṛtta vyakti rūpeṇa vā tāsām pratibandhaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ anyathāpratibaddhāt anyatas anya pratipattau atiprasaṅgāt pratipandha prasādhakam ca pramāṇam avaśyam abhyupagamanīyam anyathā gṛhīta pratibandha tvāt anyatas anya pratipattau api prasaṅgaḥ tad avasthaḥ eva yatra gṛhīta pratibandhaḥ asau arthaḥ upalabhyamāṇaḥ sādhya siddhim vidadhāti tad dharmatā tasya pakṣa dharma tva svarūpā tad grāhakam ca pramāṇam pratyakṣam anumānam vā tat uktam dharma kīrtiṇā 
TBV_3.25–3.26	 pakṣa dharma tā niścayaḥ pratyakṣataḥ anumānataḥ vā atas loka prasiddha tāntrika lakṣaṇa lakṣita anumānayoḥ bheda abhāvāt atīndriya para loka ādi artha sādhaka tvam api tasya eva iti tad prāmāṇya anabhyupagame ihalokasya api abhyupagama abhāva prasaṅgaḥ na ca kim atra nirvikalpakam yogi pratyakṣam ūhaḥ vā pratibandha niścāyakam pratibandhaḥ api niyata sāha carya lakṣāṇaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva ādiḥ vā iti cintātra upayoginī dhūmāt agni pratipatti vat prajñā medhā ādi nijñāna kārya viśeṣāt nija janma antara vijñāna svabhāva para loka pratipatti siddheḥ atas anumāna aprāmāṇya pratipādanāya pūrva pakṣa vādinā yat yukti jālam upavyastam tat nirastam draṣṭavyam pratipadam uccārya na dūṣyate grantha gaurava bhayāt 
TBV_3.27	 yat api uktam para loke pratyakṣasya apravṛtteḥ arthāpatteḥ eva iyam iha jamnāni atha anupapattyā para loka sadbhāvaḥ iti tat api na samyak pūrva anusareṇa sarvasya niyata pratyayasya pravṛtteḥ anumāna tva pratipādanāt avinā abhau= a sambandhasya grahītum aśakya tvāt na atra anumānam iti ced nanu evam tat eva advaitam śūnya tvam vā kasya kena doṣa abhidhānam tasmāt saṃvyavahāra kāriṇā pratyakṣena ūhena vā pratibandha siddhiḥ iti katham na anumānāt para loka siddiḥ 
TBV_3.28^1	 yat api uktam mātā pitṛ sāmagrī mātreṇa iha janma sambhavān na tad janma vyatirikta bhūta para loka sādhanam yuktam iti tat api prativihitam eva samanantara pratyaya mātreṇa pratyaya pratyakṣasya bhāvāt svapna ādi pratyaya vat na pratyakṣāt bāhya artha siddhiḥ api iti bauddha abhimata pakṣa siddhi prasaṅgaḥ anasta tvāt yat api pratyapādi na sannihita mātra viṣaya tvāt pratyakṣasya deśa kāla vyāptyā pratibandha grahaṇa sāmarthyam iti tat api na kiñcid evam sati ati sannihita viṣaya tvena pratyakṣasya sva rūpa mātre eva pravṛtti prasaṅgaḥ iti tat eva bauddha ādi abhimatam sva saṃvedana mātram sarva vyavahāra uccheda kāri prasaktam iti pratipādita tvāt 
TBV_3.28^2	 tasmāt loka vyavahāra pravarttana kṣamasa vikalpaka pratyakṣa balāt ūhā ākhya pramāṇāt vā deśa kāla vyāptyā yathā ukta lakṣaṇasya hetoḥ pratibandha grahaṇe pravṛttiḥ anumānasya iti na vyāhatiḥ prakṛtasya iti etat api nirastam kecid prajñā ādayaḥ ityādi na ca prajñā medhā ādayaḥ śarīra svabhāva antargatāḥ ityādi codyam yuktam tad antargata tve api parihāra sambhavāt anvaya vyatirekābhyām teṣām mātā pitroḥ pitṛ śarīra janya tvasya pitṛ śarīram tarhi hetu bhedāt na bhedaḥ mātā pitṛ śarīrāt apatya prajñā ādīnām ayam aparaḥ bṛhaspati mata anusāriṇaḥ eva doṣaḥ astu yaḥ kārya bhede api kāraṇa bhedam na icchati 
TBV_3.28^3	 asmākam tu harṣa viṣāda ādi aneka viruddha dharma ākrāntasya vijñānasya antar mukha ākāra tayā vedyasya rūpa rasa gandha sparśa ādi yugapad bhā vibāla kumāra yauvana vṛddha avasthā ādi aneka krama bhāvi viruddha dharma abhyāsita tad śarīra ādeḥ bāhya indriya prabhava vijñāna samadhigamyāt bhedaḥ siddhaḥ eva viruddha dharma adhyāsaḥ kāraṇa bhedaḥ ca padārthānām bhedakaḥ sa ca jala analayoḥ iva śarīra vijñānayoḥ vidyate eva iti katham na tayoḥ bhedaḥ tad bhedāt api abhede brahmādvaitavāda āpatteḥ tad avasthaḥ eva pṛthivī āditatva catuṣṭaya abhāva āpattyā vyavahāra ucchedaḥ athavā mātā pitṛ pūrva janma eka sāmagrī janyam etat kāryam tat na doṣaḥ avyatirikta pakṣe api vijñāna śarīrayoḥ 
TBV_3.28^4	 pūrvam api uktam vilakṣanāt api anvaya vyatirekābhyām mātā pitṛ śarīrāt vijñānam upajāyatām na hi kāraṇa ākāram eva sakalam kāryam iti tat api asat yatas na hi kāraṇa vilakṣaṇam kāryam na bhavati ipi ucyate api tu tad anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānāt tad kārya tvam tathā hi yat yat vikāra anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyi tat tad kāryam iti vyavasthāpyate yathā aguru karpūra ūrṇādi dāhya dāhaka pāvaka gata surabhi gandha ādi anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyī dhūmaḥ tad kāryatayā vyavasthitaḥ eka santati anupatita śāstra saṃskāra ādi saṃskṛta prāktana vijñāna dharma anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyi ca prajñā medhā ādi uttara vijñānam iti katham na tat kāṛyam abhyupagamyate tat anabhyupagame dhūma ādeḥ api prasiddha vahni ādi kāryasya tad kāryatva aprasiddhiḥ iti punar api sakala vyavahāra ucchedaḥ 
TBV_3.29–3.31	 tasmāt yasya eva saṃskāram niyamena anuvartate tat na antarīyakam cittam atas citta samāśritam pratipāditaḥ ca pramāṇataḥ pratiniyataḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ sarvajña sādhane kusamaya visāsaṇam iti padavyākhyām kurvadbhiḥ na punar iha ucyate yaḥ api śālūka dṛṣṭāntena vyabhicāraḥ yathā gomayāt api śālūkaḥ kaścid samāna jātīyāt api śālūkāt eva tathā kecid prajñā medhā ādayaḥ tad abhyāsāt kecid tu rasāyana upayogāt 
TBV_3.32	 apare mātā pitṛ śukra śoṇita viṣa īśāt eva iti saḥ api na samyak tatra api samāna jātīya pūrva abhyāsa sambhavāt anyathā samāne api rasāyana ādi upayoge yamalakayoḥ kasyacid kvāpi prajñā medhā ādikam iti pratiniyamaḥ na syāt rasāyana ādi upayogasya sādhāraṇa tvāt iti na ca prajñā ādīnām janma ādau rasāyana abhyāde ca viśeṣaḥ śālūka gomaya janyasya tu śālūka ādeḥ tad anyasmāt viśeṣaḥ dṛśyate kvacid jāti smaraṇam ca darśanam iti na yuktā dṛṣṭa kāraṇāt eva māṭā pitṛ śarīrāt prajñā medhā ādi kārya viśeṣa utpattiḥ na ca gomaya śālūka ādeḥ vyabhicāra viṣaya tvena pratipāditasya atyanta vailakṣaṇyam rūpa rasa gandha sparśa vat pudgala pariṇāma tvena dvayoḥ api availakṣaṇyāt vijñāna śarīrayoḥ ca antar bahirmukha ākāra vijñāna grāhya tayā sva para saṃvedya tayā sva saṃvedana bāhya karaṇa ādi janya pratyaya anubhūyamāna tayā ca parasparān anuyāyi aneka viruddha dharma adhyāsataḥ atyanta vailakṣaṇyasya pratipādita tvāt na upādāna upādeya bhāvaḥ yuktaḥ 
TBV_3.33	 yaḥ tu śarīra vṛddhi ādeḥ caitanya vṛddhi ādi lakṣaṇaḥ upādāna upādeya bhāva dharma upalambhaḥ pratipādyate asau mahā kāyasya api mātaṅga ajagara ādeḥ caitanya alpa tvena vyabhicāri iti na tad bhāva sādhakaḥ yaḥ tu śarīra vikārāat caitanya vikāra upalambha lakṣaṇaḥ tad dharma bhāvaḥ pratipādyate asau api sāttvika sattvānām anya gata cittānām vā cheda ādi lakṣaṇa śarīra vikāra sadbhāve api tad citta vikāra anupalabdheḥ asiddhaḥ dṛśyate ca sahakāri viśeṣāt api jala bhūmi ādi lakṣaṇāt bīja upādānasya aṅkura ādeḥ viśeṣaḥ iti sahakāri kāraṇa tve api śarīra ādeḥ viśiṣṭa āhāra ādi upayoga ādau yauvanāvastāyām vā śāstra ādi saṃskāra upātta viśeṣa pūrva jñāna upādānasya vijñānasya vivṛddhi lakṣaṇaḥ viśeṣaḥ na asambhavī 
TBV_3.34	 yat api uktam anādi mātā pitṛ paramparāyām tathābhūtasya api bodhasya vyavahita mātā pitṛ gatasya sadbhāvāt tatas vāsanā prabodhena yuktaḥ eva prajñā medhā ādi viśeṣasya sambhavaḥ iti tat api ayuktam anantarasya api mātā pitṛ pāṇḍiti asya prāyas prabodha sambhavāt tatas cakṣuḥ ādi karaṇa janitasya svarūpa saṃvedanasya cakṣuḥ ādi jñānasya vā yugapad krameṇa ca utpattau mayā eva upalabdham etat iti pratyabhijñānam santāna antara tad apatya jñānānām api syāt na ca mātā pitṛ jñāna upalabdheḥ tad apatya ādeḥ kasyacid pratyabhijñānam upalabhyate anena ekasmāt brahmaṇaḥ prajā utpattiḥ pratyuktāḥ eka prabhava tve hi sarva prāṇinām parasparam pratyabhijñā prasaṅgaḥ eka santāna udbhūta darśana sparśana pratyayoḥ iva 
TBV_3.35^1	 yat uktam ātmānaḥ adṛṣṭeḥ na ātmānam āśritya para lokaḥ iti tat ayuktam tad adṛṣṭi asiddheḥ tathā hi deha indriya viṣaya ādi vyatiriktaḥ ahaṃpratyaya pratyakṣa upalabhya eva ātmā na ca cakṣuḥ ādeḥ karaṇa grāmasya atīndriya ātma viṣāya tvena jñāna jananāvyāparāt katham tad janya pratyakṣa jñāna viṣayaḥ iti vaktum yuktam sva sambedana pratyakṣa grāhya tva abhyupagamāt tathā hi upasaṃhṛta sakala indriya vyāpārasya andhakāra sthitasya ca aham iti jñānam sarva prāṇinām upajāyamānam sva saṃviditam anubhūyate tatra ca śarīra ādi anavabhāse api tad vyatiriktam ātma svarūpam pratibhāti na ca etat jñānam anubhūyamānam api apahnotum śakyam anubhūyamānasya api apalāpe sarva apalāpa prasaṅgāt na api etat na utpadyate kādācitka tva virodhāt na api bāhya indriya vyāpāra prabhavam tad vyāpāra abhāve api upajāyam āva tvāt na api śabda liṅga ādi nimitta udbhūtam tad abhāve api utpatti darśanāt na ca idam bādhya tvena apramāṇam tatra bādhaka sadbhāvasya asiddheḥ 
TBV_3.35^2	 na ca idam sa vikalpaka tvena apramāṇam sa vikalpakasya api jñānasya pramāṇa tvena pratipādayiṣyamāṇa tvāt kadācid ca bāhya indri avyāpāra kāle api yadā ghaṭam aham jānāmi iti evam viṣayam avagacchati tadā sva ātmānam api tathā hi tatra yathā viṣayasya avabhāsaḥ karma tayā tathā ātmanaḥ api anabhāsaḥ kartṛ tayā na ca śarīra ādīnām jñātṛ tā yathā hi śarīrāt vyatiriktā ghaṭa ādayaḥ pratīti karma tayā pratibhānti mama ghaṭa ādayaḥ aham ghaṭa ādīnām jñātāḥ evam mama śarīra ādayaḥ aham śarīra ādīnām jñātāḥ iti evam ca pratīti karma tvena ghaṭa ādibhiḥ tulya tvāt na śarīra ādi saṅghātasya jñātṛ tā na ca jñātra pratibhāsam tad apratibhāse hi mama ete bhāvāḥ pratibhānti na anyasya iti evam pratibhāsaḥ na syāt tat avabhāsa apahnave ca ghaṭa ādeḥ api katham pratītiḥ iyān tu viśeṣaḥ ekasya pratīti karmatā aparasya tad pratīti kartṛ tā na tu anavabhāsaḥ atas liṅga ādi anapekṣaḥ ātma avabhāsaḥ api asti iti katham tasya adṛṣṭiḥ 
TBV_3.36–3.37	 katham tasya adṛṣṭiḥ na ca asya pratyayasya bādhā rahitasya apūrva artha viṣayasya akṣaja viṣaya avabhāsasya iva asan digdha rūpasya niścita rūpa tvena pratibhāsamānasya smṛti rūpa tā aprāmāṇayam na pratipādayitum yuktam atas asyām api pratītau avabhāsamāvasya aparokṣa tā eva yuktā na pramāṇa antara gamya tā yat api atra āhuḥ asti ayam avabhāsaḥ kid tu asya pratykṣatā cintyāḥ pratyakṣam hi indriya vyāpāra jam jñānam tadā ca uktam bhavadbhiḥ indriyānām sat samprayoge buddhi janma pratyakṣam pratyakṣa viṣaya tvāt tad arthasya pratyakṣatā na tu sākṣāt anindriya ja tvena tatra ghaṭa ādeḥ bāhya indriya jñāna viṣaya tvena sarva loka pratīta adhyakṣatā na tu evam ātmanaḥ 
TBV_3.38^1	 atha evam ucyeta na ātmanaḥ ghaṭa ādi tulyā pratyakṣatā ghaṭa ādeḥ hi indriya ja jñāna viṣaya tvena sā vyavasthāpyate na tu ātmā kasyacid pramāṇasya viṣayaḥ katham tarhi pratyakṣaḥ na jñāna viṣaya tvāt pratyakṣaḥ api tu aparokṣā tvena pratibhāsanāt pratyakṣaḥ ucyate tat ca kevalasya ghaṭa ādi prati iti antargatasya vā apara sa adhanam prāk pratipāditam etat api asat yatas apara sādhanam iti kaḥ arthaḥ kim cit rūpasya sattā āhosvit sva pratītau vyāpāraḥ yadi cit rūpasya sattā eva ātma prakāśanam ucyate tadā dṛṣṭāntaḥ vaktavyaḥ 
TBV_3.38^2	 na ca atra aśaṅkanīyam aparokṣe dṛṣṭānta anveṣaṇam na kartavyam yatas tathāvidhe vivāda viṣaye su prasiddham dṛṣṭānta anveṣaṇam dṛśyate na ca dīpa ādi dṛṣṭāntaḥ tatra hi sajātīya āloka anapekṣa tvena sva pratītau sva prakāśaka tvam vyavasthāpitam kaiścid na tu indriya agrāhya tvam tat agrāhya tve sva prakāśāḥ pradīpa ādayaḥ iti cakṣuṣmatā abhiva andhānām api tad pratīti prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt na sva prakāśāḥ pradīpa ādayaḥ yat tu āloka antara nirapekṣa tvam tat kasyacid viṣayasya kācid sāmagrī prakāśikāḥ iti na ekatra dṛṣṭa tvena anyatra api prasaktiḥ codyate 
TBV_3.38^3	 atha dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ saḥ api ayuktaḥ adarśanāt eva na hi kaścid padārthaḥ kartṛūpaḥ karaṇa rūpaḥ vā sva ātmani karmaṇi iva sa vyāpāraḥ dṛṣṭaḥ katham tarhi anumeya tve api ātma pratītiḥ pramātṛ antara abhāvāt ekasya eva liṅga ādi karaṇam apekṣya avasthā bhedena bhede sati adoṣāḥ kim ca pramāṇa viṣaya tve api apara ukṣata iti asya bhāṣitasya kaḥ arthaḥ jñātṛ tayā sva rūpeṇa avabhāsanam iti ced ghaṭa āsyaḥ api kim para rūpa tayā pratīti viṣayāḥ atas yat yasya rūpam tat pramāṇa viṣaya tve api avasīyate iti na jñāna aviṣayatā pramātuḥ 
TBV_3.38^4	 tathā hi tasya jñātṛ tā pramātṛ tā ātma svarūpa tā ghaṭa ādeḥ prameya tām jñeya tā ghaṭa ādi rūpa tā atas yathā tasya sva rūpeṇa avabhāsanāt na apratyakṣa tā tadvat ātmanaḥ api abhyupagamanīyam ca etat anyathā ātma ādi sva saṃvedanasya pratyakṣasya api pratyakṣa ādi lakṣaṇa vyatiriktam lakṣaṇa antaram vaktavyam tathā ca pramāṇeyatta avyāghātaḥ kenacid pratyakṣa ādi lakṣaṇena ātma ādi viṣayasya sva saṃvedanasya asaṅgrahāt itas api uktam pramātṛ vat phale api saṃvedana abhyupagama prasaṅgāt tathā abhyupagamāt adoṣaḥ iti ced tathā ca uktam 
TBV_3.39–3.40	 saṃvittiḥ saṃvitti tayā eva saṃvedyāḥ na saṃvedya tayā iti etat prāk pratikṣiptam na svarūpa avabhāse pramāṇa aviṣaya tā kim ca evam kalpyamāne bodha dvayam āntaram sva saṃvid rūpam ca kalpitam syāt tathā ca ayuktam ekasmāt eva viṣaya avabhāsa siddheḥ kim dvaya kalpanayā atha ucyate kalpanā hi anavabhāsamānasya bodha dvaye tu ghaṭa ādi vat avabhāsaḥ asti iti na kalpanā yadi īdṛśāḥ pratibhāsāḥ pramāṇa tvena vyavasthāpyante tadā ghaṭam aham cakṣuṣā paśyāmi iti karaṇa pratītiḥ api pramātṛ phala pratīti vat kalpanīyāḥ 
TBV_3.41	 yā api kaiścid karaṇa pratītiḥ pratakṣa tvena uktā sā api na atīva saṅgacchate tathā hi ghaṭam aham cakṣuṣā paśyāmi iti asyām avagatau kim golakasya cakṣuṣṭvam āhosvit tad avyatiriktasya golakasya cakṣuṣṭve na kaścid andhaḥ syāt tad vyatiriktasya ca raśmeḥ anaghi upagamaḥ abhyupagame vā na pratīti viṣayaḥ kevalam śabda mātram uccārayati ghaṭa pratīti kāle evam ca pramātṛ phala viṣayam śabda uccāraṇa mātram avasīyate na ca tayoḥ pratīti gocara tā karaṇasya iva tathā hi indriya vyāpāre sati śarīrāt vyavacchinnasya viṣayasya eva kevalasya avabhāsanam iti nyāya vidaḥ pratipannāḥ 
TBV_3.42–3.43	 kim tasya avabhāsanam iti paryanuyoge mūka tvam parihāram āhuḥ vyapadeṣṭum aśakya tvāt atas pramātṛ avabhāsā anupapattiḥ nanu aham iti pratyayaḥ sarva loka sākṣikaḥ na eva apahnotum śakyaḥ anapahnave sa viṣayaḥ nirviṣayaḥ vā nirviṣayatā pratyayānām abādhita rūpāṇām katham sa viṣaya tve api pramātra pratibhāse kiṃviṣayaḥ ayam pratyayāt na pratyaya apahnavaḥ na ca asya nirviṣayatā kin tu deha ādi vyatiriktaḥ viṣaya tvena avabhāsamānaḥ ātmā asya na viṣayaḥ na ca jñātṛ tvena avabhāsamānaḥ iti ucyate kaḥ tarhi viṣayaḥ śarīram iti brūmaḥ tathā hi kṛśaḥ aham sthūlaḥ aham gauraḥ aham iti śarīra ādi ālambanaiḥ pratyayaiṛ asya samāna adhikaraṇa tāvasīyate 
TBV_3.44	 nanu evam sukhya ādi pratyayaiḥ api ahaṅkārasya samāna adhikaraṇa tā sukhī aham duḥkhī aham iti vai atas na deha viṣaya tā yat codyate gauraḥ aham ityādi sāmāna adhikaraṇya darśanāt śarīra ālambana tvam iti tatra api etat vicāryam gaura ādīnām śarīra ādi vyatiriktānām anahaṅkāra āspada tvam dṛṣṭam tadvat śarīra ādi gatānām api yuktam vyavasthāpayitum tathā ca vārttika kṛta uktam na hi asya draṣṭuḥ yat etat mama gauram rūpam saḥ aham iti bhavati pratyayaḥ kevalam matu blopam kṛtvā evam nirdarśati ayam arthaḥ śarīre ahaṅkāraḥ aupacārikaḥ na tāttvikaḥ yathā anyasmin tad kārya kāriṇī atyanta nikaṭe ahaṅkāṛaḥ gauṇaḥ yaḥ ayam saḥ aham iti evam śarīre api atas nimittāt ayam etasmin tu ubhaysampratipanne anātma rūpe idaṃtā pratyaya viṣaye ahaṅkāraḥ tatas eva śarīre api ātma viṣayaḥ tu ahaṅkāraḥ na aupacārikaḥ idaṃpratyaya asambhinna ahaṃpratyaya pratibhāsi tvāt pramātā śarīra ādi vyatiriktaḥ 
TBV_3.45^1	 etat eva katham mama idam śarīram iti pratyaya upādānāt mama ayam ātmā iti pratyaya abhāvāt ca nanu mama ayam ātmā iti kim na bhavati pratyayaḥ na bhavati iti bhrūmaḥ katham tarhi evam ucyate kevalam śabdaḥ uccāryate na tu pratyayasya sambhavaḥ atra api mama pratyaya pratibhāsasya adarśanāt śabda uccāraṇa mātram kena vāryate kim idānīm sukha ādi yogaḥ śarīrasya iṣyate na evam sukha ādi yoga abhāvāt mithyā pratyayaḥ ayam sukhī aham iti na tu etad alambanaḥ 
TBV_3.45^2	 atas vyavasthitam jñātṛ pratibhāsā darśanāt pratibhāse vā śarīrasya jñātṛ tvena avabhāsanāt na deha ādi vyatiriktasya ahaṃpratyaya viṣaya tā śarīrasya ca jñātṛ tvena avabhāsamānasya api pramāṇa siddhāḥ buddhi yoga niṣedhāt mithyā pratyaya ālambanatā na tu tasya ācaitanye anyaḥ kaścid jñātā pratyakṣa pramāṇa viṣayaḥ sidhyati ityādi tat api asaṅgatam yatas bhavatu jaiminīyānām sat samprayoge puruṣasya indriyāṇām buddhi janma pratyakṣam iti lakṣaṇa lakṣita indriya prataykṣa vādinām aham iti anabhāsa pratyayasya anindriya ja tvena atra apratyakṣa ātva doṣaḥ na asmākam jina matta anusāriṇām na hi asmākam indriya jam eva pratyakṣam kim tu yat yatra viśadam jñānam indriyān indriya nimittam tat tatra pratyakṣam iti abhyupagamāt tat indriyān indriya nimittam iti vācaka mukhya vacanāt 
TBV_3.45^3	 tena yathā pratyakṣa viṣaya tvena ghaṭa ādeḥ pratyakṣatā tathā ātmanaḥ api dva saṃvedana adhyakṣatāyām kaḥ virodhaḥ atas eva yat ucyate ghaṭa ādeḥ bhinna jñāna grāhya tvena pratyakṣatā vyavasthāpyate ātmanasu aparokṣa tvena pratibhāsanāt pratyakṣa tvam tat ca kevalasya ghaṭa ādi prati iti antargatasya vā apara sa adhanam prāk pratipāditam iti atra apara sādhanam iti kaḥ arthaḥ kim cit rūpasya sattā ahosvit dva pratītau vyāpātaḥ iti pakṣa dvayam utthāpya prathama pakṣe cit rūpasya sattā eva ātma prakāśanam yaḥ ucyate tadā dṛṣṭāntaḥ vaktavyaḥ iti tat nirastam adhyakṣa pratīte artha dṛṣṭānta anveṣaṇasya ayukta tvāt 
TBV_3.46	 atha vivāda gocare adhyakṣa pratīte api dṛṣṭānta anveṣaṇam loke su prasiddham iti saḥ atra api vaktavya s tadā asya iva pradīpa ādi lakṣaṇaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ api jñānasya prakāśam prati sajātīya aparān apekṣaṇe sādhye tathā hi yathā pradīpa ādi ālokaḥ na sva pratipattau āloka antaram apekṣate tathā jñānam api sva pratipattau na samāna jātīyajña apekṣam etāvat mātreṇa ālokasya dṛṣṭānta tvam na punar tasya api jñāna tvam āsādyate yena indriya agrāhya tvāt cakṣuṣmatām iva andhānām api tad pratīti prasaṅgaḥ iti preryate na hi dṛṣṭānte sādhya dharmi dharmāḥ sarve api āsan jayitum yuktāḥ anyathā ghaṭe api śabha dharmāḥ śabda tva ādayaḥ prasajyeran iti tasya api śrotra grāhya tva prasaṅgaḥ na ca sādharmya dṛṣṭāntam antareṇa pramāṇa pratītasya api arthasya aprasiddiḥ iti śakyam vaktum anyathā jīvat śarīrasya api sa ātmaka tve sādhye tadvat tad prasiddha dṛṣṭāntasya abhāvāt prāṇa ādimattva ādeḥ tad siddhiḥ va syāt 
TBV_3.47–3.48	 atha sādharmya dṛṣṭānta abhāve api dṛṣṭa vaidharmya dṛṣṭāntasya ghaṭa ādeḥ sadbhāvāt kevala vyatireki balāt tatra tad siddiḥ tarhi yatra sva prakāśaka tvam na asti tatra artha prakāśaka tvam api na asti yathā ghaṭa ādau iti vyatireka dṛṣṭānta sadbhāvāt artha prakāśaka tva lakṣaṇāt dhetoḥ sva prakāśaka tvam vijñānasya kim iti na siddim āsādayati yat tu uktam kasyacid arthasya kācid sāmagrī tena prakāśaḥ prakāśa antara nirapekṣaḥ eva sva grāhiṇi jñāne pratibhāti tat yuktam eva yathā hi sva sāmagrīta upajāyamānāḥ pradīpa āloka ādayaḥ na samāna jātīyam aloka antaram sva grāhiṇi jñāne pratibhāsamānā apekṣante tatrā sva sām agrītaḥ upajāyamānam vijñānam sva artha prakāśa svabhāvam sva pratipattau na jñāna antaram apekṣate pratiniyata tvāt sva kāraṇa āyatta janmanām bhāva śaktīnām yat tu pradīpa āloka ādikam sajātīya āloka antara nirapekṣām api sva pratipattau jñānam apekṣate tat tasya ajñāna rūpa tvāt jñānasya ca tad viparyaya svabhāva tvāt yukti uktam iti na ekatra sṛṣṭaḥ svabhāvaḥ a nyatra asan jayitum yuktaḥ iti pūrva pakṣa vacaḥ niḥsāra tayā vyavasthitam 
TBV_3.49	 atha ālokasya tad antara nirapekṣā pratipattiḥ upalabdha iti na tad dṛṣṭānta balāt jñānasya api jñāna antara nirapekṣā pratipattiḥ adṛṣṭa tvāt sva ātmani kriyā virodhāt ca nanu evam upalabhyamāne api vastuni yadi adṛṣṭa tvam virodhaḥ ca ucyeta tadā sva ātma vat ghaṭa ādeḥ api bāhyasya na grāhakam jñānam adṛṣṭa tvāt jaḍasya prakāśa yogāt ca iti api vadataḥ saugatasya na vaktra vakra tā samupajāyate tathā hi asau api evam vaktum samarthaḥ jaḍam vastu na svatas prakāśate vijñāna vat jaḍa tva hā niprasaṅgāt na api paratas prakāśamāṇam nīla sukha ādi vyatiriktasya vijñānasya asaṃvedanena asattvāt 
TBV_3.50	 atha nīlasya prakāśaḥ iti prakāśamāṇa nīla ādi vyatiriktaḥ tad prakāśaḥ anyathā bhedena asyām pratipattau saṃvedanasya tad pratibhāsaḥ na syāt nanu na nīla tad vedanayoḥ pṛthak avabhāsaḥ pratyakṣa sambhavī prakāśa viviktasya nīla ādeḥ anubhavāt tad vivekena ca bodhasya apratibhāsanāt na ca adhyakṣataḥ vivekena apratīyamānayoḥ nīla tad saṃvidoḥ bhedaḥ yuktaḥ viveka adarśanasya bheda viparyaya āśraya tvāt nīla tad svarūpa vat atha api kalpanā nīla tad saṃvidoḥ bhedam ullikhati nīlasya anubhavaḥ iti nanu abhedaḥ api bheda ullekhaḥ sṛṣṭaḥ yathā śilāputrakasya vapuḥ nīlasya vā svarūpam iti atha tatra pratyakṣa ārūḍaḥ abhedaḥ bādhakaḥ iti na bheda ullekhaḥ satyaḥ sa tarhi nīla saṃvidoḥ api pratyakṣa ārūḍhaḥ abhedaḥ asti iti na bheda kalpanā satyāḥ tat evam nīla ādikam sukha ādikam ca sva prakāśa vapuḥ pratibhāti iti sthitam tad vyatiriktasya prakāśasya apratibhāsanena abhāvāt 
TBV_3.51	 bhavatu vā vyatiriktaḥ bodhaḥ tathā api na tad grāhyāḥ nīla ādayaḥ yuktāḥ tathā hi tulya kālaḥ vā bodhaḥ teṣām prakāśakaḥ bhinna kālaḥ vā tulya ka alp api parokṣaḥ sva saṃviditaḥ vā na tāvat parokṣaḥ yatas apratyakṣa upalambhasya na artha adṛṣṭiḥ prasidhyati ityādinā sva saṃvidita tvam jñānasya prasādhyante etat pakṣām nirākariṣyāmāḥ na api jñāna antara vedyaḥ anavasthā ādi dūṣaṇasya atra pakṣe pradarśayiṣyamāṇa tvāt sva saṃvedana pakṣe tu yathā antar nilīnaḥ bodhaḥ sva saṃviditaḥ pratibhāti tathā tad kāle sva prakāśa vapuṣaḥ nīla ādayaḥ bahis deśa sambandhi tayā pratibhāti iti samāna kālayoḥ nīla tad saṃvedanayoḥ svatantrayoḥ pratibhāsanāt savya itara go viṣāṇayoḥ iva na vedya vedaka bhāvaḥ samāna kālasya api bodhasya nīlam prati grāhaka tve nīlasya api tam prati grāhaka tā prasaṅgaḥ 
TBV_3.52	 samāna kāla pratibhāsā viśeṣe api buddhiḥ nīla ādīnām grahaṇam uparacayati iti grāhikā nīla ādayaḥ tu grāhyāḥ na etat api yuktam yatas nīla bodha vyatiriktā na grahaṇa kriyā pratibhāti tathā hi bodhaḥ sukha āspadībhūtaḥ hṛdi bahis sphuṭam udbhāsamāna tanuḥ ca nīla ādiḥ ābhāti na tu aparā grahaṇa kriyā pratibhāsa viṣayaḥ tad anavabhāse ca na tayā vyāpyamāna tayā nīla ādeḥ karma tā yuktāḥ bhavatu vā nīla bodha vyatiriktā kriyā tathā api kim tasyāḥ api svatas pratītiḥ yat vā anyatas tatra yadi svatas grahaṇa kriyā pratibhāti tathā sati bodhaḥ nīlam grahaṇa kriyā ca iti trayam svarūpa nimagnam eka kālam pratibhāti iti na kartṛ karma kriyā vyavahṛtiḥ atha anyatas grahaṇa kriyā pratibhāti nanu tatra api apara agrahaṇa kriyā upeyāḥ anyathā tasyāḥ grāhyatā siddheḥ punar tatra api aparā karma tā nibandhanam kriyā upeya iti anavasthā tat na grahaṇa kriyā parā asti tad svarūpa anavabhāsanāt tatas ca antar saṃvedanam bahis nīla ādikam ca sva prakāśam eva iti 
TBV_3.53	 sva saṃvitta mātra vādaḥ sādhīyān yadi tarhi antar nilīnaḥ bodhaḥ nīla ādeḥ na bodhakaḥ kin tu sva prakāśaḥ eva asau tathā sati nīlam aham vedmi iti kama kartṛ bhāva abhiniveśī pratyayaḥ na bhavet viṣayasya karma kartṛ bhāvasya abhāvāt nanu viṣayam antareṇa api pratayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ eva yathā śuktikāyām rajata avagamaḥ atha bādhaka udayāt punar bhrāntiḥ asau nīla ādau tu karmatā ādeḥ na bādhā asti iti satya tā nanu atra api bodha nīla ādeḥ svarūpa saṃsaktasya dvayasya svātantrya upalambhaḥ asti bādhakaḥ karma kartṛ bhāva ullekhasya atha kim asyāḥ bhrānteḥ nibandhanam na hi bhrāntiḥ api virbījā bhavati nanu pūrva bhrāntiḥ eva uttara karma kartṛ bhāva avagateḥ nibandhanam pūrva bhrānti karmatā ādeḥ api aparā pūrva bhrāntiḥ iti anādi bhrānti paramparā karmatā ādiḥ na tattvam 
TBV_3.54	 atha vā nīlam iti pratītiḥ tāvat mātrā adhyavasāyinī pṛthak aham iti api matiḥ antar ullekham udvahantī bhinnāḥ vedmi iti api pratītiḥ aparā eva tatas ca praspara asaṃsakta pratīti tritayam krama vat pratibhāti na karma kartṛ bhāvaḥ tulya kālayoḥ tasya ayogāt bhinna kālayoḥ api anavabhāsanāt na karmatā ādi gatiḥ kathañcid sambhavinī 
TBV_3.55	 atha api darśanāt prāk san api nīla ātmā na bhāti tad udaye ca bhāti iti karma tā tasya na etat api sādhīyaḥ yatas prāgbhāvaḥ arthasya na siddhaḥ darśanena sva kālāa vadheḥ arthasya grahaṇāt darśana kāle hi nīlam ābhāti na tu tatas prāk tat katham pūrva bhāvaḥ arthasya sidhyeta tasya darśanasya pūrva kāle virahāt na ca tad kāle darśanam prāk artha sannidhim vyanakti sarvadā tad pratibhāsa prasaṅgāt atha anyena darśanena prāc arthaḥ pratīyate nanu tad darśanāt api prāk sadbhāvaḥ arthasya anyena avaseyaḥ iti anavasthā tasmāt sarvasya nīla ādeḥ darśana kāle pratibhāsanāt na tat pūrvam sattā sidhyati 
TBV_3.56	 atha api pūrva dṛṣṭam paśyāmi iti vyavasāyāt prāc arthaḥ sidhyati pragartha sattām vinā dṛśyamānasysa pūrva dṛṣṭena eka tva gateḥ ayogāt kena punar ekatvam tayoḥ gamyate kim idānīntana darśanena pūrva darśanena vā na tāvat pūrva darśanena tatra tad kāla avadheḥ eva arthasya pratibhāsanāt na hi tena sva pratibhāsinaḥ arthasya vartamāna kāla darśana vyāptiḥ avasīyate tad kāle sāmpratika darśana ādeḥ abhāvāt na ca asat pratibhāti darśanasya vitatha tva prasaṅgāt na api idānīntana darśanena pūrva darśana ādi vyāpti nīla ādeḥ avasīyate tad darśana kāle pūrva dṛś kālasya astamayāt na ca astamita pūrva darśānādi saṃsparśam avatarati pratyakṣam vitatha tva prasaṅgāt eva tasmāt apāsta tad pūrva dṛś ādi yogam sarvam vastu dṛśā gṛhyate pūrva dṛṣṭa tām tu smṛtiḥ ullikhati tat apāstam dṛṣṭa ullekhā bhāvāt na va saḥ eva ayam iti pratītiḥ ekā saḥ iti smṛti rūpam ayam iti tu dṛśaḥ svārūpam tad parokṣa aparokṣa ākāra tvāt na eka svabhāvau pratyayau tat kutas tattva siddiḥ 
TBV_3.57	 atha anumānāt prāgbhāvaḥ arthasya sidhyati prāk sattām vinā paścāt darśana ayogāt iti tat api asat yatas paścāt t darśanasya prāk sattāyāḥ sambandhaḥ na siddhaḥ prāk sattāyāḥ kathañcid api asiddheḥ na ca asiddhayā sat tayā vyāptam paścāt darśanam sidhyati yena tatas tad siddhiḥ atas yadi pragartham antareṇa darśanam udayam āsādayati tathā sati niyāmaka abhāvāt sarvatra sarvadā sarva ākāram tat bhavet na ayam api doṣaḥ niyata vāsanā prabodhena saṃvedana niyamāt tathā hi svapna avasthāyām vāsanā balāt darśanasya deśa kāla ākāra niyamaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti jāgrat dṛśāyām api tat eva asau yuktaḥ arthasya tu na sattā siddhāḥ na api tad bhedāt saṃvitti niyamaḥ iti tat na tatas saṃvid vaicitryam tasmāt na kathañcid api nīla ādeḥ prāk sattā siddhiḥ 
TBV_3.58	 atha pūrva sattā virahe kim pramāṇam nanu anupalabdhiḥ eva pramāṇam yadi nīlam pūrva kāla sambandhi svarūpam syāt tena eva rūpeṇa upalabhyeta na ca tathā darśana kāla bhavaḥ sarvadā pratibhāsanāt yat ca yena eva rūpeṇa pratibhāti tat tena eva rūpeṇa asti yathā nīlam nīla rūpa tayā avabhāsamānam tathā eva sat na pīta ādi rūpa tayā sarvam ca upalabhyamānam rūpam vartamāna kāla tayā eva pratibhāti na pūrva ādi tayā tat na pūrvam satta arthasya 
TBV_3.59	 atha nīlam tad darśana viratau api para dṛśi pratibhāti iti sādhārana tayā grāhyam vijñānaṇ tu asādhāraṇa tayā prakāśakam na etat api yuktam yatas nīkasya na sādhāraṇa tayā siddhaḥ pratibhāsaḥ pratyakṣeṇa sva pratibhāsitāyāḥ eva avagateḥ na hi nīlam para dṛśi pratibhāti iti atra pramāṇam asti para dṛśaḥ anadhigame nīla ādeḥ tad vedya tān adhigateḥ 
TBV_3.60	 atha anumānena nīla ādīnām sādhāraṇa tā pratīyate yathā eva hi sva santāne nīla darśanāt tad ādāna arthā pravṛttiḥ tathā apara santāne api pravṛtti darśanāt tad viṣayam darśanam anumīyate na etat api asti anumānena sva para darśana bhṛtaḥ nīla ādeḥ ekatā siddheḥ tat dhi sadṛśa vyavahāra darśanāt upajāyamānam sva dṛṣṭa sadṛśa tām para dṛṣṭasya pratipādayet yathā apara dhūma darśanāt pūrva sadṛśam dahanam adhigantum īśaḥ na tu tam eva pūrva sṛṣṭam sāmānyena anvaya paricchedāt tat na anumānataḥ api grāhya ākārasya ekatā 
TBV_3.61	 nanu bhedaḥ api asya na siddhaḥ eva pratibhāsa bhede sati katham asiddhaḥ para pratibhāsa parihāreṇa sva pratibhāsān sva pratibhāsa parihāreṇa ca para pratibhāsān viveka svabhāvān vyatirecayati anyathā tasya ayogāt tatas sva para dṛṣṭasya nīla ādeḥ pratibhāsa bhedāt vyavahāre tulye api bhedaḥ eva itarathāḥ romāñca nikara sadṛśa kārya darśanāt sukha ādeḥ api sva para santāna bhuvaḥ tattvam bhavet 
TBV_3.62–3.63	 atha api santāna bhedāt sukha ādeḥ bhedaḥ nanu santāna bhedaḥ api kim anya bhedāt tathā ced anavasthā atha tasya svarūpa bhedāt bhedaḥ sukha ādeḥ api tarhi saḥ eva astu anyathā bheda asiddheḥ na hi anya bhedāt anyat bhinnam atiprasaṅgāt nīla ādeḥ api sva para pratibhāsinaḥ pratibhāsa bhedaḥ asti iti na ekatā atha deśa eka tvāt ekatvam nanu deśasya api sva para dṛṣṭasya anantara ukta nyāyāt na ekatā yuktāḥ tasmāt grāhaka ākāra vat prati puruṣam udbhāsamānam nīla ādikam api bhinnam eva tat ca eka kāla upalambhāt grāhaka vat sva prakāśam 
TBV_3.64	 atha grāhaka ākāraḥ cit rūpa tvāt vedakaḥ nīla ākāraḥ tu jaḍa tvāt grāhyaḥ atra ucyate kim idam bodhasya cit rūpa tvam yadi aparokṣam svarūpadm nīla ādeḥ api tarhi tat asti iti na jaḍa tā atha nīla ādeḥ aparikṣa svarūpam anyasmāt bhavati iti grāhyam nanu bodhasya api sarva rūpam indriya ādeḥ bhavati iti grāhyam syāt atha yat indriya ādi kāryam na tat vedyam nīla ādikam api tarhi nayana ādi kāryam astu na tu grāhyam 
TBV_3.65	 atha api bodhaḥ bodha svarūpa tayā nityaḥ nīla ādikaḥ tu prakāśya rūpa tayā anityaḥ iti grāhyaḥ tat api asat stambha ādeḥ nayana ādi balāt udeti rūpam aparokṣa tvam tat anityaḥ stambha ādiḥ bhavatu grāhyaḥ tu katham na hi yat yasmāt utpadyate tat tasya vedyam atiprasaṅgāt tasmāt aparokṣa svarūpāḥ stambha ādayaḥ sva prakāśāḥ bodhaḥ tu nityaḥ anityaḥ vā tad kāle kevalam udbhāti na tu vedakaḥ dvayoḥ api parasparam grāhya grāhaka tā āpatteḥ 
TBV_3.66	 atha nīla unmukha tvāt bodhaḥ grāhakaḥ kim idam tat unmukhavtam nāma bodhasya yadi nīla kāle sattā sā nīlasya api tad kāle samasti iti nīlam api bodhasya vedakam syāt atha anyat unmukha tvam tat tarhi svarūpa nimagnam cakāsat tṛtīyam svarūpam bhavet tathā hi tasya tad unmukha tvam tat vyāpāraḥ sa ca vyāpāraḥ yadi nīle vyāpriyate tadā tatra api aparaḥ vyāpāraḥ iti anavasthā atha na vyāpriyate na tad balāt bodhasya grāhaka tvam nīla ādeḥ tu grāhya tvam atha vyāpārasya apara vyāpāra vyarti rekeṇa api nīlam prati vyāpṛti rūpa tā tasya tad rūpa tvāt nanu nīlasya api svam svarūpam vidyate iti bodham prati grahaṇa vyāpṛtiḥ syāt 
TBV_3.67	 kiñ ca bodhena yadi nīlam prati grahaṇa kriyā janyate sā nīlāt bhinnā abhinnāḥ vā bhinnā ced na tayā tasya grāhya tvam bhinna tvāt eva atha abhinnā tarhi nīla ādeḥ jñāna rūpa tā jñāna janya tvāt uttara jñāna kṣaṇa vat atha jñānasya evaṃbhūtā śaktiḥ yena tasya nīlam prati grāhaka tā nīla ādeḥ tu tam prati grāhyatā nanu bodhasya grāhaka tve nīla ādeḥ tu grāhya tve siddhe śakti parikalpanā yuktāḥ śakteḥ kārya anumeya tvāt tad asiddhau tu tad parikalpanam ayuktam itaretara āśraya prasaṅgāt 
TBV_3.68	 tathā hi bodhasya śakti viśeṣa siddheḥ nīlam prati grāhaka tva siddhiḥ tad siddheḥ ca tad śakti siddhiḥ iti vaktam itaretara āśraya tvam tat na bodhasya nīlam prati grāhaka tva siddhiḥ tasmāt vyatirikte api bodhe abhyupagate saha upalambha niyamāt sva saṃvedanam eva yuktam paramārthataḥ tu sukha ādayaḥ nīla ādayaḥ ca aparokṣāḥ iti etāvat eva bhāti nirākāraḥ tu bodhaḥ svapne api na upalabhyate iti na tasya sadbhāvaḥ iti katham tasya artha grāhaka tvām atas eva te pramāṇayanti iha khalu yadi pratibhāti tat eva sat vyavahṛti patham avatarati yathā hṛdi prakāśamāna vapuḥ sukham na tad kāle pīḍā anudbhāsamānā samasti vijñaptiḥ eva ca nīla ādi rūpa tayā sakala tanubhṛtām ābhāti iti svabhāva hetuḥ tat evam artha grāhaka tvasya api asiddheḥ jaḍasya prakāśa viruddha tvāt ca na artha grāhaka tvam api bauddha dṛṣṭyā yuktam 
TBV_3.69	 atha bahis deśa sambaddhasya jaḍasya api nīla ādeḥ anubhavān na nīla ādi prakāśasya tat grāhaka tvam asiddham na api anubhūyamāne stambha ādike jaḍe prakāśa viṣaya tva virodha udbhāvanam yukti saṅgatam pratyakṣa siddha svabhāve vastuni tad viruddha svabhāva āvedakasya anumānasya pratyakṣa bādhita karma nirdeśa anantara prayukta kāla atyaya āpadiṣṭa tva doṣa duṣṭa hetu prabhava tvena anumāna ābhāsa tvāt na ca pratyakṣa asiddhe svabhāve virodhaḥ sidhyati anyathā jñānasya api jñāna tva virodha prāptiḥ nanu evam nīla ādi saṃvedanasya api hṛdi sva saṃvedana viṣaya tayā anubhavān na sva saṃvidita tvam asiddham na api sva ātmani kriyā virodha udbhāvanam yukti yukam anubhūyamāne virodha asiddheḥ asva saṃvedana jñāna sādhaka tvena upanyasya mānasya ca hetoḥ pratyakṣa anirākṛta pakṣa viṣaya tvena na sādhya sādhaka tvam iti api samānam 
TBV_3.70^1	 kim ca sva saṃvidita jñāna anabhyupagame pratīyate ayam arthaḥ bahis deśa sambandhi tayā iti atra pratīteḥ vyavasthāpikāyāḥ apratīta tva avyavasthitau vyavasthā api asya arthasya na vyavasthitiḥ syāt na hi svayam avyavasthitam khara viṣāṇa ādi kasyacid vyavasthāpakam upalabdham atha pratīteḥ asaṃvidita tve api eka artha samaveta ananta pratīti vyavasthāpita tvena na avyavasthita tvam tarhi tad eka artha samaveta anantara pratīteḥ api apara tathā bhūta pratītya vyavasthāpita tve na artha vyavasthāpana pratīti vyavasthāpaka tvam iti punar api tathābhūta aparā pratītiḥ pratīti vyavasthāpikā abhyupagantavyā iti anavasthā 
TBV_3.70^2	 atha pratīti vyavasthāpikā pratītiḥ sva saṃvidita tvena svayam eva vyavasthitā iti na ayam doṣaḥ tarhi artha vyavashāpikā api pratītiḥ tathā kim na abhyupagamyate nyāyasya samāna tvāt atha pratītiḥ apratītā api prati iti antar vyavasthāpikā tarhi prathama pratītiḥ api anavasthitā api artha vyavasthāpikā bhaviṣyasti iti na agṛhīta viśeṣaṇā viśeṣye buddhiḥ iti vacaḥ katham na pariplavet pratītaḥ arthaḥ iti viśeṣya pratipattau pratīti viśeṣaṇa anavagame api viśeṣya pratipatti abhyupagamāt 
TBV_3.71	 api ca yadi tad eka artha samaveta jñāna antara grāhyam jñānam artha grāhakam abhyupagamyate tadā pūrva pūrva jñāna upalambhana svabhāvānām uttarottara jñānānām anavaratam utpatteḥ viśaya antara sañcāraḥ jñānānām na syāt viṣaya antara sannidhāne api pūrva jñāna lakṣaṇasya tad eka artha samavetasya antaraṅga tvena ati sannihitatarasya viṣayasya sadbhāvāt yaḥ tu āha viṣaya upalambha nimitta mātra pratipattau pratīti viśeṣaṇasya arthasya siddha tvāt na anavasthā tat etat eva na saṅgacchate sva saṃvedana jñāna anabhyupagamāt etat ca pratipāditam 
TBV_3.72	 api ca pramāṇa samplava vādinā naiyāyikena pratyakṣa śābda jñānayoḥ eka viṣaya tvam abhyupagatam tathā ca adhyakṣa jñāna vat śābde api tasya eva anyūnā an atiriktasya viṣasyasya adhigame na pratipatti bhedaḥ iti adhyakṣa vat śābdam api spaṣṭa pratibhāsam syāt atha eka viṣaya tve sati api indriya sambandha abhāvāt śabda viṣaye pratipatti bhedaḥ nanu akṣaiḥ api viṣaya svarūpam udbhāsanīyam tat ca yadi śābdena api pradarśyate tathā sati indriya sambandha abhāve api kim iti na spaṣṭa avabhāsaḥ śābdasya na hi viṣaya bhedam antareṇa jñānānabhāsa bhedaḥ yuktaḥ anyathā jñāna avabhāsa bhedāt viṣaya bheda vyavasthā na syāt na hi bahis api tad avabhāsa bheda saṃvedana vyatirekeṇa anyat bheda vyavasthā nibandhanam utpaśyāmaḥ anyat ca pratyakṣe api sākṣāt indriya sambandhaḥ asti iti na sva rūpeṇa jñātum śakyaḥ tasya atīndriya tvāt kin tu svarūpa pratibhāsāt kāryāt tat ca avikalam yadi śābde api vastu svarūpam pratibhāti tadā tatas eva indriya sambandhaḥ tatra api kim na abhyupagamyate 
TBV_3.73–3.74	 atha tatra spaṣṭa pratibhāsā bhāvan na asau anumīyate nanu tad abhāvaḥ tad akṣa saṅgati virahāt tad abhāvaḥ ca sphuṭa pratibhāsā bhāvāt iti saḥ ayam itaretara āśraya doṣaḥ tasmāt viṣaya bheda nibandhanaḥ eva jñāna pratibhāsa bheda avasāyaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ sa ca eka viṣaya tve śābda adhyakṣa jñānayoḥ na saṅgacchate atha śābde vastu rūpa avabhāse api na sakala tad gata viśeṣa avabhāsaḥ iti aspaṣṭa pratibhāsam tat nanu evam pratyakṣa avabhāsinaḥ viśeṣasya artha kriyākṣam asya tatra apratibhāsanāt tat eva bhinna viṣaya tvam śābda adhyakṣayoh jñāna ātma bhūtau nanu evam akṣa sambaddhe viṣaye pratibhāsamāne tad kālaḥ spaṣṭṛ tva avabhāsaḥ jñāna avabhāsaḥ iti prāptam viśiṣṭa sāmagrī janyasya jñānasya viśada tvāt tad avabhāsa vyatirekeṇa tu akṣa sambaddha nīla pratibhāsa kāle anyasya bhavat abhyupagamena vaiśadya pratibhāsa nimittasya asambhavāt 
TBV_3.75^1	 atha ca bhavatu viśada jñāna pratibhāsa nimittaḥ eva tatra vaiśasya pratibhāsa vyavahāraḥ tathā api na sva saṃvidita tad jñāna siddhiḥ tad eka artha samaveta jñāna antara vedya tve api tad vyavahārasya sambhavāt eka kāla avabhāsa vyavahāraḥ tu laghu vṛtti tvāt manasaḥ krama anupalakṣaṇa nimittaḥ utpala patra śata vyatibheda vat nanu evam sati aṅguli pañcakasya eka jñāna avabhāsaḥ api krama avabhāse sati api tatas eva krama pratibhāsā anupalakṣaṇa kṛtaḥ iti sat asat dharmaḥ sarvaḥ kasyacid eka jñāna pratyakṣaḥ prameya tvāt pañcāṅguli vat iti sarvajña sādhaka prayoge dṛṣṭāntasya sādhya vikalatā prasaktiḥ tathā samasta sat asat dharma grāhakeṇa sarva vijñānena jñāna ātmā gṛhyate uta na iti 
TBV_3.75^2	 yadi na gṛhyate tadā tasya prameya tve sati tena eva prameya tva lakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ vyabhicārī aprameya tve tasya bhāga asiddhaḥ hetuḥ atha sarvajña jñānena sarva padārtha grāhiṇāḥ ātmā api gṛhyate iti na anaikāntikaḥ nanu evam sati yathā īśvara jñānam jñāna tve api ātmānam svayam gṛhṇāti na ca tatra sva ātmani kriyā virodhaḥ tathā asat ādi jñānam api evam bhaviṣyati iti na kaścid virodhaḥ kim ca evam abhyupagame jñān mam jñāna antara grāhyam prameya tvāt ghaṭa vat iti atra prayoge īśvara jñānasya prameya tve sati api jāna antara grāhya tva abhāvāt tena eva anaikāntikaḥ prameya tvāt iti hetuḥ tasmāt jñānasya jñāna antara gṛāhya tve aneka doṣa sambhavāt sva saṃviditam jñānam abhyupagantavyam 
TBV_3.76	 jñāna svarūpaḥ ca ātmā anyathā bhinna jñāna sadbhāvāt ākāśasya iva tasya jñātṛ tvam na syāt na ca ākāśa vyatirekeṇa jñānam ātmani eva samavetam iti tasya eva jñātṛ tvam na ākāśa ādeḥ iti vaktum yuktam samavāyasya niṣetsyamāna tvāt jñānasya ca sva saṃvidita tve siddhe ātmanaḥ api tad avyatiriktasya tat siddham iti katham na sva saṃvedana pratyakṣā siddha tvam ātmanaḥ tat na prathama pakṣasya duṣṭa tvam 
TBV_3.77^1	 dvitīya pakṣe api yat uktam na hi kaścid padārthaḥ kartṛ rūpaḥ karaṇa rūpaḥ vā sva ātmani karmaṇi iva sa vyāpāraḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti tat api asaṅgatam bhinna vyāpāra vyatirekeṇa api ātmanaḥ kartuḥ pramāṇasya ca jñānasya sva saṃvidita tva pratipādanāt ekasya eva ca liṅga ādi karaṇam apekṣya avasthā bhedena yathā pramātṛ tvam prameya tvam ca bhavadbhiḥ aviruddha tvena abhyupagamyate tathā ekadā api ekasya ātmanaḥ aneka dharma sadbhāvāt pramātṛ pramāṇa tva prameya tvāni aviruddhāni kim na abhyupagamyante tad tad dharma yogāt tad tad svabhāva tvasya pramāna niścita tvena avirodhāt yat ca uktam pramāṇa aviṣaya tve api apara ukṣata iti asya bhāṣitasya kaḥ arthaḥ ityādi tat api asāram jñātṛ tayā pramāṇa tvena ca svarūpa avabhāsanasya pratipādita tvāt 
TBV_3.77^2–3.78	 na ca ghādeḥ svarūpasya bhinna jñāna grāhya tvāt pramātuḥ pramāṇasya ca svarūpam abhinna jñāna grāhyam tayoḥ cit rūpa tvena ghaṭa ādeḥ tu tad viparyayeṇa svarūpasysa siddha tvāt na ca pramāṇa pramāṭṛ svarūpa grāhakasya pratyakṣasya tad lakṣaṇena asaṅgrahaḥ tad saṅgrāhakasya lakṣaṇasya pradarśita tvāt yat api ghaṭam aham cakṣuṣā paśyāmi iti anena atiprasaṅga āpādanam kṛtam tat api asaṅgatam na hi cakṣuṣaḥ jaḍa rūpasya asva saṃvidita tve pramātṛ pramityoḥ api cit rūpayoḥ asva saṃvidita tvam yuktam anya svabhāva tva anupapatteḥ yat tu uktam indriya vyāpāre sati śarīrāt vyavacchinnasya viṣayasya eva kevalasya avabhāsanam iti tat atyantam asaṅgatam viṣayasya iva tad avabhāsa saṃvedanasya api vyavasthāpita tvāt tad abhāve viṣaya avabhāsaḥ eva na syāt iti asya ca atas pramātṛ avabhāsaḥ upapannaḥ eva 
TBV_3.79	 na ca kṛśaḥ aham sthūlaḥ aham iti śarīra sāmāna adhikaraṇyena asya pratyayasya upapatteḥ tad ālambanatā cakṣuḥ ādi karaṇa vyāpāra abhāve śarīrasya agrahaṇe api aham iti pratyayasya sukha ādi samāna adhikaraṇa tvena parisphuṭa pratibhāsa viṣaya tvena utpatti darśanāt na śarīra ālambana tvam asya vyavasthāpayitum yuktam na ca kṛśaḥ aham iti prayayasya bhrānta tve jñānavān aham iti jñāna sāmānādhikaraṇyena upajāyamānasya api pratyayasya bhrānta tvam yuktam anyathā agniḥ māṇavakaḥ iti māṇavake agni pratyayasya upacarita viṣayasya bhrānta tve agnau api tad pratyayasya upacarita tvena bhrānta tvam syāt atas tatra pāṭava piṅgala tva ādi lakṣaṇasya upacāra nimittasya sadbhāvāt bhavati tatra upacaritaḥ pratyayaḥ na ca atra upacāra nibandhanam kiñcid asti tat api asaṅgatam saṃsārya ātmanaḥ śarīra ādi vyatirikte api atyanta upakārake sva bhṛtya ādau= upacaritaḥ tad nimittaḥ yaḥ ayam bhṛtyaḥ saḥ aham iti pratyayaḥ 
TBV_3.80	 na ca sukha ādi sāma anadhi karaṇyena upajāyamānasya eva ahaṃpratyayasya upacarita viṣaya tā iti vaktum śakyam agnau agni pratyaya vat abādhita tvena askhalat rūpa tvena ca asya atra mukhya tvāt gaura tva ādeḥ tu pudgala dharma tvena bāhya indriya grāhya tayā antar mukha ākārān indriya ahaṃ pratyaya viṣaya tva asambhavāt na ca gaura tva ādi rūpa āśraya bhūtasya pratikṣaṇa viśarāru tvena abhyupagama viṣayasya śarīrasya yaḥ eva aham prāk mitram dṛṣṭavān saḥ eva aham varṣa pañcaka ādi vya vadhānena spṛśāmi iti sthira ālambana tvena anubhūyamān pratyaya viṣaya tvam yuktam anyathā rūpa viṣaya tvena anubhūyamānasya tasya rasa ādi ālambana tvam syāt na ca sukha ādi vivarttā ātmaka ātma ālambana tve kiñcid bādhakam utpaśyāmaḥ yena tad viṣaya tvena asya bhrānta tvam syāt na api tatra tasya skhalat rūpa tā yena vāhīke go pratyayasya iva upacarita tva kalpanā yuktimatī syāt tasmāt abādhita askhalat rūpa ahaṃ pratyaya grāhya tvāt ātmanaḥ na asiddhiḥ śeṣaḥ tu pūrva pakṣa granthaḥ niḥsāra tayā na pratisamādhānam arhati iti upekṣitaḥ 
TBV_3.81	 na ca atra bauddha mata anusāriṇā etat vaktum yujyate ahaṃpratyayasya sa vikalpaka tvena apratyakṣa tvena na tat grāhya tvam ātmanaḥ iti sa vikalpakasya eva pratyakṣasya pramāṇa tvena vyavasthāpayiṣyamāṇa tvāt pratyakṣa viṣaya tve api vipratipatti sambhave anumānasya avatāraḥ na ca siddhe ātmanaḥ eka tve tad pratibaddhaḥ anusandhāna pratyayaḥ sidhyati tad siddhau ca tatas tasya ekatvam iti itaretara āśraya doṣa avatāraḥ yaḥ eva aham ghaṭam adrākṣam saḥ eva idānīm tam spṛśāmi iti pratyayāt pratyabhijñā pratakṣa svarūpāt ātmanaḥ ekatva siddheḥ 
TBV_3.82^1	 na ca atra etat preryam draṣṭṭa rūpam ātmanaḥ spraṣṭṭa rūpa anupraveśena pratibhāsate āhosvit ananupraveśena yadi anupraveśena tadā draṣṭṭa rūpasya spraṣṭṭā rūpe anupraveśāt spraṣṭṭa rūpa tā eva iti na draṣṭṭa rūpa tā tathā ca aham draṣṭā spṛśāmi iti kutas ekam pratyabhijñānam yatas tat ekatva siddhiḥ atha ananupraveśena tadā darśana sparśana avabhāsayoḥ bhedāt kutas ekam pratyabhijñānam na hi pratibhāsa bhede sati api eka tvam anyathā ghaṭa paṭa pratibhāsayoḥ api tat syāt atha pratibhāsasya eva atra bhedaḥ na punar tad viṣayasya ātmanaḥ kutas punar tasya abhedaḥ na tāvat pratibhāsā bhedāt tasya bhinna tve vyavasthāpita tvāt 
TBV_3.82^2	 na api svatas svatas adya api vivāda viṣaya tvāt atha darśana sparśana avasthā bhede api cit rūpasya tad avasthātuḥ abhinna tvāt na ayam doṣaḥ tat api asaṅgatam yatas darśana avasthā pratibhāsena tad sambaddham eva avasthātṛ rūpam gṛhītam na sparśana jñāna sambandhi tatra tad avasthāyāḥ anutpanna tvena apratibhāsanāt tad apratibhāsane ca tad vyāpti tvena avasthātuḥ api apratibhāsanāt na api sparśana pratibhāsena darśana avasthā vyāptiḥ avasthātuḥ avagamyate sparśana jñāne darśanasya vinaṣṭa tvena apratibhāsavāt pratibhā āsane ca anādi avasthā paramparā pratibhāsa prasaṅgaḥ na ca prāk avasthā pratibhā āsane tad avasthā vyāptiḥ avasthātuḥ avagantum śakyāḥ yat ca yena rūpeṇa pratibhāti tat tena eva sat iti abhyupagantavyam yathā nīlam nīla rūpa tayā pratibhāsamānam tena eca rūpeṇa abhyupagamyate darśana sparśana jñānābhyām ca sva sambandhi tvam eva avasthātuḥ gṛhyate iti tad rūpaḥ eva asau abhyupagantavyaḥ iti kutas avasthātṛ siddhiḥ 
TBV_3.83–3.84	 yatas nīla pratibhāse api evam vaktum śakyam kim eka nīla jñāna paramāṇu avabhāsaḥ apara tad nīla jñāna paramaṇu avabhāsa anupraveśena pratibhāti uta ananu praveśena yadi anupraveśena tadā eka tad nīla jñāna paramāṇu avabhāsānām anupraveśāt nīla jñāna saṃvedanasya eka paramāṇu rūpa tvam tasya ca ananubhavāt kutas nīla jñāna saṃvedana siddhiḥ atha ananupraveśena tadā nīla jñāna paramāṇu avabhāsānām ayaḥ śalākā kalpānām pratibhāsanāt kutas sthūlam eka nīla jñāna saṃvedanam pratinīla jñāna paramāṇu avabhāsam bhinna tvāt atha sva saṃvedana avabhāsa bhede sati api na tad pratibhāsasya nīla jñānasya bhedaḥ nanu kutas nīla jñānasya abhedaḥ kim tad sva saṃvedanā bhedāt svatas vā yadi sva saṃvedanā bhedāt tat ayuktam tad bhedasya vyavasthāpita tvāt atha svatas eva tad abhedaḥ tat api ayuktam tasya adya api asiddha tvāt 
TBV_3.85	 tathā yadi darśana avasthāyām sparśana avasthā na pratibhāti iti tad avasthā vyāptiḥ darśana jñānena avasthātuḥ na grahītum śakyāḥ nanu evam tad apratibhāsane tena tad avyāptiḥ api katham graḥitum śakyāḥ tad apratibhāsane tatas idam avasthātṛ rūpam vyāvṛttam iti etat api prahītum aśakyam eva na ca tad vivikta pratibhāsāt eva tad avyāptiḥ gṛhītā eva iti vaktum yuktam tad apratibhāsane tad viviktasya eva agrahaṇāt na ca tat avyāptiḥ tasya sva rūpam eva iti darśana jñānena tad svarūpa grāhiṇā tad abhinna svarūpā tad avyāptiḥ api gṛhītā eva iti yuktam tad vyāptau api asya sarvasya samāna tvāt na ca ābādhita eka pratyaya viṣayasya ātmanaḥ ekatvam asiddham na ca asya ekatva adhyavasāyasya kiñcid bādhakam asti tad bādhaka tvena sambhāvyamānasya pramāṇasya yathāsthānam niṣetsyamāna tvāt 
TBV_3.86	 bhavatu vā anusandhāna pratyaya lakṣaṇāt dhetoḥ tad eka tva siddhiḥ tathā api netatra itara āśraya doṣaḥ yatas na eka tva pratibaddham anusandhānam anvayi dṛṣṭānta dvāreṇa niścīyate yena ayam doṣaḥ syāt api tu aneka tve anusandhānasya asambhavāt tatas vyāvṛttam anusandhānam tat eka tvena vyāpyate iti eka santāne smaraṇa ādi anusandhāna darśanāt anumānataḥ api tad siddhiḥ na ca bhede darśana smaraṇa ādi jñānānām anusandhānam sambhavati anyathā devadatta anubhūte arthe yajñadattasya smaraṇa ādi anusandhānam syāt 
TBV_3.87	 atha devadatta yajñadattayoḥ eka santāna abhāvam na anusandhānam yatra tu ekaḥ santānaḥ tatra pūrva apara jñānayoḥ atyanta bhede api bhavati eva anusandhānam nanu santānasya yadi santānibhyaḥ bhedaḥ eka tvam ca tadā śabda antareṇa saḥ eva ātma abhihitaḥ yat pratibaddham anusandhānam atha santānibhyaḥ abhinnaḥ santānaḥ tadā pūrva uttara jñā na kṣaṇānām santāni śabda vācyānām deva datta yajña datta jñāna vat atyanta bhedāt tad abhinnasya santānasya api bhedaḥ iti kutas anusandhāna nimitta tvam atha eka santati patitānām pūrva uttara jñāna santāninām kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt bhede api eka santāna tvam tad nibandhanaḥ ca anusandhāna pratyayaḥ yuktaḥ na punar devadatta yajña datta jñānayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva atas tad nibandhana santāna abhāva nimittaḥ tatra anusandhāna abhāvaḥ nanu devadatta jñānam yajñadattena yadā vyāpāra vyāhāra ādi liṅga balāt anumīyate tadā tat yajñadatta anumāna janakam bhavati iti kārya kāraṇa bhāva nimitta eka santāna nibandhana anusandhāna prasaktiḥ syāt 
TBV_3.88^1	 atha svasantatau upādāna upādeya bhāvena jñānānām janya janaka bhāvaḥ bhinna santatau tu saha kāri bhāvena tad bhāvaḥ iti na ayam doṣaḥ nanu kim punar idam upādāna tvam yat abhāvāt bhinna santāne anusandhāna abhāvaḥ yat sva santati nivṛttau kāryam janayati tat upādānakāraṇam yathā mṛd piṇḍaḥ svayam nivartamānaḥ ghaṭam utpādayati iti sa ghaṭa utpattau upādānakāraṇam atha vā aparam anekasmāt utpadyamāne kārye sva gata viśeṣa ādhāyakam tat na tu evam nimitta kāraṇam 
TBV_3.88^2	 nanu pratikṣaṇa viśara aruṣu eka svabhāva paurvāparya avasthita jñānasya bhāveṣu kṣaṇeṣu upādāna upādeya bhāvaḥ eva na vyavasthāpayitum śakyaḥ tathā hi uttara jñānam janayat pūrva jña āmam kim naṣṭam janayati uta anaṣṭam ubhaya rūpam anubhaya rūpam vā na tāvat naṣṭam cirataraa naṣṭasya iva anantara naṣṭasya api avidyamāna tvena utpādaka tva virodhāt na api anaṣṭam kṣaṇa bhaṅga bhaṅga prasaṅgāt na api ubhaya rūpam eka svabhāvasya vuruddha ubhaya rūpā sambhavāt na api anubhaya rūpam anyonya vyavaccheda rūpāṇām eka niṣedhasya tad apara vidhānana antarīyaka tvena anubhaya rūpa tāyāḥ ayogāt 
TBV_3.89	 atha yadi vyāpāra yogāt kāraṇam kārya utpādakam abhyupagamyeta tadā syāt ayam doṣaḥ yat uta naṣṭasya vyāpāra asambhavāt katham kārya utpādaka tvam yadā tu prāgbhāva mātram eva kāraṇasya kārya utpādaka tvam tadā kutas etad doṣa avasaraḥ nanu etasmin abhyupagame prāgbhāvinaḥ anekasmāt upajāyamāne kārye kutas ayam vibhāgaḥ 
TBV_3.90	 idam atra upādāna kāraṇam idam ca sahakāri kāraṇam iti dvayoḥ api kāreṇa anuvihita anvaya vyatireka tvāt atha sati api anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāne ekasya upādāna tvena janakatvam aparasya anyathā iti nanu etat eva upādāna bhāvena janakatvam kasyacid rūpasya ananugame prāc bhāvi tva mātreṇa duravaseyam atha abhihitam eva upādāna kāraṇa tvasya lakṣaṇam tad avagamāt katham tat duravaseyam satyam uktam na tu kasyacid rūpasya ananugame tat sambhavati na api avasāntum śakyam 
TBV_3.91	 tathā hi yat sva gata viśeṣa ādhāyaka tvam upādāna tvam uktam tat kim sva gata kati paya viśeṣa ādhāyaka tvam āhosvit sakala viśeṣa ādhāyaka tvam iti tatra yadi prathamaḥ pakṣaḥ sa na yuktaḥ sarvajña jñāne sva ākāra arpakasya asmad ādi vijñānasya tam pratyupādāna bhāva prasaṅgāt tathā rūpasya api rūpa jñānam pratyupādāna bhāva prasaktiḥ tasya api sva gata kati paya viśeṣa ādhāyaka tvāt anyathā nirākārasya bodhasya sarvān prati aviśeṣāt rūpasya eva ayam grāhakaḥ na rasa ādeḥ iti tatas pratikarma vyavasthā na syāt rūpa upādāna tve ca jñānasya para lokāya dattaḥ jala añjaliḥ syāt kiñ ca katipaya viśeṣa ādhāyaka tvena upādāna tve ekasya eva jñāna kṣaṇasya tad kārya anugata vyāvṛtta an eka dharma sambandhi tva abhyupagame viruddha dharma adhyāsaḥ abhyupahataḥ bhavati tathā ca yathā yugapad bhāvi aneka viruddha dharma adhyāse api ekam vijñānam tathā krama bhāvi aneka tad dharma yoge kim iti ekam na abhyupagamyeta 
TBV_3.92–3.93	 atha sakala viśeṣa ādhāyaka tvena na tarhi nirvikalpakāt sa vikalpaka utpattiḥ na ca nirvikalpakayoḥ api upādāna upādeya tvena abhyupagatayoḥ tad bhāvaḥ syāt tathā ca kutas rūpa ākārāt samanantara pratyayāt kadācid rasa ādi ākārasya api upādeya tvena abhimatasya utpattiḥ atha vijñāna santāna bahutva abhyupagamāt na ayam doṣaḥ tena sarvasya sva sadṛśasya utpattiḥ tarhi asmin darśane ekasmin api santāne pramātṛ nānātva prasaṅgaḥ tathā ca gavāśva darśanayoḥ bhinna santāna varttinoḥ ekena dṛṣṭe arthe aparasya anusandhānam na syāt deva datta yajña datta santāna gatayoḥ iva anyena anubhūte anyasya dṛśyate ca 
TBV_3.94–3.95	 gām aham jñātavān pūrvam aśvam jānāmi aham punar kiñ ca sakala svagata viśeṣa ādhāyaka tve sarva ātmanā upādeya jñā na kṣaṇe tasya upayogāt anupayuktasya apara svabhāvasya abhāvāt yogi vijñānam rūpa ādikam ca eka sāmagrī antargatam prati na sahakāri tvam tasya iti sahakāri kāraṇa abhāve na upādeya kṣaṇa vyatirikta kārya antara utpādaḥ
