TBV_3.96^1	 atha yeṣām kāraṇam eva kārya tayā pariṇamati teṣām bhavatu ayam diṣaḥ na tu asmākam prāgbhāva mātram kāraṇa tvam abhyupagacchatām nanu atra api mate yena sva rūpeṇa vijñānam upādeyam vijñāna antaram janayati kim tena eva rūpam eka sāmagrī antargatam uta svabhāva antareṇa tatra yadi tena eva tadā rūpam api jñānam upādeya bhūtam syāt tad svabhāva janya tvāt tad uttara jñāna kṣaṇa vat atha svabhāva antareṇa tadā upādāna abhimatam jñānam dvi svabhāvam āsajyateḥ yathā ca upādāna sahakāri svabhāva rūpa dvaya yogaḥ tathā trailokya antargatānyajanya kārya antara apekṣayā tasya ājanaka tvam api svabhāvaḥ tatas ca eka tvam jñāna kṣaṇasya yathā upādāna sahakārya janakatva aneka viruddha dharma adhyāsitasya abhyupagamyate tathā harṣa viṣāda ādi aneka vivartta ātmanaḥ tad santānasya api abhyupagantavyam 
TBV_3.96^2–3.97	 atha upādāna saha kārya janaka tva ādayaḥ dharmāḥ tatra kalpanā śilpa kalpitāḥ eka tvam tu tasya sva saṃvedana adhyakṣa siddham iti na taiḥ tat apanīyate iti matiḥ tarhi ātmanaḥ api eka tvam santāna śabda abhidheya tayā prasiddhasya sva saṃvedana adhyakṣa siddhasya kramavat dharṣa viṣāda ādi kārya darśana anumīyamāna tad apekṣa janaka tvā janakatva dharma apaneyam na syāt tat na sva gata sakala dharma ādhāyaka tvam upādāna tvam bhavat abhyupagamena saṅgatam na api santān anuvṛttyā kārya utpādaka tva svabhāvam tathā abhyupagame jñāna santānanuvṛtteḥ para loka abhāva prasaṅgaḥ atha samanantara pratyaya tvam upādāna tvam ucyate tathā hi samaḥ tulyaḥ anantaraḥ avyavahitaḥ pratyayoḥ janakaḥ 
TBV_3.98^1	 na ca etat bhinna santānāt iti na tatra anusandhāna sambhavaḥ nanu atra api sama tvam kāryeṇa yadi upādāna tvam pratyayasya tadā vaktavyam kim sarvathā samatvam uta eka deśena yadi sarvathā tat asat kārya kāraṇayoḥ sarvathā tulya tve yathā kāraṇasya prāk bhāvi tvam tathā kāryasya api syāt tathā ca kārya kāraṇayoḥ eka kāla tvāt na kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ na hi eka kālayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ savya itara go viṣāṇa vat tathā kāraṇa abhimatasya api sva kāraṇa kāla tā tasya api sva kāraṇa kālatā iti sakala santāna śūnyam idānīm samastam jagat syāt atas kathañcid samāna tā tathā sati yogi jñānasya api asmad ādi jñāna ālambanasya tad ākāra tvena eka santāna tvam syāt ityādi dūṣaṇam pūrva uktam eva 
TBV_3.98^2	 atha anantara tvam upādāna tvam nanu kṣaṇikā ekānta pakṣe sarva jagat kṣaṇa anantaram vivakṣi ta kṣaṇe jagat jāyate iti sarveṣām upādāna tvam iti eka santāna tvam jagataḥ deśa ānantaryam tatra anupayogi deśa vyavahitasya api iha janma maraṇa cittasya bhāvi janma citta upādāna tva abhyupagamāt pratyaya tvam tu na upādāna tvam sahakāri tve api pratyaya tvasya bhāvāt tat na samanantara pratyaya tvam api upādāna tvam na ca pratikṣaṇa viśarārūṣu bhāveṣu kathañcid eka anvayam antareṇa janaka tvam api saṅgacchate kim uta upādāna ādi vibhāgaḥ iti kṣaṇa bhaṅga bhaṅga pratipādana avasare abhidhāsyāmaḥ 
TBV_3.99	 atra kecid tulye api janaka tve sva para santāna gatayoḥ vijñānayoḥ upādāna tve kāraṇam āhuḥ sva santatau cetitam jñānam jñāna antara janakam na tu evam para santatau atas janakatva vyatiriktasya upādāna kāraṇa tve nimittasya sambhavāt itthaṃbhūtāt dhetu phala bhāvāt vyavasthā asya api vyavasthā nimitta tvam ayuktam na hi jñānam asaṃveditam vyavasthām labhate saṃvedanam hi jñānānāṇ svatas eva iṣyate tat ca sva santati patite iva para santati patite api tulyam jñāna antara vedya tvam tu na śākyaiḥ abhyupagamyate jñānasya niyamate iti na ayam api ati prasaṅga parihātaḥ na ca svasantatau api svasa sṃvedita jñāna pūrvaka tā jñānasya siddhāḥ mūrcchā ādi avastha uttara kāla bhāvi jñānasya tathā tva anavagamāt yatas vijñāna pūrvaka tve api tatra vipratipannāḥ vādinaḥ kutas punar samvidita jñāna pūrvaka tvam tatra etat syāt vijñāna pūrvaka tvasya anumānena niścayāt katham vipratipattiḥ tat ca darśitam tad jātīyāt tad jātīya utpattiḥ iti etat asat atajjātīyāt api bhāvānām utpatti darśanāt yathā dhūma ādeḥ 
TBV_3.100	 ye api atra āhuḥ sadṛśa tādṛśa bhedena bhāvānām vijātīya utpatti asambhavāt etat dūṣaṇam teṣām api sadṛśa tādṛśa vivekaḥ na arvāk dṛś pra mātṛ gocaraḥ kārya nirūpaṇāyām api tayoḥ vivekaḥ durlabhaḥ tasmāt ayam aparihāraḥ yaiḥ punar ucyate sarvasya samāna jātīyāt upādānāt utpattiḥ ādyasya api dhūma kṣāṇasya upādāna tvena vyavasthāpitāḥ kāṣṭha antargatāḥ aṇavaḥ tatra api sajātīya tvam na vidmaḥ rūpa ādīnām hi rūpa ādi pūrvaka tvena vā sajātīya tvam dhūma tva upalakṣita avayava pūrvaka tvena vā prācye vikalpe na idānīm vijātīyāt utpattiḥ goḥ api aśvāt upajāyamānasya uttara vikalpe api kāṣṭha antargatānām avayavānām dhuma tvam laukikam pāribhāṣikam vā paribhāṣāyāḥ tāvat ayam aviṣayaḥ loke api tad ākāra vyavasthitānām avayavānām na eva dhūma tva vyavahāraḥ tārkikeṇa api loka prasiddha vyavahāra anusaraṇam yuktam kartum tasmāt na sajātīyāt utpattiḥ 
TBV_3.101	 yat ca atra ucyate tasyām avasthāyām vijñāna abhāve tad avasthātaḥ pracyutasya uttarakālam īdṛśī saṃvittiḥ na bhavet na mayā kiñcid api cetitam smṛtiḥ hi iyam anubhava pūrvikā atas yena anubhavena satā na kiñcid cetyate tasyām avasthāyām tasya avaśyam sadbhāvaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ etat su vyāhṛtam na kiñcid cetitam mayā iti bruvatā vastu avedanam vocyeta svarūpa āvedanam vā vastu avedane sakala pratiṣedhaḥ na yuktaḥ svarūpa āvedanam tu sva saṃvedana abhyupagame dūra utsāritam tasmāt idānīm eva manaḥ vyāpārāt tad avasthā bhāvī sarvān avagamaḥ saṃvedyate 
TBV_3.102	 astu vā tasyām avasthāyām vijñānam tathā api janakatvā atirikta vyāpāra viśeṣa abhāvaḥ samanantara pratyaya tve janakatvā atirikte abhyupagamyamāne tayoḥ tāttvika bheda prasaṅgaḥ tathā ca yat eva ekasyām jñāna santatau samanantara pratyaya tvam tat eva para santatau avalambana tvena janaka tvam iti etat na syāt atha janakatva samanantara tva ādayaḥ dharmāḥ kālpanikāḥ akalpitam tu yat sva rūpam tat tāttvikam tat ca bodha rūpam kim idānīm sāṃvṛtāt rūpāt bhāvānām utpattiḥ na iti ucyate katham vā kālpanika tvam atha janakatvā atiriktasya samanantara pratyayanasya evam ucyate katham tat nibandhanā vyavasthā 
TBV_3.103	 tathā hi ekasyām santatau para santati gatena vijñānena tulye api janaka tve samanantara pratyaya tvena janana viśeṣam aṅgīkṛtya eka santāna vyavasthā kriyate yadā tu vyavasthā nibandhanasya api sāṃvṛta tvam tatas tad kṛtāyāḥ vyavasthāyāḥ parama artha sattvam durbhaṇam iti ayam api saugatānām doṣaḥ na jā enānām yatas jñāna pūrvaka tvam jñānasya sva saṃveda janam ca jñānasya svarūpam iti etat prāk pratisādhitam 
TBV_3.104–3.106	 yat ca uktam atatjjātīyāt api bhāvānām utpatti darśanāt yathā dhūma ādeḥ iti api na saṅgatam yatas na asmābhiḥ atajjātīya utpattiḥ na abhyupagamyate vilakṣaṇāt api pāvakāt dhūma utpatti darśanāt kin tu kāraṇa gata dharma anuvidhānam kāryatva abhyupagama nibandham tat ca jñānasya pradarśitam prāk na ca kāya vijñānayoḥ iva anala dhūmayoḥ sarvathā vailakṣaṇyam pudgala vikāra tvena dvayoḥ api sādṛśyāt sarvathā sādṛśye ca kārya kāraṇa bhāva abhāva prasaṅgaḥ ekatva prāpteḥ yat tu sadṛśa tādṛśa vivekaḥ kārya nirūpaṇāyām api durlabhaḥ tatra yaḥ kārya darśanāt api vivekam na avadhārayitum kṣamaḥ tasya anumāna vyavahāre anadhikāraḥ eva tat uktam su vivecitam kāryam kāraṇam na vyabhicarati atas tad avadhāraṇe yatnaḥ vidheyaḥ atas eva rūpa ādīnām hi rūpa ādi pūrvaka tvena vā ityādi anabhimata upālambha mātram kathañcid sādṛśyasya kārya kāraṇayoḥ darśita tvāt tasya ca prakṛte pramāṇa siddha tvāt 
TBV_3.107^1	 yat ca supta mūrcchatā ādi avasthāsu vijñāna abhāvena tad pūrvaka tvam uttara jñānasya na sambhavati iti abhyadhāyi tat asat tad avasthāyām vijñāna abhāva grāhaka pramāṇa asambhavāt tathā hi na tāvat suptaḥ eva tad avasthāyām vijāna abhāvam vetti tadā vijñāna anabhyupagamāt tad avagame ca tasya eva jñāna tvāt na tad avasthāyām tad abhāvaḥ na api pārśvastitaḥ anyaḥ tad abhāvam vetti kāraṇa vyāpaka svabhāva anupalabdhānām viruddha vidheḥ vā atra viṣaye avyāpārāt anyasya tad abhāva avabhasatva ayogāt na ca abhāva vat tad bhāvasya api tasyām avasthāyām apratipattiḥ sva ātmani sva saṃvidita vijñāna avinābhūta tvena niścitasya prāṇa apāna śarīra uṣṇa tā ākāra viśeṣa ādeḥ tad avasthāyām upalabhyamāna liṅgasya sadbhāvena anumāna prati iti utpatteḥ 
TBV_3.107^2	 jāgrat avasthāyām api para santa nipatita cetaḥ vṛtteḥ asmad ādibhiḥ yathā ukta liṅga darśana udbhūta anumānam antareṇa apratipatteḥ na kiñcid cetitam mayā iti smaraṇāt uttara kāla bhāvinaḥ tad avasthāyām anubhava anum māne kim vastu asaṃvedanam svarūpā saṃvedanam vā ityādi yat dūṣaṇam abhihitam tat api asāram jāgrat avasthā bhāvi sva saṃvidita gacchat tṛṇa sparśa jñāna aśva vikalpa samaya go darśana ādiṣu uttara kāla bhāvi na mayā kiñcid pralakṣitam iti smaraṇa liṅga bala udbhūta anumāna viṣayeṣu api asya samāna tvāt na ca sva saṃvedita vijñāna vādinaḥ atra api samānaḥ doṣaḥ iti vaktum yuktam yasya yāvatī mātrā iti sva saṃvedita jñānasya abhyupagamāt 
TBV_3.108	 yat ca samanantara sahakāri tva ādi aneka dharma yukta tvam eka kṣaṇe jñānasya asajyate iti pratipāditam tad abhyupagamyamāna tvena adūṣaṇam atas paurvāparya vyavasthita harṣa viṣāda ādi aneka paryāya vyāpi eka ātma vyatirekeṇa jñānayoḥ sva santāne api anusandhāna nimitta upādāna upādeya bhāvā sambhavāt na para santāna vat anusandhāna pratyayaḥ syāt dṛśyate ca atas anekatva vyāvṛttāt anusandhāna pratyayāt api liṅgāt ātma siddhiḥ 
TBV_3.109	 atha api syāt gamaka tvam hi hetoḥ sva sādhya avinābhāva grahaṇa pūrvakam tad grahaṇam ca dharmi antare na ca atra eka kartṛka tvena sādhya dharmi vyatirikte dharmi antare pratisandhānasya vyāptiḥ yena pratisandhānāt ekaḥ kartā anumīyate atha brūṣe kṣaṇika tā sādhakasya sattā ākhyasya hetoḥ yathā dharmi antare vyāpti agrahaṇe api gamaka tā tadvat asya api etat acāru tasya hi kṣaṇikatāyām prāk pratyakṣeṇa niścayāt niścaya viṣayeṇa ca vyāpteḥ darśanāt vipakṣāt pracyāvitasya bādhaka pramāṇena sādhya dharmiṇi yat avasthānam tat eva sva sādhyena vyāpti grahaṇam atas eva asya hetoḥ sādhya dharmiṇī eva vyāpti niścayam icchanti nanu vyāpti sādhya niścayayoḥ niyamena paurvāparyam abhyupagantavyam vyāpti niścayasya sādhya pratipatti aṅga tvāt atra tu sāghya dharmiṇi vyāpti niścaya abhyupagame sādhya pratipatti kālaḥ anyaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ na ca asau anyaḥ anubhūya tve asti etat kārya hetoḥ api 
TBV_3.110	 asya tu bādhakāt pramāṇāt vipakṣāt pracyutasya yat eva sādhya dharmiṇi sva sādhya vyāpta tayā grahaṇam tat eva sādhya grahaṇam na ca asya evam dvairūpyam yatas vipakṣāt vyāvṛttiḥ eva anvayam ākṣipati iyān tu viśeṣaḥ kasyacid hetoḥ vyāpti viṣaya pradarśanāya dharmi viśeṣaḥ pradarśayate asya tu yat sat tat kṣaṇikam iti dharmi viśeṣa apradarśane api dharmi mātrā kṣepeṇa vyāpti pradarśanam tat ca sattvam kvacid vyavasthitam upalabhyamānam kṣaṇika tā pratipatti aṅgam atas pakṣa dharma tā api atra asti na ca atra evam 
TBV_3.111	 atra api enam eva nyāyam kecid āhuḥ katham tatra hi vyāpakasya krama yaugapadyasya nivṛttyā vipakṣāt tad nivṛttiḥ atra api pramātṛ niyata tāyāḥ vyāpikāyāḥ abhāvāt vipakṣāt pratisandhāna lakṣaṇasya hetoḥ nivṛttiḥ atha tatra bādhaka pramāṇasya vyāptiḥ pratyakṣeṇa niścīyate krama yaugapadyābhyām artha kriyā karaṇasya pratyakṣeṇa niścayāt atra tu katham atra api pramātṛ niyama pūrvaka tvena sva santānaḥ eva pratisandhānasya vyāt piniścayāt katham na tulya tā 
TBV_3.112^1	 atha brūyāt pramātṛ niyata tā iti asya bhāṣitasya kaḥ arthaḥ yadi param bhaṅgi antareṇa eka kartṛka tvam sādhyam vyapadiśyate tasya pratyakṣeṇa niścaya abhyupagame katham bādhaka pramāṇa avaseya tā vyāpteḥ na etat pramātṛ niyata tāgra ḥaṇam na eka kartṛka tva grahaṇam sarve eva hi bhāvāḥ deśa ādi niyata tayā avasīyamānāḥ vyavahāra gocara tām upayānti pramātuḥ api avasāyaḥ evam eva dṛśyate idānīm atra aham evam deśa ādi asaṃsarga vat pramātṛ antara asaṃsargaḥ api niścīyate tathā hi deśa kāla nibandhna niyama vat vyatirikta padārtha asaṃsarga svabhāva niyata pratibhāsaḥ api ghaṭa ādeḥ iva atra ekatva aneka tva niścaya abhāvaḥ pūrva pākṣika mate tasya nānā kartṛkeṣu santāna antareṣu vyāpakasya abhāvāt vipakṣāt pracyutasya pratisandhānasya kvacid upalabhyamāṇasya eka kartṛka tvena vyāptiḥ 
TBV_3.112^2	 yathā krama yaugapadyābhyām artha kriyā karaṇa darśane na evam niścayaḥ kim kṣaṇikaiḥ krama yaugapadyābhyām sā kriyate āhosvit anyathā iti atha ca pratyakṣena bādhakasya vyāpti avasāye paścāt vyāpaka anupalabdhyā mūla hetoḥ vyāpti siddhiḥ evam eka kartṛka tva anavasāye api pramātṛ niyata tayā pratisandhānasya sva santatau vyāpti niścaye sati uttara kālam vipakṣe vyāpakasya pramātṛ niyata tvasya abhāvāt eka kartṛka tvena pratisandhānasya vyāpti siddhiḥ evam anabhyupagame aham anyaḥ vā iti pramātra niścaye prameyā niścayāt andhamūkam jagat syāt aupacārikasya pramātṛ niyata tayā pratibhāsa viṣaya tve anātma pratyakṣa tvam doṣaḥ 
TBV_3.113^1	 tatra etat syāt asti ayam pramātṛ niyama niścayaḥ sa tu sva santatau kim eka kartṛka tva kṛtaḥ utsvit nimitta antara kṛtaḥ yuktaḥ tat ca ekasyām santatau hetu phala bhāva lakṣaṇam prāk pradarśitam satyam pradarśitam na tu sādhitam tathā hi tad kṛtaḥ pramātṛ niyamaḥ na anya kṛtaḥ iti na etāvat pratyakṣasya viṣayaḥ na ca pramāna antarasya api tat dhi asmin viṣaye ucyamānam anumānam ucyeta tat api pratyakṣa niṣedhāt niṣiddham na ca kṣaṇika tva vyavasthāpane hetu phala bhāva kṛtaḥ niyamaḥ iti abhyupagantum yuktam tasya upariṣṭāt niṣetsyamāna tvāt 
TBV_3.113^2	 na ca atas eva doṣāt eka kartṛka tva kṛtaḥ api na niyamaḥ iti vaktum śakyam sva saṃvedana pratyakṣa siddha tvasya tad pūrvaka anumāna siddha tvasya ca ātmani prāk vyavasthāpita tvāt abhyupagama vādena tu kṣaṇika tva vyavasthāpaka sattva hetu tulya tvam anusandhāna pratyaya hetoḥ pradārśitam na tu kṣaṇika tva vat ātmā eka tvasya pratyakṣa asiddha tvam yena anumānāt tad prasiddhi abhyupagame itaretara āśraya doṣa prasaṅgaḥ preryete atas adhyakṣa anumāna pramāṇa siddha tvāt para lokinaḥ para lokinaḥ abhāvāt para loka abhāvaḥ iti sūtram niḥsāra tayā vyavasthitam 
TBV_3.114	 yat api ucyate śarīra antargatam saṃvedanam katham śarīra antara sañcāri jīvataḥ tāvan aśarīra antara sañcāraḥ dṛṣṭaḥ parasmin maraṇa samaye bhaviṣyati iti duranvayam etat tat api na yuktam yatas kumāra śarīra antargatāḥ pāṇḍityādi vikalpāḥ vṛddha avasthā śarīra sañcāriṇaḥ dṛśyante jīvate eva capalatā ādi śarīra avasthā viśeṣāḥ vāc vikārāḥ ca tat katham na jīvataḥ śarīra antara sañcāraḥ atha ekam eva idam śarīram bāla kumāra ādi bheda bhinnam janma antara śarīram tu mātā pitṛ antar śukra śoṇita prabhavam śarīra antara prabhavam etat api ayuktam bālakumāra śarīrasya api bhedāt yathā ca bāla kumāra śarīra capa latā bhedaḥ tarūṇā ādi śarīra sañcārī upalabhyate tathā nija janma antara śarīra prabhavaḥ capalatā ādi bhedaḥ para bhava bhāvi janma śarīra sañcārī bhaviṣyati iti tatas na mātā pitṛ śuka śoṇita anvayi janma ādi śarīram api tu sva santāna śarīra anvayam eva vṛddha ādi śarīra vat 
TBV_3.115^1	 anyathā mātā pitṛ śarīra capa latā ādi vilakṣaṇa śarīra ceṣṭā vat na syāt atha iha janma bāla kumāra ādi avasthā bhede api pratyabhijñānāt ekatvam siddham śarīrasya tad avasthā vyāpakasya tena na tad dṛṣṭānta balāt atyanta bhinne janma antara śarīra ādau jñāna sañcāraḥ yuktaḥ tat asat pūrva uttara janma śarīra jñāna sañcāra kāriṇaḥ kārmaṇa śarīrasya atas eva kathañcid ekatva siddheḥ tathā hi jñānam tāvat iha janma ādau anya nija janma jñāna prabhavam prasādhitam tasya ca iha janma bāla kumāra ādi avasthā bhedeṣu tat eva idam śarīram iti abādhita pratyabhijñā pratyaya avagata eka rūpa anvayiṣu sañcāra darśanāt pūrva uttara janma avasthāsu api tathābhūta anugāmi rūpa samanvitāsu tasya sañcāraḥ anumīyate 
TBV_3.115^2	 na ca asmad ādi indriya saṃvedya rūpa ādi āśrayasya audārika śarīrasya janma antara śarīra ādi avasthā anugamaḥ sambhavati tasya tadā eva ca dāha ādinā dhvaṃsa upalabdheḥ atas janma dvaya avasthā vyāpakasya ūṣma ādi dharma anugatasya kārmaṇa śarīrasya vijñāna sañcāra kāriṇaḥ sadbhāvaḥ siddhaḥ pūrva uttara janma avasthā vyāpakasya avasthātuḥ tad avasthābhyaḥ kathañcid bhedāt mātā pitṛ śarīra vilakṣaṇa nija śarīra avasthā capa latā ādi anuvidhāne uttara avasthāyāḥ katham na avasthātṛ dharma anuvidhānam 
TBV_3.116–3.117	 tasmāt yasya eva saṃskāram niyamena anuvartate śarīram pūrva dehasya tat tad anvayi yuktimat atha pūrva aparayoḥ pratyakṣa asya apravṛttena kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ anumāna siddhau itaretara āśraya dośaḥ iti tat api prativihitam evam hi sarva śūnya tvam āyātam iti kasya dūṣaṇam sādhanam vā kena pramāṇena ihalokasya api abhāva prasakteḥ iti pratipādita tvāt 
TBV_3.118^1	 atha kārya viśeṣasya viśiṣṭa kāraṇa pūrvakatva siddhau yathā ukta prakāreṇa bhavatu pūrva janma siddhiḥ bhāvi para loka siddhiḥ tu katham bhāvini pramāṇa abhāvāt tatra api kārya viśeṣāt eva iti brūmaḥ tathā hi kārya viśeṣaḥ viṣiṣṭam sattvam eva tat ca na sattā sambhanda lakṣaṇam tasya niṣetsyamāna tvāt na api artha kriyā kāritva lakṣaṇam santati vyavacchede tasya abhāva prasaṅgāt tathā hi śabda buddhi pradīpa ādi santānānām yadi ucchedaḥ abhyupagamyate tadā tad santati cara m akṣaṇasya aparakṣaṇa ājananāt asattvam tat asattve ca pūrva pūrvakṣaṇānām artha kriyā jananāt asattvam iti sakala santatyabhāvaḥ atha santati antakṣaṇaḥ sajātī yakṣaṇa antara ajanane api sarvajña santāne sva grāhi jñāna janaka tvena san iti na ayam doṣaḥ tat asat sva santati patita upādeya kṣaṇā janaka tve para santāna vartti svagrāhi jñāna janaka tvasya api asambhavāt 
TBV_3.118^2	 na hi upādānakāraṇa tva abhāve sahakāri kāraṇa tvam kvacid api upalabdham tad sadbhāve vai eka sāmagrī adhīnasya rūpa ādeḥ asataḥ tad samāna kāla bhāvinaḥ avyabhicāriṇī pratipattiḥ na syāt rūpakṣaṇasya sva upādeya kṣaṇa antara ajanane api rasa santatau sahakāri kāraṇa tvena rasa kṣaṇa janaka tva abhyupagamāt tad sadbhāve api tad samāna kāla bhāvinaḥ rūpa ādeḥ abhāvāt tat na upādāna kāraṇa tva abhāve sahakāri tvasya api sambhavaḥ iti sva santati uccheda abhyupagame artha kriyā lakṣaṇasya sattvasya asambhavaḥ iti utpāda vyaya dhrauvya lakṣaṇam eva sattvam abhyupagantavyam iti kārya viśeṣa lakṣaṇāt dhetoḥ yathā ukta prakāreṇa atīta kāla vat anāgata kāla sambandhi tvam api ātmanaḥ siddham 
TBV_3.119	 yat api uktam yadi āgama siddha tvam ātmanaḥ tasya vā pratiniyata karma phala sambandhaḥ tad siddhaḥ abhyupagamyate tadā anumāna vaiyarthyam iti tat api mūrkha īśvara ceṣṭitam na hi vyartham iti nija kāraṇa sāmagrī bala āyātam vastu pratikṣeptum yuktam na hi āgama siddhāḥ padārthāḥ iti pratyakṣasya api pratikṣepaḥ yuktaḥ yat api pratyakṣa anumāna anuṣaye ca arthe āgama prāmāṇya vādibhiḥ tasya prāmāṇyam abhyupagamyate tat uktam 
TBV_3.120–3.121	 āmnāyasya kriyā artha tvāt ānarthakyam atad arthānām iti tat api ayuktam yatas yathā pratyakṣa pratīte api arthe vipratipatti viṣaye anumānam api pravṛttim āsādayati iti pratipāditam tathā pratyakṣa anumāna pratipanne api ātma lakṣaṇe arthe tasya vā pratiniyata karma phala sambandha lakṣaṇe kim iti āgamasya pravṛttiḥ na abhyupagamasya viṣayaḥ 
TBV_3.122–3.127	 na ca āgamasya tatra aprāmāṇyam iti vaktum yuktam sarvajña praṇīta tvena tad prāmāṇyasya vyavasthāpita tvāt pratiniyata karma phala sambandha pratipādakaḥ ca āgamaḥ bahu ārambha parigraha tvam ca nārakasya ityādinā vācaka mukhyena sūtrīkṛtaḥ asya eva anumāna viṣaya tvam pratipādayitu kāmena yathā ca karma phala sambandhaḥ api ātmanaḥ anumānāt avasīyate tathā yathāsthānam iha eva pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ ātma svarūpa pratipādakaḥ pratiniyata karma phala sambandha pratipādakaḥ ca āgamaḥ ege āyā puvvim ducciṇṇāṇam duppaḍi kaṃtāṇam kaḍāṇam kammānam iti ādikaḥ supta siddhaḥ eva tat evam pratyakṣa anumāna āgama pramāṇa prasiddha tvāt nāraka tiryak nara amara paryāya anubhūta svabhāvasya ātmanaḥ na bhava śabda vyutpattiḥ artha abhāvāt ḍittha ādi śabda vyutpatti tulyāḥ iti sthitam 
TBV_4.1–4.2	 atra āhuḥ nayāyikāḥ kleśa karma vipāka āśaya aparāmṛṣṭa puruṣa abhyupagame nityam sattvam asattvam vā iti dūṣaṇam abhyadhāyi tatra tat nitya sattva pratipādane na asmākam kācid kṣatiḥ pramāṇataḥ nitya jñāna ādi dharma kalāpa anvitasya tasya abhyupagamāt nanu yuktam etat yadi tathābhūta puruṣa sadbhāva pratipādakam kiñcid pramāṇam syāt tat ca na asti tathā hi pratyakṣam tathāvidha puruṣa sadbhāva avedakam asmad ādīnām asmad vilakṣaṇa yogibhiḥ tasya avasāyaḥ iti atra api na kiñcid pramāṇam asti yadā na tad svarūpa grahaṇe pratyakṣa pramāṇa pravṛttiḥ tadā tad gata dharmāṇām nitya jñāna ādīnām sadbhāva vārttā eva na sambhavati 
TBV_4.3–4.5	 na anumānam api yuktam etad svarūpā vedakam pratyakṣa niṣedhe tad pūrvakasya tasya api niṣedhāt sāmānyatodṛṣṭasya api na atra viṣaye pravṛttiḥ liṅgasya kasyacid tad pratipādakasya abhāvāt kāryatvasya pṛthi pṛthivī ādi saṃsthānasya atyanta vailakṣaṇyāt saṃsthāna śabda vācya tvena ca ati prasakti darśitāḥ vastu bheda prasiddhasya śabhda sāmyāt abhedinaḥ ityādinā tasmāt na anumānam tad sādhanāya alam 
TBV_4.6	 napi āgamaḥ nityasya atra darśane anabhyupagamāt abhyupagame vā kārya artha pratipādakasya siddhe vastuni avyāpṛteḥ na api īśvara pūrvakasya prāmāṇyam itaretara āśraya doṣa prasaṅgāt anīśvara pūrvakasya api sambhāvyamāna doṣa tvena pramāṇa tā anupapatteḥ tasya anyeśvara pūrvaka tve tasya api siddhiḥ kutas iti vaktavyam tad asiddhau na tasya prāmāṇyam aneka īśvara prasaṅga doṣaḥ ca bhavatu kaḥ doṣaḥ yatas ekasya api sādhane vayam atīva utsukāḥ kim punar bahūnām iti ced na kaścid pramāṇa abhāvam muktvā tat na āgamataḥ api tad pratipattiḥ evam svarūpa asiddhau katham tasya kāraṇa tā 
TBV_4.7	 atra āhuḥ yat uktam na tatra pratyakṣam pramāṇam tat evam eva yat api sarva prakārasya āgamasya na tad svarūpa āvedane vyāpṛtiḥ tatra ucyate āgamāvyāpāre api tad svarūpa sādhakam anumānam vidyate āgamasya api siddhe arthe liṅga darśana nyāyena yathā vyāpṛtiḥ tathā pratipādayiṣyāṃaḥ pratyakṣa pūrvaka anumāna niṣedhe siddha sādhanam sāmānyatodṛṣṭa anumānasya tatra vyāpāra abhyupagamāt nanu anumāna pramāṇa tāyām ayam vicāraḥ yukta ārambhaḥ tasya eva tu prāmāṇyam na anumanyante cārvākāḥ iti etat ca anuddhoṣyam anumāna pramāṇyasya vyavasthāpita tvāt 
TBV_4.8–4.9	 yat tu uktam pṛthivī ādi gatasya kāryatvasya apratipatteḥ na tasmāt īśvara avagamaḥ tatra pṛṭhivyādīnām bauddhaiḥ kāryatvam abhyupagatam te katham evam vadeyuḥ ye api cārvāka ādyāḥ pṛthivī ādīnām kārya tvam na icchanti teṣām api viśiṣṭa saṃsthāna yuktānām katham akārya tā sarvam saṃsthāna vat kāryam tat ca puruṣa pūrvakam dṛṣṭam ye api āhuḥ saṃsthāna śabda vācya tvam kevalam ghaṭa ādibhiḥ samānam pṛthivī ādīnām na tatvataḥ arthaḥ kaścid dvayoḥ anugataḥ samānaḥ vidyate teṣām api na kevalam atra anugata artha abhāvaḥ kintu dhūma ādau api pūrva apara vyakti gataḥ na eva kaścid anugataḥ arthaḥ samānaḥ asti 
TBV_4.10^1	 atha tatra vastu darśanāyāt akalpanā nimittam uktam atra tathābhūtasya pratibhāsasya abhāvāt na anugata artha kalpanā tathā hi kasyacid ghaṭa ādeḥ kriyamāṇasya viśiṣṭām racanām kartṛ pūrvikām dṛṣṭvā adṛṣṭa kartṛkasya api ghaṭa prāsāda ādeḥ tasya racanā viśeṣasya kartṛ pūrvakatva pratipattiḥ pṛthivī ādeḥ tu saṃsthānam kadācid api kartṛ pūrvakam na avagatam na api tādṛśam dharmi antare dṛṣṭa kartṛkaḥ iva paṭa ādau tat pṛthivī ādi gatasya saṃsthānasya vailakṣaṇaāt tatas na tatas kartṛ pūrvakatva pratipattiḥ evam hetoḥ asiddatvena na etat sādhanam ayuktam etat yatas yati anavagata sambandhān pratipattṝn adhikṛtya hetoḥ asiddha tvan ucyate tadā dhūma ādiṣu api tulyam 
TBV_4.10^2	 atha gṛhīta avinā bhāvānām api kāryatva darśanāt tat vā ādiṣu īśvara ādi kṛta tva pratibhāsā anutpatteḥ evam ucyate tat asat ye hi kārya tva ādeḥ buddhimat kāraṇa pūrvaka tvena gṛhīta avinābhāvāḥ te tasmāt īśvara ādi pūrvaka tvam teṣām avagacchanti eva tasmāt vyutpannānām asti eva pṛthivī ādi saṃsthānavattva kārya tva ādeḥ hetoḥ dharmi dharma tā avagamaḥ avyutpannānām tu prasiddha anumāne dhūma ādau api na asti 
TBV_4.11^1	 api ca bhavatu prāsāda ādi saṃsthānebhyaḥ pṛthivī ādi saṃsthānasya vailakṣaṇyam tathā api karya tvam śākya ādibhiḥ pṛthivī ādīṇām iśyate kāryam ca kartṛ karaṇa ādi pūrvakam dṛṣṭam atas kāryatvāt buddhimat kāraṇa pūrvakatva anumānam atha kartṛ pūrvakasya kāryatvasysa saṃsthānavat tvasya ca tad vailakṣaṇyāt na tatas sādhya avagamaḥ atas eva adhiṣṭhātṛ bhāva abhāva anuvṛttimat yat saṃsthānam tad darśanāt kartṛ adarśinaḥ api tad pratipattiḥ yuktā iti asya dūṣaṇasya kāryatve api samāna tvāt katham gamaka tā 
TBV_4.11^2	 yadi evam anumkāna uccheda prasaṅgaḥ dhūma ādikam api yathāvidham agni ādi sāmagrī bhāva abhāva anuvṛttimat tathāvidham eva yadi parvata upari bhavet syāt tatas vahni ādi avagamaḥ atha adhūma vyāṛttam tathāvidham eva dhūma ādi tarhi kārya tva ādi api tathāvidham pṛthivī ādi gatam kim na iṣyate atha pṛthivī ādi gata kārya tva ādi darśanāt kartṛ adarśinām tad apratipattiḥ evam śikharī ādi gata vahni ādi adarśinām dhūma dibhyaḥ api tad apratipattiḥ astu na ca atra śabda sāmāṇyam vastu anugamaḥ na asti iti vaktum yuktam dhūma ādau api śabda sāmānyasya vaktum śakya tvāt tat na śākya dṛṣṭyā kārya tva ādeḥ asiddha tā 
TBV_4.12–4.13	 na api cārvāka mīmāṃsaka dṛṣṭyā teṣām api saṃsthāna vat avaśyam kāryam ghaṭa ādi vat pṛthivī ādi sva avayava saṃyogaiḥ ārabdham avaśyaṃtayā viśleṣāt vināśam anubhaviṣyati evam vināśāt vā sambhāvitāt kāryatva anumānam racanā svabhāva tvāt vā yathā uktam bhāṣya kṛtāḥ yeṣām api anavagata utpattīnām bhāvānām rūpam upalabhyate teṣām tantu vyatiṣaṅga janitam rūpam dṛṣṭvā tad vyatiṣaṅga vimocanāt tad vināśāt vā vinaṅkṣyati iti anumīyate 
TBV_4.14–4.16	 anena saṃsthānavataḥ anupalabhyamāna utpatteḥ samavāya saṃvāyi kāraṇa vināśāt vināśam āha tathā pṛthivī ādeḥ saṃsthānavataḥ adṛṣṭa janmanaḥ rūpa darśanāt nāśa sambhāvanā bhaviṣyati sambhāvitāt ca nāśāt kāryatva anumitau kartṛ pratipattiḥ yathā uktam nyāya vidbhiḥ tattva darśanam pratyakṣataḥ anumānataḥ vā kāryatva vināśi tvayoḥ ca samavyāptika tvāt ekena aparasya anumānam iṣṭam tena yatra api ubhau dharmau iti atra atas jaiminīyānām na kārya tva ādeḥ asiddha tā 
TBV_4.17	 na api cārvāka mate asiddha tvam teṣam racanāvat tvena avaśyambhāvinī kārya tā pratipattiḥ adṛṣta utpattīnām api kṣiti ādīnām anyathā veda racanāyāḥ api kartṛ darśana abhāvāt na kārya tā yatas tatra api etāvat śakyam vaktum na racanā tvena veda racanāyāḥ kāryatva anumānam kartṛ bhāva ābhābā anuvidhāyinī tad darśanāt laukikī eva racanā tad pūrvikā aḥ tu mā bhūt vaidikī atha tayoḥ viśeṣa anupalambhāt laukikī iva vaidikī api kartṛ pūvikā tarhi prāsāda ādi saṃsthāna vat pṛthivī ādi saṃsthāna vat tvasya api tad rūpa tāḥ tu viśeṣa anupalakṣanāt tat na hetoḥ asiddha tā 
TBV_4.18^1	 mā bhūt asiddhatvam tathā api asmāt sādhya siddhiḥ na yuktāḥ na hi kevalāt pakṣa dharma tvāt vyāpti śūnyāt sādhya avagamaḥ nanu kim ghaṭa ādau kartṛ karma karaṇa pūrvaka tvena kāryatva ādeḥ vyāpti anavagamaḥ asti evam ghaṭa gate kāryatve pratipattiḥ tathā api navya āptiḥ sā hi sakalākṣepeṇa gṛhyate atra tu vyāpti grahaṇa kāle eva keṣāñcid kāryāṇām akartṛ pūrvakānām kāryatva darśanāt na sarvam kāryam kartṛ pūrvakam yathā vaneṣu vanaspatīnām atha tatra na kartṛ abhāva niścayaḥ kim tu kartṛ a grahaṇam tat ca vidyamāne api kartari bhavati iti katham sādhya abhāve hetoḥ darśanam 
TBV_4.18^2	 kva punar vidyamāna kartṛkāṇām tad apratipattiḥ yathā ghaṭa ādīnām anavagata utpattīnām yuktā tatra kartuḥ apratipattiḥ utpāda kālān avagamāt tad kāle ca tasya tatra sannidhānam anyadā asya sannidhāna abhāvāt agrahaṇam vana gateṣu ca sthāvareṣu upalabhyamāna janmasu kartṛ sadbhāve tad avagamaḥ avaśyaṃabhāvī yathā upalabhyamāna janmani ghaṭa ādau atas upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasysa kartuḥ teṣu abhāva niścayāt tatra vyāpti grahaṇa kāle eva kārya tva ādeḥ hetoḥ darśanāt na kartṛ pūrvaka tvena vyāptiḥ 
TBV_4.19	 itas ca dṛṣṭa anyadṛṣṭa parikalpanā sambhavāt dṛṣṭāntām kṣiti ādīnām kāraṇa tva tyāgaḥ adṛṣṭasya ca kartuḥ kāraṇa tva kalpanā na yuktimatī atha na kṣiti ādeḥ kāraṇa tva nirākaraṇam kartṛ kalpanāyām api tad sadbhāve api tasya apara kāraṇa tva kpteḥ tat asat yatas yat yasya anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyi tat tasysa kāraṇam itarat kāryam kṣiti ādīnām tu anvaya vyatirekau anuvidhatte tatra ākṛṣṭa jātam vanaspati ādi na aparasya katham atas vyatiriktam karaṇam bhavet evam api kāraṇa tva kalpanāyām doṣaḥ uktaḥ caitrasya vraṇa rohaṇe ityādinā tasmāt pakṣa dharma tve api vyāpti abhāvāt agamaka tvam hetoḥ 
TBV_4.20	 atha teṣam pakṣe antarbhāvāt na taiḥ vyabhicāraḥ tat asat tāttvikam vipakṣa tvam katham icchā kalpitena pakṣa tvena apodyeta vyāptau siddhāyām sādhya tad abhāvayoḥ agrahaṇi vādi icchā parikalpitam pakṣa tvam kathyate grahaṇa kāle vyabhicāra āśaṅkāyām niścaye nā vyabhicāra viṣayasya pakṣe antarbhāvena gamaka tva kalpane na kaścid dhetuḥ vyabhicārī bhavet tasmāt na īśvara siddhau kaścid hetuḥ avyabhicāri asti 
TBV_4.21^1	 atra āhuḥ na ākṛṣṭa jātaiḥ sthāvara ādibhiḥ vyabhicāraḥ vyāpti abhāvaḥ vā sādhya abhāve vartamānaḥ hetuḥ vyabhicārī ucyate teṣam tu kartṛ a grahaṇam na sa kartṛka tva abhāva niścayaḥ nanu uktam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta tve kartuḥ abhāva niścasya tatra yuktaḥ na etat yuktam upalabdhi lakṣana prāpta tāyāḥ kartuḥ teṣu anabhyupagamāt yat tu uktam kṣiti ādi anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāna darśanāt teṣām tat vyatiriktasya kāraṇa tva kalpane ati prasaṅga doṣaḥ iti etasyām kalpanāyām dharma adharmayoḥ api na kāraṇa tā bhavet na ca tayoḥ akāraṇa tā eva tayoḥ kāraṇa tva prasādhanāt na hi kiñcid jagati asti yat kasyacid na sukha sādhanam duḥkha sādhanam vā na ca tad sādhanasya adṛṣṭa nirapekṣasya utpattiḥ iyān tu viśeṣaḥ śarīra ādeḥ pratiniyata adṛṣṭa ākṣipta tvam prāyeṇa sarva upabhogyānām tu sādhāraṇa adṛṣṭa ākṣipta tvam etat sarva ādibhiḥ abhyupagamāt apratyākhyeyam yuktiḥ ca pradarśitā eva cārvākaiḥ api etat abhyupagantavyam tān prati pūrvam etad siddhau pramāṇasya ukta tvāt 
TBV_4.21^2	 pramāṇa siddam tu na kasyacid na siddham atha adṛṣṭasya kāryeṇa anvaya vyatirekān anuvidhāne api na akāraṇa tā na tarhi vaktavayam bhūmi ādi vyatirekeṇa sthāvara ādinā kāryeṇa īśvarasya anvaya vyatirekān anuvidhānāt akāraṇa tvam atha jagat vaicitryam adṛṣṭasya kāraṇa tvam vinā na upapadyate iti tat kalpyate sarvān utpattimataḥ prati bhūmi ādeḥ sādhāraṇa tvāt atas adṛṣṭa ākhya vicitra kāraṇa kṛtam kārya vaicitryam evam adṛṣṭasya kāraṇa tva kalpanāyām īśvasrasya api kāraṇa tva pratikṣepaḥ na yuktaḥ yathā kāraṇa gatam vaicitryam vinā kārya gatam vaicitryam na upapadyate iti tat parikalpyate tathā cetanam kartāram vinā kārya svarūpa anupapattiḥ iti kim iti tasya nābhyupagamaḥ na ca ākṛṣṭa jāteṣu sthāvara ādiṣu tasya agrahaṇena pratikṣepaḥ anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta tvāt adṛṣṭa vat na ca sarvā kāraṇa sāmagrī upalabdhi lakṣana prāptā atas eva dṛśyamāneṣu api kāraṇeṣu kāraṇa tvam apratyakṣam kāryeṇa eva tasya upalambhāt 
TBV_4.22	 sahakāri sattā dṛśyamānasya kāranatā keṣāñcid sahakāriṇām dṛśya tve api adṛṣṭa ādeḥ sahakāriṇaḥ kāryeṇa eva pratipattiḥ evam īśvarasya kāraṇa tve api na tad svarūpa grahaṇam pratyakṣeṇa iti sthitam tatas anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta tvāt kartuḥ upalabhyamāna janmasu sthāvareṣu dhetoḥ vṛtti darśanāt na vyāpti abhāvah yatas niścita vipakṣa vṛttiḥ hetuḥ vyabhicārī 
TBV_4.23	 nanu niścita vipakṣa vṛttiḥ yathā vyabhicārī tathā sandigdha vyatirekaḥ api ukteṣu sthāvareṣu kartṛ a grahaṇam kim kartṛ abhāvāt āhosvit vidyamāna tve api tasya agrahaṇam anupalabdhi lakṣana prāpta tvena evam sandigdha vyatireka tve na kaścid dhetuḥ gamakaḥ dhuma ādeḥ api sakala vyakti ākṣepeṇa vyāpti upalambha kāle na sarvāḥ vahni vyaktayaḥ dṛśyāḥ tāsu ca adṛśyāsu dhūma vyaktīnām dṛśya tve sandigdha vyatireka āśaṅkā na nivartate yatra vahneḥ adarśane dhūma darśanam tatra kim vahneḥ adarśanam abhāvāt āhosvit anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta tvāt iti na niścayaḥ atas dhūmaḥ api sandigdha vyatireka tvāt na gamakaḥ 
TBV_4.24	 atha dhūmaḥ kāryam hutabhujaḥ tasya tad abhāve svarūpa anupapatteḥ adṛṣṭa tve api analasya sadbhāva kalpanā nanu tat kāryam atra upalabhyamānam kim iti kāraṇam antareṇa kalpyate atha dṛṣṭa śakteḥ kāraṇasya kalpanā aḥ tu mā bhūt buddhimataḥ vahni ādeḥ dhūma ādīn prati katham dṛṣṭa śakta tā pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām iti ced buddhimataḥ api tābhyām kāraṇa tva kptau vahni ādibhiḥ tulya tā yathā vahni ādi sāmagryā dhūma ādiḥ janyamānaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ sa tām antareṇa kadācid api na bhavati sva rūpa hāni prasaṅgāt tadvat sarvam utpattimat kartṛ karma karaṇa pūrvakam dṛṣṭam tasya sakṛt api tathā adarśanāt tad janya tā svabhāvaḥ tasya evam svabhāva niścitau anyatama abhāve api katham bhavaḥ 
TBV_4.25	 kim ca anupalabhyamāna kartṛkeṣu sthāvareṣu kartuḥ anupalambhaḥ śarīra ādi a bhāvāt na tu asattvāt yatra śarīrasya kartṛ tā tatra kulāla ādeḥ pratyakṣeṇa eva upalambhaḥ atra tu caitanya mātreṇa upādāna ādi adhiṣṭhānāt katham pratyakṣa vyāpṛtiḥ na api etat vaktavyam śarīra ādi a bhāvāt tarhi kartṛ tā api na yuktāḥ kāryasya śarīreṇa saha vyabhicāra darśanāt yathā sva śarīrasya pravṛtti nivṛttī sarvaḥ cetanaḥ karoti tena tasya vyabhicāraḥ atha śarīre eva dṛṣṭa tvāt karotu na anyatra tat na yatas kāryam śarūreṇa ninā karoti iti naḥ sādhyam tat sva śarīra gatam anya śarīra gatam vā iti na anena kiñcid etena etat api parākṛtam yat āhuḥ eke 
TBV_4.26–4.27	 acetanaḥ katham bhāvaḥ tad icchām anuvartate acetanasya śarīra ādeḥ ātma icchā anuvartti tva darśanāt na ca acetanasya tad icchān anuvarttinaḥ api prayatna prerya tvam parikāraḥ iti vaktavyam yatas īṣvarasya api prayatna sadbhāve na kācid kṣatiḥ na ca śarīra abhāvāt katham prayatnaḥ iti vaktum yuktam śarīra antara abhāve api śarīrasya prayatna prerya tva darśanāt tat kartuḥ śarīra abhāvāt akṛṣṭa utpattiṣu sthāvareṣu agrahaṇam na tatra adarśanena hetoḥ vyabhicāraḥ ye api pratyakṣa anupalambha sādhanam kārya kāraṇa bhāvam āhuḥ teṣām api kasyacid kārya kāraṇa bhāvasya tad sādhana tve yathā indriyānām adṛṣṭasyaḥ ca tau vinā kāraṇa tvam siddhiḥ tathā īśvarasya api atas na vyāpti abhāvaḥ 
TBV_4.28–4.30	 atas eva na sat pratipakṣatā api na ekasmin sādhya anvite hetau sthite dvitīyasya tathāvidhasya tatra avakāśaḥ vastunaḥ dvairūpya asambhavāt na api bādhaḥ abuddhimat kāraṇa pūrvakatvasya pramāṇena agrahaṇāt sādhya abhāve hetoḥ abhāvaḥ sva sādhya vyāpta tvāt eva siddhaḥ na api dharmya siddha tā kārya kāraṇa saṅghātasya pṛthivī ādeḥ bhūta grāmasya ca pramāṇena siddha tvāt tad āśraya tvena hetoḥ yathā pramāṇena upalambhaḥ tathā pūrvam pradarśitam atas asmāt īśvara avagame na tad siddhau pramāṇa abhāvaḥ 
TBV_4.31	 na api hetoḥ viśeṣa viruddha tā tad viruddha tve hetoḥ viśeṣaṇe abhyupagamyamāne na kaścid dhetuḥ anuruddaḥ bhavet prasiddha anumāne api viśeṣa viruddha ādīnām sulabha tvāt yathā ayam dhūmaḥ dahanam sādhayati tathā etat deśa avacchinna vahni abhāvam api sādhayati na hi pūrva dhūmasya etat deśa avacchinnena vahninā vyāptiḥ evam kāla ādi avacchedena hetoḥ viruddha tā vaktavyā atha deśa kāla dīn vihāya vahni mātreṇa hetoḥ vyāpteḥ na viruddha tā tarhi tadvat kārya mātrasya buddhimat kāraṇa pūrvaka tvena vyāpteḥ yadi api dṛṣṭānte anīśvaraḥ asarvajñaḥ kṛtrima jñāna sambandhī sa śarīraḥ kṣiti ādi upaviṣṭaḥ kartā tathā api pūrva ukta viśeṣaṇānām dharmi viśeṣa rūpānām vyabhicārāt tad viparyaya sādhaka tve api na viruddha tā 
TBV_4.32–4.35	 viruddaḥ hi hetuḥ sādhya viparyaya kāri tvāt bhavati na ca eteṣām sādhya tā buddhimat kāraṇa pūrvakatva mātrasya asmāt dhetoḥ sādhya tvena iṣṭa tvāt yathā ca viśeṣa viruddhinām adūṣaṇa tvam tathā siddhāntam abhyupetya tad virodhī viruddhaḥ iti atra sūtre nirṇītam itaṣ ca etat adūṣaṇam pūrvasmāt dhetoḥ sva sādhya siddhau uttareṇa pūrva siddhasya eva sādhyasya kim viśeṣaḥ sādhyate uta pūrva hetoḥ sva sādhya siddhi pratibandhaḥ kriyate na tāvat pūrvaḥ vikalpaḥ yadi nāma tatra apareṇa hetunā viśeṣādhānām kṛtam kim tāvatā pūrvasya hetoḥ sādhya siddhi vighātaḥ yathā kṛtaka tvena śabdasya anitya tva siddhau hetu antareṇa guṇa tva siddhau api na pūrvasya kṣatiḥ tadvat atra api atha uttaraḥ vikalpaḥ tathā api sva sādhya siddhi pratibandhaḥ vyāpti abhāva pradarśanenea kriyate vyāpya bhāvaḥ ca hetu rūpāṇām anyatama abhāvena na ca dharmi viśeṣa viparyaya udbhāvanena kasyacid api rūpasya abhāvaḥ kathyate na ca hetu rūpa abhāva asiddhau agamaka tvam tat na viśeṣa viruddha tā 
TBV_4.36	 viśeṣāḥ tu dharmiṇaḥ svarūpa siddhau uttara kālam pramāṇa antara pratipādyāḥ na tu pūrva hetu balāt abhyupagamyante tat ca pramāṇa antaram āgamaḥ pūrva hetoḥ hetu antaram ca tat ca anvaya vyatireki pūrvaka kevala vyatireki saṃjñam yathā gandha ādi upalabdhyā tad sādhana karaṇa mātra prasiddhau prasakta pratiṣedhe karaṇa viśeṣa siddhiḥ kevala vyatireki nimittā tathā iha api kāryatvāt buddhimat kāraṇa mātra prasiddhau prasakta pratiṣedhāt kāraṇa viśeṣa siddhiḥ kevala vyatireki nimittāḥ tathā hi kāryatvāt buddhimat kāraṇa mātra siddhau prasaktānām kṛtrima jñāna śarīra sambaddha tva ādīnām dharmāṇām pramāna antareṇa bādha upapattau viśiṣṭa buddhimat kāraṇa siddhiḥ vyatireki balāt iti kecid 
TBV_4.37^1	 anye manyante yatra anvaya vyatirekiṇaḥ hetoḥ na viśeṣa siddhiḥ tatra tad pūrvakāt kevala vyatirekiṇaḥ viśeṣa siddiḥ bhavatu yathā ghrāṇa ādiṣu atra tu pūrvasmāt dhetoḥ viśeṣa siddhau na hetu antara parikalpanā yathā dhūmasya vahninā anvaya vyatireka siddhau atra deśe vahniḥ iti pakṣa dharma tva balāt pratipattiḥ na anvayāt vyatirekāt vā tayoḥ hi etad deśa avacchinnena vahninā sambhavāt yadi api vyāpti kāle sakala ākṣepeṇa tad deśasya api ākṣepaḥ anyathā atra vyāpteḥ asambhavāt tathā api vyāpti grahaṇa velāyām sāmānya rūpa tayā tat ākṣepaḥ na viśeṣa rūpeṇa iti viśeṣa avagamaḥ na anvaya vyatireka nimmittaḥ api tu pakṣa dharma tva kṛtaḥ 
TBV_4.37^2	 atas eva pratyutpanna kāraṇa janyām smṛtim anumānam āhuḥ pratyutpannam ca kāraṇam pakṣa dharma tvam eva tathā kāryatva ādeḥ buddhimat kāraṇa mātreṇa vyāpti siddhau api kāraṇa viśeṣa pratipattiḥ pakṣa dharma tva sāmarthyāt yaḥ itthaṃbhūtasya pṛthivī ādeḥ kartā niyamena asau akṛtrima jñāna sambandhī śarīra rahitaḥ sarvajñaḥ ekaḥ iti evam yadā pakṣa dharma tva balāt viśeṣa siddhiḥ tadā na viśeṣa viruddha ādīnām avakāśaḥ 
TBV_4.38	 anvaya sāmarthyāt api viśeṣa siddhim anye manyante tathā dhūma mātrasya vahni mātreṇa vyāptiḥ evam dhūma viśeṣasya vahni viśeṣaṇaḥ iti dhūma viśeṣa pratipattau na vahni mātreṇa anvaya anusmṛtiḥ kintu vahni viśeṣeṇa evaṃviśiṣṭa kāryatva darśanāt na kāraṇa mātra anusmṛtiḥ kintu tathāvidha kārya viśeṣa janaka kāraṇa viśeṣa anusmṛtiḥ tad anusmṛtau atra anvaya sāmarthyāt eva karaṇa viśeṣa pratipattiḥ iti na viśeṣa viruddha avakāśaḥ 
TBV_4.39	 eteṣām pakṣānām yukta ayukta tvam sūrayaḥ vicārayiṣyanti iti na asmākam atra nirbandhaḥ sarvathā viśeṣa viruddhasya adūṣaṇa tvam asmābhiḥ pratipādyate tad viruddha lakṣaṇa paryālocanayā prasaktānām ca viśeṣāṇām pramāṇa antara bādhayā anvaya vyatireki mūla kevala vyatireki balāt vā pakṣa dharma tva sāmarthyena vā kārya viśeṣasya kāraṇa viśeṣa anvita tvena vā na atra prayatyate sarvathā prastuta hetau na vyāpti asiddhiḥ 
TBV_4.40	 prasaktānām viśeṣāṇām pramāṇa antara bādhayā viśeṣa viruddha tā anavakāśaḥ iti uktam tatra katamasya prasaktasya viśeṣasya kena pramāṇena nirākṛtiḥ śarīra sambandhasya tāvat vyāpti abhāvena śarīra antara rahitasya api ātmanaḥ sva śarīra dhāraṇa pareṇa kriyāsu yathā atha ātmanaḥ prayatna vat tvāt dhāraṇa ādi kriyāsu śarīra ādi ādhārāsu kartṛ tvam yuktam na īśvarasya tad rahita tvāt tathā ca bhavatām mukhyam kartṛ lakṣaṇam 
TBV_4.41–4.42	 jñāna cikīrṣā prayatnānām samavāyaḥ kartṛ tā iti kena īśvarasya tat rahita tvāt prayatna pratiṣedhaḥ kṛtaḥ ātma manaḥ saṃyoga janya tvāt prayatnasya īśvarasya tad asambhavāt kāraṇa abhāvāt tad niṣedhaḥ buddhiḥ tarhi īśvare katham tasyāḥ api manaḥ saṃyoga janya tā eva sā api mā bhūt kā naḥ kṣatiḥ nanu tat asat tā eva na tu anyā kācid sā api bhavatu tad abhāve kasya niśeṣaḥ śarīra ādi saṃyoga lakṣaṇaḥ sādhyate atas eva anyaiḥ uktam 
TBV_4.43	 na atīndriya artha pratiṣedhaḥ viśeṣasya kasyacid sādhanena nirākaraṇena vā kāryaḥ tad abhāve viśeṣa sādhanasyaḥ tad nirākaraṇa hetoḥ vā āśraya asiddha tvāt kintu atīndriyam artham abhyupagacchan tad siddhau pramāṇam praṣṭavyaḥ sa ced tad siddhau prayogakam hetum darśayati om iti kṛtvā asau pratipattavyaḥ atha na darśayati pramāṇa abhāvāt eva asau na asti na tu viśeṣa abhāvat tasmāt jñāna cikīrṣā prayatnānām samavāyaḥ asti īśvare te tu jñāna ādayaḥ asmad ādi jñāna ādibhyaḥ vilakṣaṇāḥ vailakṣaṇyam ca nitya tva ādi dharma yogāt tat na īśvara śarīrasya kartṛ viśeṣasya vyāpti abhāvāt siddhiḥ 
TBV_4.44	 na api asarvajña tvam viśeṣaḥ kulāla ādiṣu dṛṣṭaḥ tatra sādhyate tad siddau api viśeṣa viruddhasya vyāpti abhāvaḥ eva na hi asarva vidā kartrā kulāla ādinā kiñcid kāryam kriyate nanu kulāla ādeḥ sarva vid tve ca idānīm kaścid asarva vid evam eva yat yaḥ karoti sa tasya upādāna ādi kāraṇa kalāpam prayojanam ca jānāti anyathā tad kriyā yogāt sarvajña tvam ca prakṛta kārya tad nimitta apekṣam atas kulāla ādiḥ yathā kartā sva kāryasya sarvam jānāti upādāna ādi evam īśvare api sarva kartā sarvasya karaṇa prayojanam vivāda viṣayasya sarvasya upādāna kāraṇa ādi ca kartṛ tvāt eva jānāti atas katham asau asarva vid 
TBV_4.45	 anye tu āhuḥ kṣetrajñānām niyata artha viṣaya grahaṇam sarva vidadhiṣṭhitānām yathā pratiniyata śabda ādi viṣaya grāhakāṇām indriyāṇām aniyata viṣaya sarva vid adhiṣṭhitānām jīvat śarīre tathā ca indriya vṛtti uccheda lakṣanam kecid maraṇam āhuḥ cetanā anadhiṣṭhitānām asti ca kṣetrajñānām pratiniyata viṣaya grahaṇam tena api aniyata viṣaya sarva vid adhiṣṭhitena bhāvyam yaḥ asau kṣetrajña adhiṣṭhāyakaḥ anityata viṣayaḥ sa sa srva vid īśvaraḥ nanu evam tasya eva sakala kṣetrajña adhiṣṭhāyaka tvāt kim antargaḍu sthānīyaiḥ kṣetrajñaiḥ kṛtyam na kiñcid pramāṇa siddha tām muktvā nanu evam aniṣṭhā yathā indriya ādhiṣṭāyakaḥ kṣetrajñaḥ tad adhiṣṭhāyakaḥ ca īśvaraḥ evam anyaḥ api tad adhiṣṭhāyakaḥ astu bhavatu aniṣṭhā yadi tad sādhakam pramāṇam kiñcid asti na tu aniṣṭhā sādhakam kiñcid pramāṇam utpaśyāmaḥ tāvat eva anumāna sidda tvāt 
TBV_4.46–4.51	 āgamaḥ api asmin vastuni vidyate tathā ca bhagavān vyāsaḥ dvau imau puruṣau loke kṣaraḥ ca akṣaraḥ eva ca kṣaraḥ sarvāṇi bhūtāni kūṭasthaḥ akṣaraḥ ucyate uttamaḥ puruṣaḥ tu anyaḥ paramātmā iti udāhṛtaḥ yaḥ lokatrayam āviśya bibharti avyayaḥ īśvaraḥ tathā śrutiḥ ca tad pratipādikā upalabhyate viśvatas cakṣuḥ uta viśvatas mukhaḥ viśvatas bāhuḥ uta viśvatas pāt sam bāhubhyām dhamati sam patatraiḥ dyāvābhumī janayan devaḥ ekaḥ āste ityādi 
TBV_4.52^1	 na ca svarūpa pratipādakānām aprāmāṇyam pramāna janaka tvasya sadbhāvāt tathā hi pramājanaka tvena pramāṇasya prāmāṇyam na pravṛtti janaka tvena tat ca iha asti eva pravṛtti nirvṛttī tu puruṣasya sukha duḥkha sādhana tva adhyavasāye samarthasya arthi tvāt bhavataḥ iti atha vidhau aṅga tvāt amīṣām prāmāṇyam na svarūpa artha tvāt iti ced tat asat sva artha pratipādaka tvena vidhi aṅga tvāt tathā hi stuteḥ sva artha pratipādaka tvena pravartaka tvam nindāyāḥ tu nivartaka tvam iti anyathā hi tad artha aparijñāne vihita pratiṣiddheṣu aviśeṣeṇa pravṛttiḥ nivṛttiḥ vā syāt tathā vidhi vākyasya api sva artha pratipādana dvāreṇa eva puruṣa preraka tvam dṛṣṭam evam svarūpa pareṣu api vākyeṣu syāt vākya svarūpa tāyāḥ aviśeṣāt viśeṣa hetoḥ ca abhāvāt iti tathā svarūpa arthānām aprāmāṇye medhyāḥ āpaḥ darbhāḥ pavitram amedhyam aśuci iti evam svarūpa aparijñāne vidhi aṅga tāyām api aviśeṣeṇa pravṛtti nivṛtti prasaṅgaḥ na ca etat asti medhyeṣu eva pravartate amedhyeṣu ca nivartate iti upalambhāt 
TBV_4.52^2	 tat evam svarūpa arthebhyaḥ vākyebhyaḥ artha svarūpa avabodhe sati iṣṭe pravṛtti darśanāt aniṣṭe ca nivṛtteḥ iti jñāyate svarūpa arthānām pramājanaka tvena pravṛttau nivṛttau vā vidhi sahakāri tvam iti aparijñānāt tu pravṛttau atiprasaṅgaḥ atha dvarūpa arthānām prāmāṇye grāvāṇaḥ plavante iti evamādīnām api yathārtha tā syāt na mukhye bādhaka upapatteḥ yatra hi mukhye bādhakam pramāṇam asti tatra upacāra kalpanā tad abhāve tu prāmāṇyam eva na ca īśvara sadbhāva pratipādaneṣu kiñcid asti bādhakam iti svarūpe prāmāṇyam abhyupagantavyam iti āgamāt api siddha prāmāṇyāt tad avagamaḥ īśvarasya ca sattā mātreṇa sva viṣaya grahaṇa pravṛttānām kṣetrajñānām adhiṣṭāyaka tā yathā sphaṭika ādīnām upadhāna ākara grahaṇa pravṛttāṇām savitṛ prakāśaḥ yathā teṣām sāvitram prakāśam vinā na upadhāna ākāra grahaṇa sāmarthyam tathā īśvaram vinā kṣetra vidām na sva viṣaya grahaṇa sāmarthyam iti asti bhagavaṇ īśvaraḥ sarva vid 
TBV_4.53	 itas ca asau sarva vid jñānasya sannihita sadartha prakāśaka tvam nāma svabhāvam tasya anyathā bhāvaḥ kutaścid doṣa sadbhāvāt etat tāvat rūpam cakṣuḥ ādi āśrayāṇām jñānānām yat punar cakṣuḥ anāśritam na ca rāga ādi mala āvṛtam tasya viṣaya prakāśana svabhāvasya viṣayeṣu kim iti prakāśana sāmarthya vighātaḥ yathā dīpa ādeḥ pavaraka antargatasysa nanu rāga ādeḥ āvaraṇasya katham tatra abhāvaḥ avagataḥ tad pratipādaka pramāṇa abhāvāt pramāṇasya abhāve saṃśayaḥ astu rāga ādīnām na tu abhāvaḥ viparyāsa kāraṇā rāga ādayaḥ eṣām kāraṇa abhāve katham tatra bhāvaḥ viparyāsaḥ ca adharma nimittaḥ na ca bhagavati adharmaḥ tad sadbhāve vā itthaṃvidhasya asmad ādibhiḥ cintayitum api aśakyasya kāryasya katham tasmāt utpādaḥ aneka adṛṣṭa kalpanā prasaṅgāt kiñca rāga ādayaḥ iṣṭa aniṣṭa sādhaneṣu viṣayeṣu upajāyamānāḥ dṛṣṭāḥ na ca bhagavataḥ kaścid iṣṭa aniṣṭa sādhanaḥ doṣayaḥ avāpta kāma tvāt 
TBV_4.54–4.59^1	 yā tu pravṛttiḥ śarīra ādi sarge sā kaiścid krīḍā artham uktāḥ sā ca āvapta prayojanānām eva bhavati na tu anyeṣām atas yat uktam vārttika kṛtā kṛīḍā hi ratim avindatām na ca rati arthī bhagavān duḥkha abhāvāt tat pratikṣiptam na hi duḥkhitāḥ krīḍāsu pravartante tasmāt krīḍā arthā pravṛttiḥ anye manyante kārūṇyāt bhagavataḥ pravṛttiḥ nanu evam kevalaḥ sukha rūpaḥ prāṇi sargaḥ astu na evam nirapekṣasya kartṛ tve ayam doṣaḥ sa apekṣa tve tu katham eka rūpaḥ sargaḥ yasya yathāvidhaḥ karma āśayaḥ puṇya rūpaḥ apuṇya rūpaḥ vā tasya tathāvidha phala upabhogāya tad sādhanān śarīra ādīn tathāvidhān tad sāpekṣaḥ sṛjati iti 
TBV_4.54–4.59^2	 na ca īśvara tva vyāghātaḥ sa apekṣa tve api yathā savitṛ prakāśasya sphaṭika ādi apekṣasya yathā nā karaṇa ādhiṣṭāyakasya kṣetrajñasya sa apekṣa tve api teṣu tasya īśvara tā tadvat atra api na īśvaratā visam ghātaḥ iti kecid anye manyante yathā prabhuḥ sevā bheda anurodhena phala bheda pradaḥ na aprabhuḥ tathā īśvaraḥ api karma āśaya apekṣaḥ phalam janayati iti anīśvaraḥ iti na yujyate vaktum bhāṣya kāraḥ kārūṇi apreritasya pravṛttim āha tad nimittāyām api pravṛttau na vārttikakārī iyam dūṣaṇam 
TBV_4.60	 saṃsṛjeta śubham eva ekam anukampā prayojitaḥ iti evamādi yatas karma āśayānām kuśala akuśala rūpānām phala upabhogam vinā na kṣayaḥ iti bhagavān anagacchan tad upabhogāya prāṇi sargam karoti upabhohgaḥ karma phalasya śarīra ādi kṛtaḥ kasyacid tu aśubhasya karmaṇaḥ prāyaścittāt prakṣayaḥ tatra api su alpena duḥkha upabhogena dīrgha kāla duḥkha pradam karma kṣīyate na tu phalam adattvā karma kṣayah yeṣām api matam samyak jñānāt viparyāsa nivṛttau tad janya kleśa kṣaye karma āśayānām sadbhāve api saha kārya bhāvāt na śarīra ādi ākṣepaka tā tatra api kuśalam karma samādhim na antareṇa na tattva jñāna utpattiḥ tayoḥ tu sañcaye pravṛttasya yama niyama anuṣṭhāne anekavidha duḥkha utpattiḥ atas katham kevala sukhi rūpaḥ prāṇi sargaḥ nāraka tiryak ādi sargaḥ api akṛta prāyaścittānām tatra atyaduḥkha anubhave punar viśiṣṭa sthāna avāptau abhyudaya hetuḥ iti siddham duḥkhi prāṇi sṛṣṭau api karuṇayā pravartanam tat na asarvajña tvam viśeṣaḥ 
TBV_4.61^1	 na api kṛtrima jñāna sambandhi tvam tat jñānasya pratyartha niyama abhāvāt yat jñānam anityam tat śarīra ādi sāpekṣam pratyartha niyatam tad jjānasya tu śasrīḥ ādi abhāve kutas prati artha niyata tā bhavatu tat jñānam pratiniyata viṣayam na tasya pratiniyata viṣayave asmākam pakṣa kṣatiḥ katham na kṣatiḥ tasya tathāvidha tve yugapad sthāvara anutpāda prasaṅgaḥ tad anutpāde ca kartṛ tva asiddhiḥ tad asiddhau kasya kṛtrimajjāna sambandhitā viśeṣaḥ atha yugapad kāryā ani atha anupapattyā pratyartha niyatām anekām buddhim īśvare pratipadyeta tatra api santānena vā tathābhūtāḥ buddhayaḥ yugapad vā bhaveyuḥ prācye vikalpe punar api yugapad kārya anutpāda prasaṅgaḥ yugapad utpattau vā buddhīnām śarīra ādi yogaḥ tasya aiṣitavyah sa ca pūrvam pratikṣiptaḥ 
TBV_4.61^2	 atha kāryasya bahu tva mahat tvābhyām bahavaḥ buddhimantaḥ kartāraḥ bhavantu na tu ekaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarva śakti yuktaḥ nanu etasmin api pakṣe īśvara anekatva prasaṅgaḥ bhavatu kaḥ doṣaḥ vyāhata kāmānām svatantrāṇām ekasmin arthe apravṛttiḥ atha tad madhye anyeṣām eka āyattatā tadā saḥ eva īśvaraḥ anye punar tad adhīnāḥ anīśvarāḥ atha sthapati ādīnām mahā prasāda ādi karaṇe yathā ekamatyam tadvat atra api na etat evam tatra kasyacid abhiprāyeṇa niyamitānām aikamatyam na tu atra bahūnām niyāmakaḥ kaścid asti sadbhāve vā saḥ eva īśvaraḥ evam yasya yasya viśeṣasya sādhanāya vā nirākṛtaye vā pramānam ucyate tasya tasya pūrva uktena nyāyena nirākaraṇam kartavyam tat na viśeṣa viruddha tā īśvara sādhakasya 
TBV_4.62	 prasaṅga viparyayayoḥ api anutpattiḥ prasaṅgasya vyāpti abhāvāt tad mūla tvāt tad viparyayasya tathā iṣṭa vihāta kṛtaḥ ca yat ca nitya tvāt akartṛka tvam ucyate śākyaiḥ tat api kṣaṇa bhaṅga bhaṅge pratikṣiptam yat api vyāpāram vinā na kartṛ tvam tat api jñāna cikīrṣā prayatna lakṣaṇasya vyāpārasya ukta tvāt nirākṛtam 
TBV_4.63–4.65	 vārttikakāreṇa aparam pramāṇa dvayam upanyastam tad siddhaye mahābhūta ādi vyaktam cetanā adhiṣṭhitam prāṇinām sukha duḥkha nimittam rūpa ādimat tvāt turya ādi vat tathā pṛthivī ādīni mahābhūtāni buddhimat kāraṇa adhiṣṭhitāni svāsu dhāraṇa ādyāsu kriyāsu pravartante anitya tvāt vā asya ādi vat iti aviddha karṇaḥ tu tad siddhaye idam pramāṇa dvayam āha 
TBV_4.66–4.69	 dvi indriya grāhya agrāhyam vimati adhikaraṇa bhāva āpannam buddhimat kāraṇa pūrvakam su a ārambhaka avaya vasanniveśa viśiṣṭa tvāt ghaṭa ādi vat vaidhyarmyeṇa paramāṇavaḥ iti tatra dvābhyām darśana sparśana indriyābhyām grāhyam mahat aneka dravyavat tva rūpa ādi upalabdhi kāraṇa upetam pṛthivī udaka jvalana saṃjñakam trividham dravyam dvi indriya grāhyam agrāhyam vāyu ādi yasmāt mahat tvam aneka dravyavat tvaṇ rūpa samavāya ādiḥ ca upalabdhi kāraṇam iṣyate tat ca vāyyādau na asti yathā uktam mahati aneka dravyavat tvāt rūpāt ca upalabdhiḥ rūpa saṃskāra abhāvāt vāyau anupalabdhiḥ rūpa saṃskāraḥ rūpa samavāyaḥ dvi aṇuka ādīnām tu anupalabdhiḥ amahat tvāt iti anye tu vāyoḥ api sparśana indriya pratyakṣa grāhya tvam icchanti 
TBV_4.70^1	 dvi indriya grāhya tva apekṣayā tu rūpa samavāya abhāvāt anupalabdhiḥ iti uktam tatra sāmānyena dvi indriya grāhya agrāhyasya buddhimat kārana pūrvaka tva sādhane siddha sādhya tā doṣah ghaṭa ādiṣu ubhaya siddheḥ vivāda abhāvāt abhyupeta bādhā ca aṇu ākāśa ādīnām tathā anabhyupagamāt teṣām ca nitya tvāt pratyakṣa ādi bādhāḥ tatas tad artham vimati adhikaraṇa bhāva āpanna grahaṇam vividhā matiḥ vimatiḥ vipratipattiḥ iti yāvat tasyāḥ adhikaraṇa bhāva āpannam vivāda spadībhūtam iti arthaḥ evam ca sati śarīra indriya bhuvana ādayaḥ eva atra pakṣīkṛtāḥ iti na aṇu ādi prasaṅgaḥ kāraṇa mātra pūrvaka tve api sādhye siddha sādhya tā me bhūt iti buddhimat kāraṇa grahaṇam 
TBV_4.70^2	 sāṅkhyam prati matu bartha anupapatteḥ na siddha sādhya tā avyatiriktā hi buddhiḥ pradhānāt sāṅkhyaiḥ ucyate na ca tena eva tat eva tadvat bhavati su a ārambhakāṇām avayavānām sanniveśaḥ pracaya ātmakaḥ saṃyogaḥ tena viśiṣṭam vyavacchinnam tad bhāvaḥ tasmāt avayava sanniveśa viśiṣṭa tvam go tva ādibhiḥ vyabicāri iti atas su a ārambhaka grahaṇam go tva ādīni tu dravya ārambhaka avayava sanniveśena viśiṣyante na tu su a ārambhaka avayava sanniveśena iti tena yaḥ asau buddhimān saḥ īśvaraḥ iti ekam dvitīyam tu tanu bhuvana karaṇa upādānāni cetana acetanāni cetanā adhiṣṭhitāni svaka arayam arabhante iti pratijānīmahe rūpa ādimat tvāt yat yat rūpa ādimat tat tat cetana adhiṣṭhitam sva kāryam ārabhate yaḥ asau cetanaḥ tanu bhuvana karaṇa upādāna ādeḥ adhiṣṭātā sa bhagavān īśvaraḥ iti 
TBV_4.71–4.74	 uddyota karaḥ tu pramāṇayati bhuvana hetavaḥ pradhāna paramāṇu adṛṣṭāḥ sva kārya utpattau atiśaya buddhimantam adhiṣṭhātāram apekṣante sthitvā pravṛtteḥ tantu turya ādi vat iti praśasta matiḥ tu āha sarga ādau puruṣānām vyavahāraḥ anya upadeśa pūrvakaḥ uttara kālam prabuddhānām pratyartha niyata tvāt aprasiddha vāc vyavahārāṇām kumārāṇām gavā ādiṣu pratyartha niyataḥ vāc vyāvahāraḥ yathā mātṛ ā ādi upadeśa pūrvakaḥ iti prabuddhānām pratyartha niyata tvāt iti prabuddhānām satām pratyartham niyata tvāt iti arthaḥ yat upadeśa pūrvakaḥ ca sa sarga ādau vyavahāraḥ saḥ īśvaraḥ pralaya kālaḥ api alupta jñāna atiśayaḥ iti siddham 
TBV_4.75–4.77	 tathā aparāṇi api uddyota kareṇa tad siddhaye sādhanāni upanyastāni buddhimat kāraṇa adhiṣṭhitam mahābhūta ādikam vyaktam sukha duḥkha nimittam bhavati acetana tvāt kāryatvāt vināśitavāt rupādimat tvāt vā asya ādi vat iti atha bhavatu asmāt dhetu kadambakāt īśvarasysa sarva jagat hetu tva siddhiḥ sarvajña tvam tu katham tasya siddham yena asau niḥśreyasa abhyudaya kāmānām bhakti viṣaya tām yāyāt jagat kartṛ tva siddheḥ vā iti brūmaḥ tathā ca āhuḥ praśastam ati prabhṛtayaḥ 
TBV_4.78^1	 kartuḥ kārya upādāna upakaraṇa prayojana sampradāna parijñānāt iha hi yaḥ yasya kartā bhavati sa tasya upādāna ādīni jānīte yathā kulālaḥ kuṇḍa ādīnām kartā tad upādānam mṛd piṇḍam upakaraṇāni cakra ādīni prayojanam udaka āharaṇa ādi kuṭumbinam ca sampradānam jānīte iti etat siddham tathā īśvaraḥ sakala bhuvanānām kartā sa tad upādāni paramāṇu ādi lakṣanāni tad upakaranāni dharma diś kāla ādīni vyavahāra upakaraṇāni sāmānya viśeṣa samavāya lakṣāṇāni prayojanam upabhogam sampradāna saṃjñakān ca pururṣān jānīte iti atas siddham asya sarvajña tvam iti 
TBV_4.78^2	 atas eva na atra etat preraṇīyam sarvajña pūrvaka tve kṣiti ādīnām sādhye sādhya vikalaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ hetuḥ ca viruddhaḥ asarvajña kartṛ pūrvaka tvena kumbha ādeḥ kāryasya vyāpti darśanāt kiñcid jña pūrvaka tve sādhye abhyupeta bādhāḥ kāraṇa mātra pūrvaka tve sādhye karmaṇā siddha sādhanam iti yatas sāmānyena sva kārya upādāna upakaraṇa sampradāna abhijña kartṛ pūrvaka tvam sādhyate tatra ca asti eva vastra ādi dṛṣṭāntaḥ tasya hi upādāna upakaraṇa ādi abhijña kartṛ pūrvaka tvam sakala loka prasiddham katham anyathā kartum śakyate apahnotum vā 
TBV_4.79	 na tu karmaṇā siddha sādhya tā tasya sakala jagat lakṣaṇa kārya upādāna ādi anabhijña tvāt tad abhijña tve vā tasya eva bhagavataḥ karma iti nāma antaram kṛtam syāt śeṣam tu atra cintitam eva tat evam sakala doṣa rahitāt ukta hetu kalāpāt jñāna ādi atiśaya vat guṇa yuktasya siddheḥ tasya ca śāsana praṇetṛ tvam na anyeṣam yoginām iti bhava jinānām śāsanam iti ayuktam uktam iti sthitam iti pūrva pakṣaḥ 
TBV_5.1	 atra pratividhīyate yat tāvat uktam sāmānyatodṛṣṭa anumānasya tatra vyāpāra abhyupagamāt pratyakṣa pūrvaka anumāna niṣedhe siddha sādhanam iti tat asaṅgatam sāmānyatodṛṣṭa anumānasya api tad sādhaka tvena apravṛtteḥ tathā hi tanu bhuvana karaṇa ādikam buddhimat kāraṇa pūrvakam kāryatvāt ghaṭa ādi vat iti atra dharmya siddheḥ āśraya asiddhaḥ tāvat kāryatva lakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ 
TBV_5.2	 tathā hi avayavi rūpam tāvat tanu ādi avabhāsamāna tanu na yuktam deśa ādi bhinnasya tanu ādeḥ sthūlasya ekasya anupapatteḥ na hi aneka deśa ādi gatam ekam bhavitum yuktam viruddha dharma adhyāsasya bheka lakṣaṇa tvāt deśa ādi bhedaya ca viruddha dharma rūpa tvāt tathā api abhede sarvatra bhinna tvena abhyupagate ghaṭa paṭa ādau api bheda uparati prasaṅgāt na hi binna tvena abhyupagate tatra api anyat bheda nibandhanam utpaśyāmaḥ pratibhāsa bhedāt tatra bhedaḥ iti ced na viruddha dharma adhyāsam bhedakam antareṇa pratibhāsasya api bheda anupapatteḥ 
TBV_5.3^1	 atha avayavī ekaḥ na bhavati viruddha dharma adhyāsita tvāt iti etat kim svatantra sādhanam uta prasaṅga sādhanam iti na tāvat svatantra sādhanam yuktam avayavinaḥ pramāṇa asiddhatvena hetoḥ āśraya asiddha tva doṣāt pramāṇa siddha tve vā tad pratipādaka pramāṇa bādhita pakṣa nirdeśa anantara prayukta tvena tasya kāla atyaya apadiṣṭa tva doṣa duṣṭa tvāt na ca parasya avayavī siddhaḥ iti na āśraya asiddha tva doṣaḥ iti vaktum yuktam yatas parasya kim pramāṇataḥ asau siddhaḥ uta apramāṇataḥ pramāṇataḥ ced tarhi bhavataḥ api kim na siddhaḥ pramāṇa siddhasya sarvān pratyaviśeṣāt 
TBV_5.3^2	 tathā ca tat eva kāla atyaya apadiṣṭa tvam hetoḥ atha apramāṇataḥ tadā na parasya api siddhaḥ iti punar api āśraya asiddha tvam tat na prathamaḥ pakṣaḥ na api dvitīyaḥ yatas vyāpya abhyupagamaḥ yatra vyāpaka abhyupagamana antarīyakaḥ pradarśyate tat prasaṅga sādhanam na ca parasya bheda viruddha dharma adhyāsayoḥ vyāpya vyāpaka bhāvaḥ siddhaḥ deṣa ādi bheda lakṣaṇa viruddha dharma adhyāsa abhāve api rūpa rasayoḥ bheda abhyupagamāt tad bhāve api sāmānya ādau abhedasya pramāna siddha tvāt iti na vaktavyam 
TBV_5.4	 yatas prathamaḥ pakṣaḥ tāvat anabhyupagamāt eva nirastaḥ prasaṅga sādhana pakṣe tu yat dūṣaṇam abhihitam deśa bheda lakṣaṇa viruddha dharma adhyāsa abhāve api rūpa rasayoḥ bhedaḥ iti tat vyāpya vyāpaka bhāva aparijñānam sūcayati na punar vyāpya vyāpaka bhāva abhāvam yatas deśa bhede sati yadi abhedah kaścid siddhaḥ syāt tadā vyāpaka abhāve api viruddha dharma adhyāsasya bhāvān na tasya tena vyāptiḥ syāt yadā tu deśa abhede api rūpa rasayoḥ bhedaḥ tadā deśa bhedaḥ bheda vyāpakaḥ na syāt na punar etāvatā bhedaḥ viruddha dharma adhyāsa vyāpakaḥ na syāt yadi hi bheda vyāvṛttau api deśa ādi bhedaḥ na vyāvarteta tadā vyāpaka vyāvṛttau= api vyāpyasya avyāvṛttena bhedena deśa ādi viruddha dharma adhyāsaḥ vyāpyeta na ca etat kvacid api siddham yat tu sāmāṇi ādau abhedasya pramāṇataḥ siddheḥ bheda vyāvṛttau api na deṣa ādi bheda lakṣaṇasya viruddha dharma adhyāsasya nivṛttiḥ iti tat ayuktam sāmānya ādeḥ pramāṇataḥ abhinna rūpasya asiddheḥ uktam ca 
TBV_5.5–5.6	 yadi viruddha dharma adhyāsaḥ padārthānām bhedakaḥ na syāt tadā anyasya tad bhedakasya abhāvāt viśvam ekam syāt pratibhāsa bhedasya api tam antareṇa bheda vyavasthāpakasya abhāvāt iti vyāpya vyāpaka bhāva siddheḥ katham na prasaṅga sādhanasya atra avakāśaḥ atha eka tva pratibhāsāt deśa ādi bhede api tanu ādeḥ ekatā na deśa bhedena vyavasthitānām avayavānām pratibhāsa bhedena bhedāt na hi eka rūpāḥ bhāgāḥ bhāsante piṇḍasya aṇu mātra tā āpatteḥ tad vyatiriktasya ca aparasya tanu ādi avayavinaḥ dravyasya upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupalambhena asattvāt na ca tasya upalabdhi lakṣana prāpta tā paraiḥ na abhyupagamyate 
TBV_5.7–5.8^1	 mahati aneka dravyavat tvāt rūpāt ca upalabdhiḥ iti vacanāj tat siddam anupalabdheḥ upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya iti viśeṣaṇam na ca madhya ūrdhva ādi bhāga vyatirikta vapuḥ bahis grāhya ākāra tām bibhrāṇas tanu ādiḥ dravya ātmā darśane cakāsti iti anupalabdhiḥ api siddhāḥ na ca samāna deśa tvāt avayavinaḥ avayavebhyaḥ pṛthak anupalakṣaṇam iti vaktum śakyam samāna deśa tvāt iti vikalpa anupapatteḥ tathā hi samāna deśa tvam avayava avayavinoḥ kim pāribhāṣikam laukikam vā yadi pāribhāṣikam tat anudghoṣyam paribhāṣāyāḥ atra anadhikārāt na ca tat tatra bhavat abhiprāyeṇa siddham 
TBV_5.8^2	 tathā hi anyaḥ eva pāṇi ādayaḥ ārambhakāḥ diśāḥ tanu ādi avayavinaḥ bhavadbhiḥ paribhāṣyante anye ca pāṇi ādīnām tad avayavānām ārambhakāḥ deśāḥ ārabhya ārambhaka vāda niṣedhāt tat na pāribhāṣikam samāna deśa tvam na api laukikam ākāśasi sa loka prasiddhasya samāna deśasya asmān prati asiddha tvāt prakāśa dirūpasya ca deśasysa tad siddhasya samāna tve api bhinnānām vāta ātapa ādīnām bhedena upalabdheḥ tathā hi samāna deśāḥ api bhāvāḥ vāta ātapa ādayaḥ bhinnatnu avaḥ pṛthak prathante na ca evam avayavi nirbhāsaḥ tat na avayavī tanu ādiḥ bhinnaḥ asti 
TBV_5.9^1	 atha manda manda prakāśe avayava pratibhāsam antareṇa api avayavini pratibhāsaḥ upalabhyate tat katham pratibhāsā bhāvāt tasya abhāvah asat etat na hi tathābhūtaḥ aspaṣṭa pratibhāsaḥ avayavi svarūpa vyavasthāpakaḥ yuktaḥ tad pratibhāsasyā spaṣṭa rūpasya spaṣṭa jñāna avabhāsi tat svarūpeṇa virodhāt atha sva srūpa dvayam etat avayavinaḥ spaṣṭam aspaṣṭam ca tatra aspaṣṭam manda āloka jñāna viṣayaḥ spaṣṭam tu sāloka jñāna bhūmiḥ nanu etat svarūpa dvayam kena avayavinaḥ gṛhyate na tāvat manda āloka jñānena tatra sa āloka jñāna viṣaya spaṣṭa rūpa anavabhāsanāt aspaṣṭa tad svarūpa pratibhāsam hi tat anubhūyate 
TBV_5.9^2	 na api sa āloka jñānena spaṣṭa tad svarūpa avabhāsinā tatra manda āloka jñāna avabhāsi tat svarūpa anavabhāsanāt na hi parisphuṭa pratibhāsa velāyām aviśada rūpa ākāraḥ avayavi arthaḥ pratibhāti tat katham asau avayavinaḥ sva rūpam atha manda āloka dṛṣṭam avayavinaḥ svarūpam parisphuṭam idānīm paśyāmi iti tayoḥ ekatā nanu kim aparisphuṭa rūpa tayā parisphuṭam rūpam avagamyate āhosvit parisphuṭa tayā parisphuṭām tatra yadi ādyaḥ pakṣaḥ tadā aparisphuṭa rūpa sambandhi tvam eva avayavinaḥ prāpnoti parisphuṭasya rūpasya asphuṭa rūpa tā anupraveśena pratibhāsanāt 
TBV_5.9^3	 atha dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ tathā asati spaṣṭa svarūpa sambandhi tvam eva aspaṣṭasya viśada svarūpa anupraviṣṭa tvena pratibhāsanāt tat na sva rūpa dvaya avagamaḥ avayavinaḥ eka tva pratibhāsanam tu pratibhāsa rahitam abhimāna mātram spaṣṭa aspaṣṭa rūpayoḥ anyathā sa āloka jñāna vat manda āloka jñānam api parisphuṭa pratibhāsam syāṭ atha āloka bhāva abhāva kṛtaḥ tatra spaṣṭa aspaṣṭa pratibhāsa bhedaḥ nanu ālokena api avayavi svarūpam eva udbhāsanīyam tat ced avikalam mandāloke pratibhāti katham na tatra tad avabhāsa kṛtaḥ spaṣṭa avabhāsaḥ anyathā viṣayāḥ avabhāsa vyatirekeṇa api jñāna pratibhāsa bhede na jñāna avabhāsa bhedaḥ rūpa rasayoḥ api bheda vyavasthāpakaḥ syāt 
TBV_5.9^4	 atha avayavi svarūpam ekam eva ubhayatra pratīyate vyakta avyakta ākārau tu jñānasya ātmanau iti ucyeta tat api asat yatas yadi jñāna ākārau tau katham avayavi rūpa tayā pratibhātaḥ tad rūpa tayā ca pratibhāsanāt avayavi ākārau tau abhyupagantavyau na hi vyakta rūpa tām avyakta rūpa tām ca muktvā avayavi svarūpam aparam ābhāti tat tasya anavabhāsāt abhāvaḥ eva vyakta avyakta eka ātmanaḥ ca avayavinaḥ vyakta avyakta ākāra vat bhedaḥ na hi pratibhāsa bhede api ekatā atiprasaṅgāt tat na aspaṣṭa pratibhāsam andhakāre avayavinaḥ rūpam avayava apratibhāse api pratibhāti iti vaktum yuktam ukta doṣa prasaṅgāt 
TBV_5.10	 kiñca kim katipaya avayava pratibhāsi sati avayavī pratibhāti iti abhyupagamyate āhosvit samasta avayava pratibhāse yadi ādyaḥ pakṣaḥ sa na yuktaḥ jala magna mahā kāya stambha ādeḥ uparitana katipaya avayava pratibhāse api samasta avayava vyāpinaḥ stambhādyavayavinaḥ apratibhāsanāt atha dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ saḥ api na yuktaḥ madhya para bhāga vartti samasta avayava pratibhāsā sambhavena avayavinaḥ apratibhāsa prasaṅgāt atha bhūyovayava grahaṇe sati avayavī gṛhyate iti abhyupagamaḥ saḥ api na yuktaḥ yatas arvāc bhāga bhāvi avayava grāhiṇā pratyakṣeṇa para bhāga bhāvi avayava agrahaṇāt na tena tad vyāptiḥ avayavinaḥ grahītum śakyāḥ vyāpya agrahaṇe tena tad vyāpaka tvasya api grahītum aśakteḥ grahaṇe vā atiprasaṅgaḥ tathā hi yat yena rūpeṇa avabhāti tat tena eva rūpeṇa sat iti vyavahāra viṣayaḥ 
TBV_5.11^1	 yathā nīlam nīla rūpa tayā pratibhāsamānam tena eva rūpeṇa tad viṣayaḥ arvāc bhāga bhāvi avayava sambandhi tayā ca avayavī pratibhāti iti svabhāva hetuḥ na ca para bhāga bhāvi vyavahita avayava apratibhāsane api avyavahitaḥ avayavī pratibhāti iti vaktum śakyam tat pratibhā āsane tad gata tvena apratibhāsanāt yasmin ca pratibhāsamāne yat rūpam na pratibhāti tat tatas bhinnam yathā ghaṭe pratibhāsamāne apratibhāsamānam paṭa svarūpam na pratibhāti ca arvāc bhāga bhāvi avayava sambandhya vayavi svarūpe pratibhāsamāne para bhāga bhāvi avayava sambandhya vayavi svarūpam iti katham na tat tatas bhinnam tathā api abhede ati prasaṅgaḥ pratipāditaḥ na api para bhāga bhāvi a vayava avayavi grāhiṇā pratyakṣeṇa arvāc bhāga bhāvi avayava sambandhi tvam tasya gṛhyate tatra tad avayavānām pratibhāsāt tad sambandhi eva avayavi svarūpam pratibhāseta na arvāc bhāga bhāvi avayava sambandhi teṣām tatra apratibhāsanāt 
TBV_5.11^2	 tad pratibhā āsane ca tad sambandhi rūpasya api apratibhāsanāt vyāpya apratipattau tad vyāpaka tvasya api apratipatteḥ na api smaraṇena arvāk para bhāga bhāvi avayava sambandhya vayavi svarūpa grahaḥ pratyakṣa anusāreṇa sa maraṇasya pravṛtti upapatteḥ pratyakṣasya ca tad grāhaka tva niṣedhāt na api ātmā arvāk para bhāga avayava vyāpi tvam avayavinaḥ gragītum samarthaḥ sattā mātreṇa tasya tad grāhaka tva anupapatteḥ anyathā svāpa mada mūrcchā ādi avasthāsu api tad pratipatti prasaṅgāt kintu darśana sahāyaḥ tat ca darśanam na avayavinaḥ avayava vyāpti grāhakam pratyakṣa ādikam sambhavati iti pratipāditam atha arvāk bhāga darśane sati uttara kālam para bhāga darśane anantara smaraṇa sahakāri indriya janitam saḥ eva ayam iti pratyabhijñā jñānam adhyakṣam avayavinaḥ pūrva apara avayava vyāpti grāhakam tat ayuktam pratyabhijñā jñānasya etat viṣayasya pratyakṣa tvā anupapatteḥ 
TBV_5.11^3	 akṣa anusāri hi pratyakṣam na ca akṣānām arvāk para bhāga bhāvi avayava grahaṇe vyāpāraḥ sambhavati vyavahite teṣām vyāpāra asambhavāt sambhave vā ati vyavahite api meru pṛṣṭha ādau vyāpāraḥ syāt tat na tad anusāriṇaḥ adhyakṣa rūpasya pratyabhijñā jñānasya tatra vyāpāraḥ na ca smaraṇa sahāyasya api indriyasya aviṣaye vyāpāraḥ sambhavati yat yasya aviṣayaḥ na tat tara smaraṇa sahāyam api pravartate yathā parimala smaraṇa sahāyam api locanam gandha ādau aviṣayaḥ ca vyavahitaḥ akṣāṇām para bhāga bhāvi avayava sambandhi tva lakṣaṇaḥ a vayavinaḥ svabhāvaḥ iti na akṣajasya pratyabhijñā jñānasya avayavi svarūpa grāhaka tvam na ca saḥ eva ayam iti pratītiḥ ekā saḥ iti smṛteḥ rūpam ayam iti tu dṛśaḥ sva rūpam tat parokṣa aparokṣa ākāra tvāt na eka svabhāvau etau pratyayau atha saḥ eva ayam iti eka adhikāraṇa tayā etau pratibhātaḥ iti ekam pratyabhijñā jñānam na ākāra bhede sati darśana smaraṇayoḥ iva sāmāna adhikaraṇya adhyavasāye api ekatva anupapatteḥ 
TBV_5.11^4	 anyatra api ākāra bhede eva bhedaḥ sa ca atra api vidyate iti katham eka tvam kiñca saḥ iti eva prāptaḥ na ayam iti api iti katham ekā pratyabhijñā atha saḥ eva ayam iti ākārau parasparān anupraviṣṭau pratibhātaḥ tathā api bhinna ākārau bhinna viṣayau ca dvau pratyayau iti katham eka arthāḥ ekā pratyabhijñā pratibhāsa bhedasya viṣaya bheda vyavasthāpaka tvāt na ca pratibhāsa bhede api viṣaya abhedaḥ pratibhāsā bheda vyatirekeṇa viṣaya abheda vyavasthāyām pramāṇam vinā prameya abhyupagamaḥ syāt tathā ca sarvam sarvasya sidhyeta tat na pratyabhijñātaḥ api avayavi ekatva grahaḥ anumānasya ca avayavi svarūpa grāhakasya pratyakṣa niṣedhe tad pūrvakasya niṣedhaḥ kṛtaḥ eva sāmānyatodṛṣṭasya ca avayavi pratiṣedha prastāve niṣedhaḥ vidhāsyate iti āstām tāvat 
TBV_5.12	 atha ekaḥ ghaṭaḥ iti dravya pratītiḥ asti tad avayava vyatirekiṇī tat katham abhāvaḥ avayavinaḥ na ghaṭāvasāye api tad avayava adhyavasāyaḥ nāma ullekhaḥ ca adhyavasīyate na avayavi dravayam varṇa ākṛti akṣara ākāra śūnyasya tad rūpasya kenacid api ananubhavāt varṇa ākṛti akṣara ākāra śūnyam ca avayavi svarūpam abhyupagamyate na ca tena rūpeṇa kalpanā jñāne api tat pratibhāti na ca anya ākāraḥ pratibhāsaḥ anya ākārasya vastu svarūpasya vyavasthāpakaḥ anyathā nīla pratibhāsaḥ pītasya vyavasthāpakaḥ syāt iti na vastu vyavashtā syāt 
TBV_5.13	 tasmāt na kalpanā ullikhyamāna vapuḥ api anayavī bahis asti kevalam anādiḥ ayam eka vyavahāraḥ mithyā arthaḥ na ca vyavahāra mātrāt bahis ekam vastu sidhyati nīla ādīnām svabhāvaḥ iti atra api vyavahāra abhedāt eka tā prāpteḥ svabhāvasya atha tatra pratinīla ādi svabhāvam darśana bhedāt ekatvam bādhyate iha api tarhi bahī rūpasya ūrdhva adhas madhya ādi nirbhāsasya bhedāt eka tā tanu ādīnām pratidalatu tat na avayavi rūpaḥ bāhyaḥ arthaḥ asti 
TBV_5.14	 atha āvayinaḥ abhāve tad avayavānām api pāṇi ādīnām diś bheda ādi viruddha dharma adhyāsāt bhedaḥ tad avayavānām api aṅguli ādīnām tatas eva bhedāt tāvat bhedaḥ yāvat paramāṇavaḥ teṣām ca sthūla pratibhāsa viṣaya tva anupapattiḥ stūla tanuḥ ca bahis nīla ādi rūpaḥ pratibhāsaḥ sphuṭam udbhāti na ca sthūla rūpam pratyekam paramāṇuṣu sambhavati tathā tve parama aṇu tva ayogāt na api samuditeṣu sthūla rūpa sambhavah samudita avasthāyām api aṇūnām svarūpeṇa sūkṣmāt na ca tad vyatiriktaḥ samudāyaḥ asti tathā tve dravya vāda prasaṅgāt tatra ca uktaḥ doṣaḥ tat na sthūla tā paramāṇuṣu kathañcid api sambhavati na ca anyādṛś nirbhāsaḥ anyāt ṛkṣasya arthasya prakāśakaḥ nīla darśanasya api pīta vyavasthāpakatva āpatteḥ tathā ca niyata viṣāya vyavasthā ucchedaḥ kiñca paramāṇoḥ api nānā ādiś sambandhāt ekatā na upapannā eva tathā ca āha 
TBV_5.15–5.17	 ṣaṭkena yugapad yogāt paramāṇoḥ ṣaṣ aṃśa tā iti punar tad aṃśānām api nānā ādiś sambandhāt sāṃśata āpattiḥ tathā ca anavasthā tasmāt na paramāṇūnām api sattvam iti avayavi agrahaṇe sarva agrahaṇa prasaṅga iti pratibhāsā bhāva āpatteḥ na prasaṅga sādhanasya avakāśaḥ asat etat avayavi abhāve api nirantara utpannānām ghaṭa ādi ākāreṇa pramāṇūnam sadbhāvāt tad grāhakāṇām api jñāna paramāṇūnām tathā utpannānām tad grāhaka tvāt na bahis artha abhāvaḥ na api tad pratibhāsā bhāvaḥ iti katham prasaṅgasāt bhavasya na avakāśaḥ sthūla eka rūpa avayavi abhāve api yadi ca avayavinaḥ abhāve paramāṇūnām api abhāva prasakteḥ pratibhāsā bhāvena prasaṅga sādhana anavakāśaḥ pratipādyeta tadā sutarām paramāṇu rūpasya jñāna rūpasya ca arthasya abhāvi kāryatva ādi lakṣanasya hetoḥ āśraya asiddha tā doṣaḥ 
TBV_5.18	 bāhya arthanyena ca asmābhiḥ āśraya asiddha tā doṣāt kāryatva lakṣaṇāt dhetoḥ na īśvara siddhiḥ iti pratipādayitum abhipretam yadi punar vijñāna śūnya vāda anukūlam bhavatā api anuṣṭhīyate tadā sādhya dṛṣṭānta dharmi sādhya sādhana dharma ādīnām anumiti aṅga bhūtānām sarveṣām api asiddheḥ kutas upavyasta prayogāt īśvara siddhiḥ tat evam tanu ādi lakṣaṇasya kāryatva ādi hetu āśrayasya avayavinaḥ asiddheḥ āśraya asiddhaḥ hetuḥ 
TBV_5.19^1	 tathā buddhimat kāraṇam iti sādhya nirdeśe buddhimat iti matu barthasya sādhya dharma viśeṣaṇasya anupapattiḥ tat jñānasya tatas vyatireke akārya tve ca tasya iti sambandha anupapatteḥ tad guṇa tvāt tat tasya iti ced na akārya tve vyatireke ca tasya eva tad guṇaḥ na ākāśa ādeḥ iti vyavasthāpayitum aśakteḥ samavāyaḥ vyavasthā kārī iti ced na tasya api tābhyām artha antara tve saḥ eva doṣaḥ vyatireke samavāyasya api sarvatra anuśeṣāt na tatas api tad vyavasthā atha īśvara ātma kārya tvāt īśvara ātma guṇaḥ tat jñānam kutas etat tasmin sati bhāvāt iti ced ākāśa ādau api sati tasya bhāvāt tad kāryatā kim na syāt atha tad bhāve abhāvāt tad kāya tvam tat na nitya vyāpi tvābhyām tasya tad ayogāt tad ātmani utkalitasya tasya darśanāt tat kāryatā iti kim idam tasya tatra utkalita tvam 
TBV_5.19^2	 tatra samaveta tvam tasya iti ced nanu idam eva pṛṣṭam kim idam samaveta tvam nāma tatra samavāyena varttanam iti ced nanu kim vyāptyā samavāyena tatra varttanam āhosvit avyāptyā yadi vyāptyā tadā asmad ādi jñāna vailakṣaṇyam yathā tad jñānasya adṛṣṭasya api kalpyate tathā ākṛṣṭa utpattiṣu vane vanaspati ādiṣu ghaṭa ādau karma kartṛ karaṇa nirvartyam kāryatvam upalabdham api cetana kartṛ rahitam api bhaviṣyati iti kāryatva lakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ buddhimat kāraṇa pūrvaka tve sādhye sthāvaraiḥ vyabhicāri iti lābham icchataḥ mūla kṣatiḥ āyāta iti atha avyāptyā tat tatra vartate tadā deśa antara utpattimatsu tanu ādiṣu tasya āsannidhāne api yathā vyāpāraḥ tathā adṛṣṭasya api agni ādi deśeṣu asannihitasya api ūrdhva jvalana ādi viṣayaḥ vyāpāraḥ bhaviṣyati iti 
TBV_5.20–5.22	 agneḥ ūrdhva jvalanam vāyoḥ tiryak pavanam aṇumanasoḥ ca ādyam karma adṛṣṭa kāritam iti anena sūtreṇa sarva gata ātma sādhaka hetu sūcanam yat kṛtam tat asaṅgatam syāt jñāna ādi viśiṣṭa guṇavat adṛṣṭa guṇasya tatra asat nihitasya api agni ādi ūrdhva jvalana ādi kāryeṣu vyāpāra sambhavāt na ca sāmānya guṇa viśeṣa guṇa tva lakṣaṇaḥ api viśeṣaḥ guṇa guṇinoḥ bhede sambhavati kim ca samavāyasya sarvatra aviśeṣe tatra eva tena varttanam na anyatra iti kutas ayam vibhāgaḥ atha tatra ādheya tvam samaveta tvam tadā ātma vat gagana ādeḥ api sarva gata tve tad ātmani eva tad ādheya tvam na anyatra iti durlabhaḥ ayam vibhāgaḥ tatas tad jñānasya tadā ātmanaḥ vyatireke tasya eva tat jñānam iti sambandha anupapattiḥ atha tatas tat jñānasya bhede api sambandhasya samavāya rūpasya bhāvān na ayam doṣaḥ asat etat samavāyasya anupapatteḥ 
TBV_6.1	 tathā hi kim satām samavāya āhosvit asatām iti tatra yadi asatām iti pakṣaḥ sa na yuktaḥ śaśa viṣāṇa vyoma utpala ādīnām api tad prasaṅgāt atha atyanta asattvāt teṣām na tad prasaṅgaḥ nanu tad ātma tajjñānayoḥ atyanta asattva abhāvaḥ kutas tad samavāyāt iti ced itaretara āśraya tvam siddhe tad samavāye tayoḥ atyanta asattva abhāvaḥ tad abhāvāt ca tad samavāyaḥ iti vaktam itaretara āśraya tvam atha sattām samavāyaḥ nanu teṣām samavāyāt prāk kutas sattvam yadi apara samavāyāt tat asat tasya eka tva abhyupagamāt aneka tve api yadi apara samavāyāt prak teṣām sattvam tad samavāyāt api prāc apara samavāyāt teṣām sattvam abhyupagantavyam iti anavasthā atha samavāyāt prāk teṣām svatas eva sattvam iti na anavasthā tarhi samavāya vyatirekeṇa api sattva abhyupagame vyartham samavāya parikalpanam iti sattā sambandhdāt padārthānām sattā iti ucyamānam na śobhām āvahati 
TBV_6.2^1	 atha samavāyāt prāk padārthānām sattvam na api asattvam sattā samavāyaḥ sattvam asat etat yatas yadi tad samavāyāt prāk padārthāḥ yogi jñānam api na janyanti tadā katham teṣām na asattvam atha tat janayanti tadā katham teṣām na sattvam kim ca anyonya vyavaccheda rūpām eka niṣedhasya apara sadbhāvana āntarīyaka tvāt katham asattva niṣedhe na sattva vidhānam tad vidhāne vā katham na asattva niṣedhaḥ iti ayuktam uktam udyota kareṇa go tva sambandhāt prāk na gauḥ na api agauḥ go tva yogāt gauḥ iti api ca samavāyāt yadi padārthānām sattvam samavāyasya kutas sattvam iti vaktavyam 
TBV_6.2^2	 yadi apara samavāyāt anavasthā atha svatas eva samavāyasya sattvam padārthānām api tat svatas eva astu punar api vyartham sattā samavāya kalpanam atha yadi nāma samavāyasya svatas sattvam iti rūpam katham anya padārthānām api tat eva rūpam iti sacetasā vaktum yuktam na hi lavaṇasya svatas lavaṇa tve sūpa ādeḥ api tad vyatirekeṇa tat bhavati asat etat yatas adhyakṣataḥ siddhe padārtha svabhāve yujyeta tat vaktum na ca samavāya ādeḥ svarūpataḥ sattvam anya padārthānām tu tad sadbhāvāt sattvam iti adhyakṣāt siddham 
TBV_6.3	 api ca ayam samavāyaḥ kim samavāyinoḥ parikalpyate uta asamavāyinoḥ iti vikalpa dvayam tatra yadi asamavāyinoḥ iti pakṣaḥ sa na yuktaḥ ghaṭa paṭayoḥ atyanta bhinnayoḥ tad prasaṅgāt na ca asamavāyinoḥ bhinna samavāyena samavāyi tvam tat abhinnam vidhātum śakyam viruddha dharma adhyāsena tābhyām tasya bheda prasaṅgāt na api bhinnam tad bhinna samavāyi tva karaṇe punar api tayoḥ asamavāyi tvam anyonya upakāra karaṇe tu anavasthā svatas eva tu samavāyinoḥ kim samavāyena tad hetunā parikalpitena atha samavāyena tayoḥ tad vyavahāraḥ kriyate nanu yadi samavāyinoḥ svarūpam pratyakṣa ādi pramāṇa gocaraḥ tadā tata eva tad vyavahārasya api siddheḥ vyartham eva tad artham tad parikalpitam 
TBV_6.4–6.5^1	 atha pratyakṣa pramāṇa siddha tvāt samavāyasya evam vikalpanam ayuktam yadi hi tad siddha tvam tasya syāt tadā yuktam etat na ca pratyakṣa pramāṇe tad svarūpa avabhāsaḥ na hi tad ātmā jñānam tad samavāyaḥ ca iti tritayam indriya jādhyakṣa gocaraḥ na api sva saṃvedana adhyakṣa viṣayaḥ tasya bhavatā anabhyupagamāt na api eka artha samavetā anantara manaḥ adhyakṣa viṣayah tasya prāk eva niṣiddha tvāt na ca bāhyeṣu api ghaṭa rūpa ādiṣu artheṣu ayam ghaṭah ete ca tad samavetāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ ayam ca tad antarāla varttī bhinnaḥ samavāyaḥ iti tritayam adhyakṣa pratītau vibhinna svarūpam pratibhāti tad pratibhāne vā dravya guṇa samavāyānām adhyadkṣa siddha tvāt vibhinna svarūpa tayā na guṇa guṇi bhāve samavāye vā kasyacid vivādaḥ syāt na api ekatva vibhramaḥ ghaṭa rūpa ādīnām tatas ca tad nirākaraṇa artham śāstra praṇayanam apārthakam syāt 
TBV_6.5^2	 nanu yathā pratyakṣeṇa pratipanne api anekānte jainena sva lakṣaṇe vā bauddhena sva durāgam āhita vāsanā balāt lokasyaḥ tena tad apratipanna tā vibhramaḥ tad nirākaraṇa artham ca śāstra praṇayanam tathā atra api syāt iti tarhi tathāvidha śāstra rahitānām abalā bāla ādīnām na samavāya pratyakṣatā vibhramaḥ iti teṣām śuklaḥ paṭaḥ iti pratītiḥ na syāt api tu ayam paṭaḥ ete śukla ādayaḥ guṇāḥ ayam ca tad antarāla varttī aparaḥ samavāyaḥ iti prtītiḥ syāt 
TBV_6.5^3	 atra samavāyasya sūkṣma tvāt pratyakṣa tve api anupalakṣaṇāt tatrastha tvena rūpa ādīnām upacārāt śuklaḥ paṭaḥ iti pratipattiḥ syāt na etat evam daṇḍe api puruṣaḥ iti pratipattiḥ syāt upacārāt ca iyam pratipattuḥ upajāyamānā skhalat rūpā syāt vāhīke go buddhi vat na ca samavetam idam vastu atra iti pratipattau viśeṣaṇa bhūtaḥ samavāyaḥ pratibhāti iti vaktum yuktam bahiṣpratibhā samāna rūpa ādi vyatirekeṇa antar ca abhijalpam antareṇa aparasya varṇa ākṛti akṣara ākāra śūnyasya grāhya ākāra tām vibhrāṇasya bahis samavāya svarūpasya apratibhāsanāt varṇa ādi ākāra rahitam ca paraiḥ samavāya sva rūpam abhyupagamyate na ca tad kalpanā buddhau api pratibhāti na ca anyadṛśaḥ pratibhāsaḥ anyāt ṛkṣasya arthasya vyavasthāpakaḥ atiprasaṅgāt tat na samavāyaḥ adhyakṣa pramāṇa gocaraḥ 
TBV_6.6	 yaḥ tu āha nitya anumeya tvāt samavāyasya anumāna gocara tā tena ayam adoṣaḥ iti tat ca anumānam iha tantuṣu paṭaḥ iti buddhiḥ tantu paṭa vyatirikta sambandha pūrvikā iha iti buddhi tvāt iha kaṃsa pātryām jala buddhi vat iti etat saḥ api ayukta vādī samavāyasya anyasya vā padārthasya nitya eka rūpasya kāraṇatva asambhavāt kvacid api iti pratipādayiṣyamāna tvāt na ca tantuṣu paṭaḥ śṛṅge gauḥ śādhāyām vṛkṣaḥ iti laukikī pratītiḥ asti paṭe tantavaḥ gaviśṛṅgam vṛkṣe śākhāḥ iti ākāreṇa prati iti utpatteḥ saṃvedanāt tasyāḥ ca samavāya nibandhana tve tantu ādīnām paṭa ādi ārabdha tva prasaṅgaḥ 
TBV_6.7	 kim ca samavāyasya samavāyibhiḥ anabhisambandhe tasya tatra sambaddha buddhi jananam teṣām sambandhaḥ eva ca iti ca na yuktam na hi daṇḍa puruṣayoḥ saṃyogaḥ sahya vindhyābhyām anabhisambandhyamānaḥ tatra sambandha buddhi hetuḥ tad sambandhaḥ vā taiḥ tad abhisambandhe vā svatas dravya guṇa karmaṇām sva ādhāraiḥ svatas sambandhaḥ kim na syāt yatas samavāya parikalpana ānarthakyam aśnuvīta iha samavāyiṣu samavāyaḥ iti ca buddhiḥ aparinimittikā prakṛtasya hetoḥ anaikāntika tvam katham na sādhayet svatas tad sambandha abhyupaganme samavāya antareṇa tasya tad abhisambandhe anavasthālatā gagana tala avalambinī prasajyeta viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāva lakṣaṇa sambandha balāt tasya tad abhisambandhe tasya api taiḥ sambandhaḥ apara viśeṣana viśeṣya bhāva lakṣaṇa sambandha balāt yadi sā eva anavasthā samavāya balāt tasya tad sambandhe vyaktam itaretara āśraya tvam svatas taiḥ tasya abhisambandhe buddhi ādīnām api svatas eva sva ādhāraiḥ sambandhaḥ bhaviṣyati iti āstām tāvat 
TBV_6.8–6.9	 tat evam buddheḥ tad ātmanaḥ vyatireke sambandha asiddheḥ matu bartha anupapattiḥ atha avyatiriktā tad ātmanaḥ tad buddhiḥ tathā api tad anupapattiḥ na hi tat eva tena eva tadvat bhavati kim ca tad ātmanaḥ tad buddheḥ avyatireke yadi tad ātmani tad buddheḥ anupraveśaḥ tadā buddheḥ abhāvāt buddhi vikalaḥ gagana ādi vat jaḍa sva srūpaḥ tad ātmā katham jagat sṛṣṭā syāt buddhi ādi viśeṣa guṇa gaṇa vaikalye ca tadā ātmanaḥ asmad ādi a ātmanaḥ api ātma tvena tad vaikalyāt mukta ātmanaḥ iva saṃsāri tvam na syāt navānām viśeṣa guṇānām ātyantika kṣaya upetasya ātmanaḥ mukta tva abhyupagamāt tasya ca asmad ādi ātmasu api samāna tvāt bhavat abhyupagamena 
TBV_6.10	 atha ātma tva aviśeṣe api tad ātmā asmad ādya ātmabhyaḥ viśiṣṭaḥ abhyupagamyate tarhi kāryatva aviśeṣe api ghaṭa ādi kāryebhyaḥ sthāvara ādi kāryam akartṛka tvena viśiṣṭam kim na abhyupaganyate tathā ca na kāryatva ādi lakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ anupalabhyamāna kartṛkaiḥ sthāvara ādibhiḥ avyabicārī syāt atha tad buddhau tadā ātmanaḥ anupraveśaḥ tadā buddhi mātram ādhāra śūnyam abhyupagantavyam abhāti tathā ca asmad ādi buddheḥ api tadvat ādhāra vikala tvena matu bartha asambhavāt ghaṭa ādau api buddhimat kāraṇa tvasya asiddha tvāt sādhya vikalaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ atha asmad ādi buddhibhyaḥ buddhi tve samāne api tad buddheḥ eva anāśrita tva lakṣaṇaḥ viśeṣaḥ abhyupagamyate tarhi ghaṭa ādi kāryebhyaḥ pṛthivī ādi kāryasya kāryatve samāne api akartṛ pūrvakatva lakṣaṇaḥ viśeṣaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ iti punar api kāryatva lakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ taiḥ eva vyabhicārī 
TBV_6.11	 kim ca asau tad buddhiḥ kṣaṇikāḥ akṣaṇikāḥ vā iti vaktavyam yadi kṣaṇikā iti pakṣah tadā ātmānam samavāyi kāraṇam ātma manaḥ saṃyogam ca asamavāyi kāraṇam tad śarīra ādikam ca nimitta kāraṇam antareṇa katham dvitīya kṣaṇe tasyāḥ utpattiḥ tad anutpattau ca acetanasya aṇvādeḥ cetanā anadhiṣṭhitasya katham bhūdhara ādi kārya karaṇe pravṛttiḥ vā asya ādeḥ iva acetanasya cetanā anadhiṣṭhitasya pravṛtti anabhyupagamāt tatas ca idānīm bhūruha ādīnām anutpatti prasaṅgāt kārya śūnyam jagat syāt atha samavāyi ādi kāraṇam antareṇa api tad buddheḥ asmad ādi buddhi vailakṣaṇyāt utpattiḥ abhyupagamyate nanu evam ghaṭa ādi kārya vailakṣaṇyam bhūdhara ādi kāryasya kim na abhyupagamyate iti tat eva codyam kim ca yad i īśa bhuddhiḥ samavāyi ādi kāraṇa nirapekṣā eva utpattim āsādayati tarhi muktānām api ānanda ādikam śarīra ādi nimitta kāraṇa ādi vyatirekeṇa api utpatsyate iti na buddhi sukha ādi vikalam jaḍa ātma svarūpam muktiḥ syāt
