TBV_6.12^1	 atha akṣaṇikā tad buddhiḥ nanu evam asmad ādi buddhiḥ api akṣaṇikā kim na abhyupagamyate atha pratyakṣa ādi pramāṇa virodhāt na asmad ādi buddhiḥ akṣanikā tarhi tad virodhāt eva adṛṣṭa utpattiṣu sthāvareṣu kārya tvam buddhimat kāraṇa pūrvakam na abhyupagantavyam atha asmad ādi buddheḥ kṣaṇika tva sādhakam anumānam akṣaṇika tva abhyupagama bādhakam pravartate na punar adṛṣṭa utpattiṣu sthāvareṣu kim punar tad anumānam atha kṣaṇikā buddhiḥ asmad ādi pratyakṣa tve sati vibhu dravya viśeṣa guṇa tvāt śabda vat iti etat nanu yathā asya anumānasya asmad ādi buddhi akṣa nika tva abhyupagama bādhakasya sambhavaḥ tathā adṛṣṭa utpattiṣu sthāvareṣu kartṛ pūrvaka tva abhyupagama bādhakasya tasya sambhavaḥ pratipādayiṣyate iti na atra vastuni bhavatā autsukyam āstheyam 
TBV_6.12^2	 yathā ca buddhi kṣaṇika tva anumānasya aneka doṣa duṣṭa tvam tathā śabdasya paudgalika tva vicāraṇāyām pratipādayiṣyate iti etat api āstām tāvat yathā vā buddhi tva aviśeṣe api īśa asmad ādi buddhyoḥ ayam aksaṇika tva kṣaṇika tva lakṣaṇaḥ viśeṣas tathā bhūruha ghaṭa ādi kāryayoḥ api akartṛ kartṛ pūrvakatva lakṣanaḥ viśeṣah kim na abhyupagamyate iti punar api tat eva dūṣaṇam kārya tva ādeḥ hetoḥ anaikānitka tva lakṣaṇam prakṛta sādhye tat evam buddhimat kāraṇa pūrvakatva lakṣaṇe sādhye matu bartha asambhavāt tanu ādīnām anekadhā pramāṇa vādha asambhavāt ca śāstra vyākhyāna ādi liṅga anumīyamāna pāṇḍitya guṇasya devadattasya iva mūrkha tva lakṣaṇi sādhye anumāna bādhita karma nirdeśa anantara prayuktasya kārya tva ādeḥ hetoḥ kāla atyaya apadiṣṭa tvena tad putra tva ādeḥ iva āgamaka tvam anumāna bādhita tvam vā pakṣasya iti sthitam 
TBV_6.13	 tathā kāryatvāt iti hetuḥ api asiddhaḥ tathā hi kim idam tanu ādīnām kāryatvam prāk asataḥ sva kāraṇa samavāyaḥ sattā samavāyaḥ vā iti ced kutas prāk iti kāraṇa samavāyāt iti ced nanu tad samavāya samaye prāk iva sva rūpa sattva vaidhuḥ ye prāk iti viśeṣaṇam anarthakam sati sambhave vyabhicāre ca viśeṣaṇam upādīyamānam arthavat bhavati atra tu vyabhicāraḥ eva na sambhavaḥ tathā hi yadi kāraṇa samavāya samaye svarūpiṇa sat bhavati tanu ādi tadā tad kāle iva tasya prāk api sattve kāryatvam na syāt iti viśeṣaṇam upādīyate prāk asataḥ iti yadā punar prāk iva kāraṇa samavāya velāyām api svarūpa sattavikalatā tadā prāk iti viśeṣaṇam na kañcid artham puṣṇāti asataḥ iti eva astu 
TBV_6.14	 na ca asataḥ kāraṇa samavāyaḥ api yuktaḥ śaśa viṣāṇa ādeḥ api tad prasaṅgāt tasya kāraṇa virahān na tad prasaṅgaḥ iti ced kutas etat asattvāt tanu karaṇa ādeḥ api tadvat asattve kim kṛtaḥ ayam vibhāgaḥ asya kāraṇam asti na śaśaśṛṅga ādeḥ iti tanu ādeḥ kāraṇam upalabhyate na itarasya iti api na uttaram yatas kārya kāraṇayoḥ upalambhe sati etat syāt idam asya kāraṇam kāryam ca idam asya iti 
TBV_6.15	 na ca parasya tad upalambhaḥ pratyakṣataḥ upalambha kāraṇam upalambha viṣayaḥ iti naiyāyikānām matam arthavat pramāṇam iti atra bhāṣye pramātṛ prameyābhyām artha antaram avyapadeśya avyabhicāri vyavasāya ātmaka jñāne kartavye arthaḥ sahakārī vidyate yasya tas arthavat pramāṇam iti vyākhyānāt na ca ajanakam sahakāri saha karoti iti sahahakāri iti vyutpatteḥ na ca asat śaśa viṣāṇa samam jñānasya anyasya vā kāraṇam virodhāt api ca indriya artha sannikarṣāt pratyakṣam jñānam utpattimat kārya kāraṇa ādinā ca indriya sannikarṣaḥ saṃyogaḥ saḥ api katham tena asatā janyate iti cintyam samyoga abhāve ca rūpa ādinā indriyasya saṃyukta samavāyaḥ rūpa tva ādinā tu saṃyukta samaveta samavāyaḥ iti sarvam durghaṭām etena dravya tva ādi sāmānya sambandhaḥ api tasya nirūpitaḥ tat na tanu ādi viṣayam adhyakṣam atas eva na anumānam api tat evam khara viṣa an a ādi vat kārya kāraṇa ādeḥ anupalambhāt na yuktam etat śarīra ādeḥ kāraṇam asti na śaśaśṛṅga ādeḥ iti 
TBV_6.16^1	 yadi punar tanu karaṇa ādiḥ san vandhyā suta ādi parihāreṇa iti matiḥ tatra kutas saḥ eva san kāraṇa samavāyāt saḥ api kutas sattvāt anyonya saṃśrayaḥ tad samavāyāt sattvam atas ca tad samavāyaḥ iti prāc asataḥ sattā samavāyāt saḥ eva san iti ced kutas prāk sattā samavāyāt nanu tad samavāya kāle prāk iva svarūpa sattva virahe prāk iti viśeṣaṇam anarthakam ityādi sarvam vaktavyam asataḥ ca sattā samavāye kharaśṛṅga ādeḥ api sambhavet aviśeṣāt prāk iti ca viśeṣaṇam śaśaśṛṛṅga ādi vyavaccheda artham pareṇa uktam sattā sambandha samaye ca tanu ādeḥ sva rūpa sattva abhāve kaḥ tatas viśeṣaḥ 
TBV_6.16^2	 ayam asti viśeṣaḥ kūrma roma ādikam atyanta asat itarat punar svayam na sat na api asat atas eva sattā sambhandāt tat eva sat iti ucyate iti tat etat jaḍa ātmanaḥ bhavataḥ kaḥ anyaḥ bhāṣate tathā hi na sat iti vacanāt tasya sattā sambandhāt prāc abhāvaḥ uktaḥ sat pratiṣedha lakṣaṇa tvāt asya na api asat iti abhidhānāt bhāvaḥ asattva niṣedha rūpa tvāt bhāvasya rūpa antara abhāvāt tathā eva vaiyākaraṇānam nyāyaḥ dvau pratiṣedhau prakṛtam artham gamyataḥ iti katham anyathā na idam nirātmakam jīvat śarīram prāṇa ādimattvāt iti atra nairātmya niṣedhaḥ sa ātmakaḥ sidhyet 
TBV_6.17	 atra kecid bruvate na evam prayogaḥ kriyate api tu sa ātmakam jīvat śarīram prāṇa ādimattvāt iti taiḥ api evam prayogam kurvadbhiḥ sa ātmaka tva abhāvaḥ niyamena prāṇa ādi mattva abhāvena vyāptaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ anyathā vyabhicāra āśaṅkā na nirvarteta tad abhyupagame ca idam avaśyam vaktavyam jīvat śarīre prāṇa ādimat tvam pratīyamānam svāhāvam nivartayati sa ca nivartamānaḥ sva vyāpyam sa ātmaka tva abhāvam ādāya nivartate itarathā tena asau vyāptaḥ na syāt yasmin nivartamāne yat na nivartate na tena tat vyāptam yathā nivartamāne api pradīpe anivartamānaḥ paṭa ādiḥ na tena vyāptaḥ na nivartate ca prāna ādi mattva abhāve nivartamāne api sa ātmaka tva abhāvaḥ iti nivartate iti ced tad nivṛttau api yadi sa ātmaka tvam na sidhyati na tarhi tad abhāvaḥ nivartate sa ātmaka tva abhāva abhāve api tad abhāvasya tad avastha tvāt sidhyati iti ced āyātam idam dhvau pratiṣidhau prakṛtam artham gamayataḥ iti tathā ca idam api yuktam na idam nirātmakam jīvat śarīram prāṇa ādimattvāt iti 
TBV_6.18	 anye tu manyante anyatra dṛṣṭaḥ dharmaḥ kvacid dharmiṇi vidhīyate niṣidhyate ca iti vacanāt kevalam ghaṭa ādau nairātmyam aprāṇa ādimattvena vyāptam dṛṣṭam tat eva niṣidhyate jīvat śarīre api prāṇa ādi mattva abhāvena na punar sa ātmaka tvam vidhīyate tasya anyatra adarśanāt iti teṣām ghaṭāsau nairātmyam pratipannam pratiṣidhyate iti bhavatu sūktam tathā api tad niṣedha sāmarthyāt yadi jīvat śarīre sa ātmaka tvam na syāt na tarhi tatra tad niṣedhaḥ yadā hi nairātmyam iti aparaḥ tad niṣedhaḥ mṛgyaḥ tathā ca sati anavasthānāt na nairātmya niṣedhaḥ kim ca yadi nāma ghaṭa ādau nairātmyam upalabdham kim iti anyatra niṣidhyate itarathāḥ devadatte pāṇḍityam upalabdham yajñadatta ādau niṣidhyeta tatra prāṇa ādimattva darśanāt iti ced yuktam etat yadi prāṇdimat tvam nairātmya viruddham syāt agniḥ iva śīta viruddhaḥ na ca evam anyathā sarvam aśoea viruddham bhavet prāṇa ādimattvena svābhāvaḥ nairātmya vyāpakaḥ viruddhaḥ 
TBV_6.19	 tatas prāṇa ādi mattva bhāvāt tad abhāvaḥ nivartate vahni bhāvāt iva śītam sa ca nivartamānaḥ sva vyāpyam nairātmyam ādāya nivartate yathā dhūma abhāvaḥ pāvaka abhāvam iti dattam atra uttaram yadi nairātmya abhāvaḥ sa ātmakaḥ na bhavet tad avastham nairātmyam iti bhavatu tarhi nairātmya niṣedhaḥ sa ātmakaḥ tathā sati sattā sambandhāt prāk tanu ādiḥ nā sat iti vacanāt tadā tasya sattvam uktam na sat iti abhidhānāt asattvam iti virodhaḥ tatas asat eva tat abhyupagantavyam iti na vandhyā suta ādeḥ tanu karaṇa ādeḥ viśeṣaḥ bhavatu evam tathā api tanu ādeḥ eva sattā sambandhāt sattvam na khara śṛṅga ādeḥ tathā adarśanāt iti ced uktam atra tathā adarśana upāya abhāvāt iti 
TBV_7.1^1	 api ca sattā api yadi asatī katham tatas vandhyā suta ādeḥ iva aparasya sattvam satī ced yadi anya sattātaḥ anavasthā svatas ced padārthānām api svatas eva sattvam syāt iti vyartham tad parikalpanam kiñca yadi svatas eva sattā satī upeyate tadā pramānam vaktavyam atha svatas sattā satī tad sambandhāt tanu ādīnām sattvāni atha anupapatteḥ tarhi anyonya saṃśrayaḥ tad sambandhāt tanu ādi sattve siddhe sattā sattva siddhiḥ tatas tad sambandhāt tanu ādi sattva siddhiḥ iti vyaktam itaretara āśraya tvam atha sattā svatas satī sat abhidhāna pratyaya viṣaya tvāt avāntara sāmānya ādi vat na dravya ādinaḥ vyabhicāraḥ dravya ādiḥ api sat dravyam san guṇaḥ sat karma iti evam sat abhidhāna pratyaya viṣayaḥ bhavati na ca asau pareṇa svatas san abhyupagataḥ sattā prakalpana vaiphalya prasaṅgāt na ca dravya ādau tad viṣaya tvam para apekṣam na sattāyām iti vaktum yuktam tasyām api tad apekṣa tva sambhavāt 
TBV_7.1^2	 atha tatra tasya tad apekṣa tve kim tad aparam iti vaktavyam nanu etat dravya ādau api samānam tatra sattā iti ced atra api dravya ādikam iti tulyam yathā eva hi sattā sambandhāt dravya ādikam sat na svatas tathā dravya ādi svarūpa sattva sambandhāt sattā satī na svatas dravya ādeḥ svarūpa sattvam na asti tena ayam adoṣaḥ tad astitve koḥ doṣaḥ iti vācyam nanu tasya svatas sattve avāntara sāmānya abhāva prasaṅgaḥ doṣaḥ nanu svatas asattve khara viṣāṇa ādeḥ iva sutarām tad abhāva doṣaḥ api ca yaḥ hi tatra sattā sambandham na icchati sa katham avāntara sāmānya sambandham icced na ca atra pramāṇam svatas asantaḥ dravya ādayaḥ nāva antara sāmānyam iti atha etat dravya ādayaḥ na svatas santaḥ avāntara sāmānyavat tvāt yat punar svatas sat na tat avāntara sāmānya vat yathā sāmānya viśeṣa samavāyāḥ iti vyatirekī hetuḥ na etat yadi hi dravya ādayaḥ dharmiṇaḥ kutaścid pratīti gocara cāriṇet santaḥ bhavanti sa katham avāntara sāmānya sambandham icchet 
TBV_7.1^3	 na ca atra pramāṇam svatas asantaḥ dravya ādayaḥ nāva antara sāmānyam iti atha etat dravya ādayaḥ na svatas santaḥ avāntara sāmānyavat tvāt yat punar svatas sat na tat avāntara sāmānya vat yathā sāmānya pratītiḥ sattvam sādhayantī svatas iti pratijñām tat asattva viṣaya ābādhane ced cāriṇaḥ santaḥ bhavanti tadā katham na tad pratītiḥ svatas sattvam sādhayantī na svatas santaḥ te iti pratijñām tad asattva viṣayām bādhate na ced matra uttaram na svatas santaḥ te pratīti viṣayāḥ kintu sattā sambandhāt iti yatas na svayam asantaḥ tad sambandhāt tad viṣayāḥ bhavanti iti uktam kim ca dravya ādeḥ ekāntena yasya bhinnāni avāntara sāmānyāni katham tasya tāni syuḥ yatas avāntara sāmānyavat tvāt iti hetuḥ siddhaḥ syāt atha tathā api tasya iti na parasparam api syuḥ iti sāmānya samavāyāt pariśeṣa vat sāmānya samavāya viśeṣa vat iti vaidharmya nidarśanam ayuktam 
TBV_7.1^4	 yadi matam dravya ādau tāni samavetāni tatas tasya tāni na sāmānya ādeḥ viparyayāt iti tat na samyak tatra samavetāni iti samavāyena sambaddhāni iti yadi arthaḥ sa na yuktaḥ samavāyasya niṣiddha tvāt niṣetsyamāna tvāt ca bhavatu vā samavāyaḥ tathā api yatra dravye guṇe karmaṇi ca dravya tvam guṇa tvam karma tvam ca avāntara sāmānyam tatra eva pṛthivī tva ādīni rūpa tva ādīni gamana tva ādīni ca tathāvidhāni sāmānyāni samavāyaḥ api tatra eva sāmānya vat tasya sarva gata tvāt ca dravya ādi vat anyonya sattāni iti na dravya ādeḥ svatas sattva bādhanam iti āśaṅkā na nivartate kim dravya ādi sambandhāt sattā satī kim vā tayā dravya ādikam sat iti tat na sattātaḥ tanu ādeḥ sattvam tasyāḥ eva asiddha tvāt 
TBV_7.2^1	 sattā pratyakṣa ādi pramāṇa siddha tvāt sattāyāḥ pratyakṣa bādhita viṣaya tvena evam upanyasyamānasya prasaṅga sādhanasya anavakāśaḥ na ca dravaya pratibhāsa velāyām pratyakṣa buddhau parisphuṭa rūpeṇa vyakti vivekena sattā na pratibhāti iti śakyam vaktum anugata ākārasya vyāvṛtta ākārasya ca pratyakṣa anubhavasya saṃvedanāt na ca anugata vyāvṛtta vastu vyatirekeṇa dvi ākārā buddhiḥ ghaṭati na hi viṣaya vyatirekeṇa pratītiḥ utpadyate nīla ādi sva lakṣaṇa pratīteḥ api tathā abhāva prasaṅgāt atha taimirikasya bāhya artha sannidhi vyatirekeṇa api keśoṇḍuka ādi pratītiḥ udeti tathā eva anugata rūpam antareṇa api bhinna vastuṣu anugata ākārā buddhiḥ udeṣyati iti na tatas ssttā vyavasthā tat ayuktam taimirika pratītau hi pratibhāsamānasya keśoṇḍikā ādeḥ bādhaka kāraṇa doṣa parijñānāt atattvam sattā darśane tu na bādhaka pratyaya udayaḥ na api kāraṇa doṣa parijñānam iti na tad grāhiṇaḥ vijñānasya mithyātvam 
TBV_7.2^2	 tathā hi vibhinneṣu api ghaṭa paṭa ādiṣu artheṣu sat sat iti abhedam ullikhantī pradtītiḥ udayam āsādayati na ca asau kāla antara ādau viparyayam upagacchantī lakṣyate sarvadā sarveṣām ghaṭa paṭa ādiṣu sat sat iti vyāhṛteḥ vyavahāram upacāryantī ca pratītiḥ paraiḥ api pramāṇam abhyupagamyate yathā uktam taiḥ prāmāṇyam vyavahāreṇa iti tat evam avastthitam anugata ākārā hi buddhiḥ vyāvṛtta rūpa pratīti anadhigatam sādhāraṇa rūpam ullikhantī su pariniścita rūpā bādhā yogāt pramānam sā ca akṣa anvaya vyatireka anusāritayā pratyakṣam tathā hi visphārita locanasya ghaṭa paṭa ādiṣu rūpam ārūḍhām sattām ullikhantī sat sat iti pratītiḥ tad abhāve ca na bhavati iti tad anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyitayā katham na pratyakṣam tasmāt bahuṣu vyāvṛtteṣu tulya ākārā buddhiḥ eka tām avasyti yat ca atra vibhinneṣu ghaṭa ādiṣu pratiniyatam ekam anugata svarūpam sā eva jātiḥ 
TBV_7.3	 atha vyakti riktā jātiḥ upeyate na ca vyakti darśana velāyām tad rūpa saṃsparśa viṣaya vyatirikta vapuḥ aparam anugati rūpam pratibhāti tat katham tat sāmānyam na etat asti yasmāt agṛhīta saṅketasya api tanubhṛtaḥ prathamam udbhāti vastu dvitīye tulya rūpa tām anusarati buddhiḥ kvacid eva na sarvatra pratipatti anya tā ca sarvatra bheda vyavahāra nibandhanam tulya deśa kālaḥ api rūpa rasa ādau ca pratipatti anya tā jātau api vidyate iti katham na sā bhinnā asti tathā hi vyakti ākāra vivekena viśadam anugati rūpa tā bhāti tad vivekena ca vyāvṛtta rūpa tā iti katham vyakti svarūpāt bhinna avabhāsinī jātiḥ bhinnāḥ nābhyupagama viṣayaḥ 
TBV_7.4	 atha eka indriya avaseya tvāt jāti vyaktyoḥ eka tā rūpa rasa ādau tu bhinna indriya grāhya tvāt bhedaḥ tat api asaṅgatam yatas eka indriya grāhyam api vāta ātapa ādikam samāna deśam ca bhinnam pratibhāti iti bhinna vapuḥ abhyupeyate tathā pratiniyata indriya viṣayam api jāti vyakti dvayam bhinnam bhinna pratibhāsāt eva tathā hi ghaṭam antareṇa api paṭa grahaṇe sat sat iti pūrva pratipannā sattā avagatiḥ dṛṣṭāḥ yadi tu vyaktiḥ eva satī na jātiḥ tad sattve api tat avyatiriktā ca tathā sati vyakti rūpavat tad ananugatiḥ api sarvadā tena eka rūpā eva jātiḥ pratyakṣe tathābhūtāyāḥ eva tasyāḥ pratibhāsanāt śabda liṅgayoḥ api tasyām eva sambandha grahaṇam iti tābhyām api sā pratīyate tat evam pratyakṣa ādi pramāṇa avaseya tvāt sattāyāḥ na tad nirākaraṇāya prasaṅga sādhana anumāna pravṛttiḥ iti 
TBV_7.5–7.6	 asat etat yatas na vyakti darśana velāyām sva rūpeṇa bahis grāhya ākāra tayā pratītim avatarantī jātiḥ udbhāti na hi ghaṭa paṭavaḥ tu dvaya pratibhāsa samaye tadā eva tad vyavasthita mūrtti bhinna abhinnā vā jātiḥ ābhāti tad ākārasya aparasya grāhya tayā bahis tatra apratibhāsanāt bahis grāhya avabhāsaḥ ca bariḥ artha vyavasthā kārī na antara avabhāsaḥ yadi tu saḥ api tad vyavasthā kārī syāt tathā sati hṛdi parivartamāna vapuṣaḥ sukha ādeḥ api pratibhāsāt bahis tad vyavasthā syāt tathā ca sukha asya ātmakāḥ śabda ādayaḥ iti sa aṅkya darśanam eva syāt atha sukha ādiḥ ākāraḥ bāhya rūpa tayā na pratibhāti iti na bahis asau jātiḥ api tarhi na bahīrūpa tayā pratibhāti iti na bahīrūpa abhyupagantavyā yatas kalpanā matiḥ api darśana dṛṣṭam eva ghaṭa ādi rūpam bahis ullikhantī tad giram ca antar pratibhāti 
TBV_7.7^1	 na tu tad vyatirikta vapuṣam jātim uddyotayati tat na tat avaseyā api bahis jātiḥ asti taimirika jāne bahiṣprakāśa māna vapuṣaḥ api hi keṣa uṇḍuka ādayaḥ na tathā abhyupeyante bādhyamāna jñāna viṣaya tvāt jātiḥ tu na bahīrūpa tayā kvacid api jñāne pratibhāti iti katham sā sattva abhyupagama viṣayaḥ buddhiḥ eva kevalam ghaṭa paṭa ādiṣu pratibhāsamāneṣu sat sat iti tulya tanuḥ āabhāti yadi tarhi na bāhyā jātiḥ asti buddiḥ api katham eka rūpā pratibhāti na hi bahis nimittam antareṇa tad ākāra utpattimatī sā yuktāḥ 
TBV_7.7^2	 nanu kena ucyate bahis nimitta nirāpekṣā jāti matiḥ iti kin tu bahis jātiḥ na nimittam iti bāhyāḥ tu vyaktayaḥ kāścid eva jāti buddheḥ nimittam nanu yadi vyakti nibandhana anugata ākārā bahis tathā sati yathā khaṇḍa muṇḍa vyakti darśane gauḥ gauḥ iti pratipattiḥ udeti tathā giri śikhara ādi darśane api gauḥ gauḥ iti etat ākārā pratipattiḥ bhavet vyakti bheda aviśeṣāt tat ayuktam bheda aviśeṣe api khaṇḍa muṇḍa ādi vyaktiṣu gauḥ gauḥ iti ākārā matiḥ udayam āsādayantī samupalabhyate iti tāḥ eva tām upajanayitum samarthāḥ iti avasīyate na punar guru śikhara ādiṣu gauḥ garuḥ iti matiḥ dṛṣṭā iti na te tad nibandhanam 
TBV_7.7^3	 yathā ca āmalakī phala ādiṣu yathā vidhānam upayukteṣu vyādhi virati lakṣaṇam phalam upalabhyate iti tāni eva tad vidhau samarthāni iti avasīyate bheda aviśeṣe api na punar trapuṣa dadhi ādīni atha bhinneṣu api bhāveṣu sat sat iti matiḥ asti vibhinneṣu ca bhāveṣu yat eka tvam tat eva jātiḥ tatra ucyate tat eka tvam ghaṭa paṭa ādiṣu kim anyat uta ananyat na tāvat anyat tasya apratibhāsanāt iti ukte na api ananyat eka rūpa apratibhāsanāt na hi ghaṭasi sa paṭasya buddhiḥ ea tulya ākāra pratibhāsā sat sat iti śabdaḥ ca dṛśyate iti tad anvayaḥ eva yuktaḥ na jāti anvayaḥ tasya adarśanāt na ca buddhi dvarūpam api apara buddhi svarūpam anugacchati iti na tat api sāmānyam iti eva anugata jāti vādaḥ mithyā vādaḥ 
TBV_7.8^1	 api ca aneka vyakti vyāpi sāmānyam tad vādibhiḥ abhyupagamyate na ca tat vyapi tvam tasya kenacid jñānena vyavasthāpayitum śakyam tathā hi sannihita vyakti pratibhāsa kāle jātiḥ tad vyakti saṃsparśinī sphuṭam avabhāti na vyakti antara sambandhi tayā tasya atathā sannidhānena pratibhāsā yogāt tad apratibhāse ca tat miśratā api na avagatā iti katham asan= hita vyakti antara sambaddha śarīrā jātiḥ avabhāti yat eva hi parisphuṭa darśane pratibhāti rūpam tat eva tasyāḥ yuktam darśana asaṃsparśinaḥ svarūpasya asambhavāt sambhave vā tasya dṛśya svabhāvāt bheda prasaṅgāt tat eka tve sarvatra bheda pratihatoḥ anāna ekam jagat syāt 
TBV_7.8^2	 darśana gocara atītam ca vyakti antara sambaddham gāti svarūpam apratibhāsanāt asat pratibhāsane vā tasya tad sambaddhānām vyavahita vyakti antarāṇām api pratibhāsa prasaṅgaḥ iti sakala jagat pratibhāsaḥ syāt atha matam sannihita vyakti darśana kāle vyakti antara sambandhinī jātiḥ na bhāti yadā tu vyakti antaram dṛśyate tadā tad darśana velāyām tad gata tvena jātiḥ ābhāti iti sādhāraṇa svarūpa paricchedaḥ paścāt sambhavati iti tatas ca paścāt artha anvaya darśane katham na tasyāḥ tad vyāpita āgrahaḥ asat etat yatas vyakti antara darśana kāle api tad pariharam eva jāteḥ svarūpam pratibhāti na pūrva vyakti saṃsparśitayā tasyāḥ pratyakṣa gocara atikrānta tayā tad sambaddhasya api rūpasya tad atikrānta tvāt tat katham sannihita asat nihita vyakti sambaddha jātiḥ upāvagamaḥ 
TBV_7.9	 atha pratyabhijñānāt aneka vyakti sambandhi tvena jātiḥ pratīyate nanu kā iyam pratyabhijñā yadi pratyakṣam kutas tad avaseyā jātiḥ eka aneka vykti vyāpinī pratyakṣāḥ atha nayana vyāpara antantaram samupajāyamānā pratyabhijñā katham na pratyakṣam nirvikalpakasya api akṣa anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānāt pratyakṣa tvam tat atra api tulyam asat etat yadi akṣajā pratyabhijñā tathā sati prathama vyakti darśana kāle eva samasta vyakti sambaddha jāti rūpa paricchedaḥ astu atha tadā smṛti sahakāri virahāt na tattva avagatiḥ yadā tu dvitīya vyakti darśanam tadā pūrva darśana āhita saṃskāra prabodha samupajāta smṛti sahitam indriyam tattva darśanam janayati tat api asat yatas smaraṇa sacivam api locanam puras sannihitāyām eva vyaktau tad stha jātau ca pratipattim janayitum īśam na pūrva vyaktau asannidhānāt tat na tad sthitām jātim darśanam paridṛśyamāne vyakti antare sandhatte 
TBV_7.10–7.11^1	 atha indriya vṛttiḥ na smaraṇa samavāyinī karaṇa tvāt iti na asau sandhāna kāriṇī puruṣaḥ tu kartṛ tayā smṛti samavāyī iti cakṣuṣā parigate arthe tad upadarśita pūrva vyakti gatām jātim sandhāsyati iti tat asat yatas saḥ api na svatantra tayā artha grāhakaḥ kintu darśana sahāyaḥ yadi punar savatantraḥ eva artha grāhakaḥ syāt tathā sati svāpa mada mūrchā ādiṣu api sarva vyakti anugata jāti pratipattiḥ syāt tasmāt ātmā api darśana sahāyaḥ eva artha vedī darśanam ca puras sannihitam vyakti svarūpam anusarati na hi smṛti gocaram api pūrva dṛṣṭa vyakti gatam jāti ādikam iti na darśana sahāyaḥ api tad anusandhāna samarthaḥ ātmā atha smaraṇa upanītam jāti rūpam ātmā tatra sandhāsyati nanu atra api smṛtiḥ parihṛta puras vartti vyakti darśana viṣayā pūrva dṛṣṭam artham anusarantī saṃlakṣyate tat katham puras varttini apravartamānā sva viṣayān sāmānya ādīn tatra saṅghatayitum kṣamā 
TBV_7.11^2	 tat asmṛtam ca saṅghatanam katham ātmā api kartum kṣamaḥ tathā hi darśane asti draṣṭari tasya svarūpe jāte tad nimagnam na smṛti kṛtam smartṛ rūpam bhāti yadi tu bhāti tathā sati draṣṭṛ rūpaḥ eva asau na smartā atha smartṛ rūpe draṣṭṛ svarūpam anupraviṣṭam pratibhāti tathā api smartā eva asau na dṛṣṭāḥ atha draṣṭṛ smrtṛ sava rūpe vivikte bhātaḥ tathā sati tayoḥ bhedaḥ iti na ekatvam tathā hi draṣṭa sva rūpam dṛś viṣaya avabhāsaḥ pratibhāti smartṛ svarūpam api puṃsaḥ smṛti viṣayam avatīrṇam avabhāti tat kutas pūrva aparayoḥ jāti rūpayoḥ saṅghānam 
TBV_7.12^1	 yat punar uktam smarataḥ pūrva dṛṣṭa artha anusaṅghānāt utpadyamānā matiḥ cakṣuḥ sambaddha tve pratyakṣam iti etat api asat na indriya matiḥ smṛti gocara pūrvarūpa grāhiṇī tat katham sā tad saṅghānam ātmasāt karoti pūrva dṛṣṭa saṅghānam hi tad pratibhāsanam tad pratibhāsa sambandhe ca indriya mateḥ parokṣa artha grāhi tvāt parisphuṭa pratibhāsanam asat nihita viṣaya grahaṇam ca tat kutas tayoḥ aikyam atha parokṣa grahaṇam sva ātmanā na indriya matiḥ saṃspṛśati evam tarhi tad vivikta indriya matiḥ iti katham tad saṅghāyikā sāmagrī abhyupiyate yadi ca smṛti viṣaya svabhāva tayā dṛśyamānaḥ arthaḥ pratyakṣa buddhibhiḥ avagamyate tathā sati smṛti gocaraḥ pūrva svabhāvaḥ vartamāna tayā bhāti iti viparīta khyātiḥ sarvam darśanam bhavet atha yat tadā tatra avidyamānam artham avaiti jñānam tatra viparīta khyātiḥ pratyakṣa pratītiḥ tu pūrva saṅghānāt api upajāyamānā puras sat eva vastu gṛhṇatī katham viparīta khyātiḥ bhavet 
TBV_7.12^2	 nanu purva rūpa tā ahitayā tasyāḥ sat artha grahaṇam eva na sambhavati smaraṇa upaneyam hi rūpam pratiyatī vartamāna tayā pratyakṣa buddiḥ na pratibhāsamāna vapuṣaḥ sattām sādhayitum akṣam pratyasta mite api rūpe smṛteḥ avatārāt tad anusāriṇī ca akṣa matiḥ api tat eva anusarantī na sattā āspadam tasmāt indriya matiḥ sakalā pūrvarūpa grahaṇam pariharantī vartamāne parisphuṭe vartate iti tadā eva tad gatām jātim udbhāsayitum prabhuḥ iti na pūrva apara vyakti gatā jātiḥ samasti yat eva hi dvitīya vyakti gatam rūpam bhāti tat eva sat pūrva vyakti gatam tu rūpam na abhāti iti nan tat sat tatas ca aneka vyakti vyāpikāyāḥ jāteḥ siddhiḥ iti na tatra liṅga śabdayoḥ api pravṛttiḥ iti na tābhyām api tad pratipattiḥ yathā ca vyakti bhinna anusyūtā jātiḥ na sambhavati tathā yathāsthānam pratipādayiṣyate iti āstām tāvat 
TBV_7.13–7.14	 tat evam sattā samavāyayoḥ para parikalpitayoḥ asiddheḥ prāc asataḥ kāraṇa samavāyaḥ sattā samavāyaḥ vā kāryatvam iti kāryatvasya asiddha tvāt sva rūpa asiddhaḥ api kāryatva lakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ atha syāt eṣa doṣaḥ yadi yathā ukta lakṣaṇam karya tvam hetu tvena upanyastam syāt yāvatā abhūtvā bhavana lakṣaṇam kārya tvam hetu tvena upanyastam tena ayam adoṣaḥ nanu evam api bhū bhūdhara ādeḥ katham evaṃbhūtam kārya tvam siddham atha yadi atra vipratipatti viṣaya tā tadā anumānataḥ teṣu kārya tvam sādhyate tat ca anumānam bhū bhūdharāyaḥ kāryam racanāvat tvāt ghaṭa ādi vat iti katham na teṣu kāryatva lakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ siddhaḥ asat etat yatas atra api prayoge bhū bhūdhara ādeḥ avayavinaḥ asiddheḥ āśraya asiddhaḥ racanāvat tvāt iti hetuḥ tat asiddha tvam ca prāk pratipāditam 
TBV_7.15–7.16	 kiñca yadi avayava sanniveśaḥ racanā tadvat tvam ca pṛthivī ādeḥ tad utpādya tvam tadā avayava sanniveśasya saṃyoga apara nāmnaḥ asiddha tvāt asiddha viśeṣaṇaḥ racanāvat tvāt iti hetuḥ tathā pṛthivī ādiṣu samyoga janya tvasya viśeṣyasya asiddha tvāt asiddha viśeṣaḥ ca prakṛtaḥ hetuḥ katham saṃyoga asiddha tvam yena ukta doṣa aduṣṭaḥ prakṛtaḥ hetuḥ syāt ucyate tad grāhaka pramāṇa abhāvāt bādhaka pramāṇa upapatteḥ ca tathā hi 
TBV_8.1–8.3	 saṅkhyā parimāṇāni pṛthaktvam saṃyoga vibhāgau paratva aparatve karma ca rūpi dravya samavāyāt ca akṣāṇi iti vacanāt dṛśya vastu samavetasya saṃyogasya pareṇa pratyakṣa grāhya tvam abhyupagatam na ca niranara utpanna vastu dvaya pratibhāsa kālaḥ adhyakṣa pratipattau tad vyatirekeṇa paraḥ saṃyogaḥ bahis grāhya rūpa tām vibhrāmaḥ pratibhāti na api kalpana buddhau vastu dvayam yathoktam vihāya śabda ullekham ca antaram aparam varṇa ākṛti akṣara ākāra rahitam saṃyoga svarūpam udbhāti tat evam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya saṃyogasya anupalabdheḥ bhāvam śaśa viṣāṇa vat tena yat āha uddyota karaḥ 
TBV_8.4^1	 yadi saṃyogaḥ na artha antaram bhavet tadā kṣetra bīja udaka ādayaḥ nirviśiṣṭa tvāt sarva dā eva aṅkura ādi kāryam kuryuḥ na ca evam tasmāt sarvadā kārya anārambhāt kṣetra ādīni aṅkura utpattau karaṇa antara sāpekṣāṇi yathā mṛd piṇḍa ādi sāmagrī ghaṭa ādi karaṇe kulāla ādi sāpekṣā yaḥ asau kṣetra ādibhiḥ apekṣyaḥ sa saṃyogaḥ iti siddham kiñca asau saṃyogaḥ dravyayoḥ viśeṣana bhāvena pratīyamāna tvāt tatas artha antara tvena pratyakṣa siddhaḥ eva tathā hi kaścid kenācid saṃyukte dravye āharaḥ iti uktaḥ yayoḥ eva dravyayoḥ saṃyogam upalabhate te eva āharati na dravya mātram kiñca dūratara vartinaḥ puṃsaḥ sa antare api vane nirantara rūpa avasāsinī buddhiḥ udayām āsādayati sā iyam mithyā buddhiḥ mithya padārtha anubhavam antareṇa na kvacid upajāyate 
TBV_8.4^2	 na hi ananubhūta go darśanasya gavaye gauḥ iti vibhramaḥ bhavati tasmāt avaśyam saṃyogaḥ mukhyaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ tathā na caitraḥ kuṇḍalī iti anena pratiṣedha vākyena na kuṇḍalam pratiṣidhyate na api caitraḥ tayoḥ anyatra deśa ādau sattvāt tasmāt caitrasya kuṇḍala saṃyogaḥ pratiṣidhyate tathā caitraḥ kuṇḍalī iti anena api vidhi vākyena na caitra kuṇḍalayoḥ anyatara vidhānam tayoḥ siddha tvāt pāriśeṣyāt samyoga vidhānam tasmāt asti eva saṃyogaḥ iti tat nirastam draṣṭavyam saṃyukta dravya svarūpa avabhāsa vyatirekeṇa aparasya saṃyogasya pratyakṣe nirvikalpake sa nikalpake vā aparita bhāsasya pratipādita tvāt 
TBV_8.5^1	 na ca saṃyukta pratiyayā ani atha anupapattyā samyoga kalpanā upapannā nirantara avasthayoḥ eva bhāvayoḥ saṃyukta pratyaya hetu tvāt yāvat ca tasyām avasthāyām saṃayoga janaka tvena saṃyukta pratyaya viṣayau tau iṣyete tāvat samyogam antareṇa saṃyukta pratyaya hetu tvena tad viṣayau kim neṣyete pāramparyeṇa na ca sa antare vane nirantara avabhāsinī buddhiḥ mukhya padārtha anubhava pūrvikā askhalat pratyaya tvena anupacarita tvāt na caitraḥ kuṇḍalī ityādau caitra sambandhi kuṇḍalam niṣidhyate vidhīyate vā na saṃyogaḥ 
TBV_8.5^2	 na ca sambandha vyatirekeṇa caitrasya kuṇḍala sambandha anupapattiḥ iti vaktum śakyam yatas caitra kuṇḍalayoḥ kim sambandhinoḥ sa sambandhaḥ uta asambandhinoḥ na asambandhinoḥ himavat vindhyayoḥ iva asambandhinoḥ sambandha anupapatteḥ na ca asambandhinoḥ bhinna sambandhena tat abhinnam sambandhi tvam śakyam vidhātum viruddha dharma adhyāsena bhedāt na api bhinnam tad sadbhāve api tayoḥ sva rūpeṇa asambandhi tva prasaṅgāt bhinnasya tad kṛta upakāram antareṇa tad sambandhi tva ayogāt tatas apara upakāra kalpane anavasthā prasaṅgāt sambandhinoḥ tu sambandha parikalpanam vyartham sambandham antareṇa api tayoḥ svatas eva sambandhi svarūpa tvāt 
TBV_8.6^1	 yat tu uktam viśiṣṭa avasthā vyatirekeṇa kṣiti bīja udaka ādīnām na aṅkura janaka tvam sā ca viśiṣṭa avasthā teṣām saṃyoga rūpā śaktiḥ tat asāram yatas yathā viśiṣṭa avasthā yuktāḥ kṣiti ādayaḥ saṃyogam utpādayanti tathā tad avasthā yuktāḥ aṅkura ādikam api kāryam niṣpādayiṣyanti iti vyartham saṃyoga śakteḥ tad antarāla vartinyāḥ parikalpanam atha saṃyoga śakti vyatirekena na kārya utpādane kāraṇa kalāpaḥ pravartate iti nirbandhaḥ tarhi saṃyoga śakti utpādane api apara samyoga śakti vyatirekeṇa vā asau pravartate iti aparā saṃyoga śaktiḥ parikalpanīyā tatra api aparā iti anavasthā 
TBV_8.6^2	 atha tām antareṇa api śaktim utpādayanti tarhi kāryam api tām antareṇa eva aṅkura ādikam nirvartayiṣyanti iti vyartham saṃyoga śakteḥ tad antarāla vartinyāḥ kalpanam na ca viśiṣṭa avasthā vyatirekeṇa pṛthivī ādayaḥ saṃyoga śaktim api nirvartayitum kṣamāḥ tathā abhyupagame sarvadā tad nirvartana prasaṅgāt aṅkura ādeḥ api anavarata utpatti prasaṅgaḥ na ca anyatara karma ādi savyapekṣāḥ saṃyogam utpādayanti kṣiti ādayaḥ iti na ayam doṣaḥ karma utpattau api samyoga pakṣa ukta dūṣaṇasya sarvasya tulya tvāt tasmāt eka sāmagrī adhīna viśiṣṭa utpattimat padārtha vyatirekeṇa na aparaḥ saṃyogaḥ tasya bādhaka pramāṇa viṣaya tvāt sādhaka pramāṇa abhāvāt ca 
TBV_8.7	 yaḥ tu saṃyukte dravye ete iti anayoḥ vā ayam saṃyogaḥ iti vyapadeśaḥ sa bheda antara pratikṣepa apratikṣepābhyām tathā avasthā utpanna vastu dvaya nibandhanaḥ eva na atas aparasya saṃyogasya siddhiḥ na ca akṣaṇika tve tayoḥ sa sambandhī yuktaḥ tad sambandhasya samavāyasya niṣiddha tvāt niṣetsyamāna tvāt ca na ca tad janya tvāt asau tad sambandhī akṣaṇika tve janakatva virodhasya pratipādayiṣyamāṇa tvāt kṣaṇika tve api tayoḥ eka sāmagrī adhīnā nairantarya utpattiḥ eva na aparaḥ saṃyogaḥ iti racanāvat tvāt iti atra hetoḥ viśeṣaṇasya saṃyoga viśeṣasya racanā lakṣaṇasya asiddheḥ tadvataḥ viśeṣyasya api asiddhiḥ iti dvarūpa asiddhatvam 
TBV_8.8^1	 atha pṛti vyādeḥ kārya tvam bauddhaiḥ abhyupagamyate eva iti na asiddha tvam taiḥ asya hetoḥ pareranīyam nanu atra api yādṛś bhūtam buddhimat pūrvaka tvena devakula ādiṣu anvaya vyatirekābhyām vyāptam kāryatvam upalabdham yat akriyā darśinaḥ api jīrṇa devakula ādau upalabhyamānam laukika parīkṣaka ādeḥ tatra kṛtabuddhim utpādayati tādṛś bhūtasya kṣiti ādiṣu kāryatvasya anupalabdheḥ asiddhaḥ kāryatva lakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ upalambhe vā tatra tatas jīrṇa deva kula ādiṣu iva akriyā darśinaḥ api kṛtabuddiḥ syāt na hi anvaya vyatirekābhyām su vivecitam kāryam kāraṇam vyabhicarati tasya ahetuka tva prasaṅgāt 
TBV_8.8^2	 atas kṣiti ādiṣu kāryatva darśanāt akriyā darśinaḥ kṛta buddhi anupapatteḥ yat buddhimat kāraṇa tvena vyāptam kāryatvam devakula ādiṣu niścitam tat tatra na asti iti asiddhaḥ hetuḥ kevalam kāryatva mātram prasiddham tatra na ca prakṛtyā parasparam artha antara tvena vyavasthitaḥ api dharmaḥ śabda mātreṇa ābhedī hetu tvena upādīyamānaḥ abhimata sādhya siddhaye paryāptaḥ bhavati sādhya viparyaye api taya bhāva avirodhāt yatha valmīke dharmiṇi kumbhakāra kṛta tva siddhaye mṛd vikāra mātram hetu tvena upādīyamānam iti yat buddhimat kāraṇa tvena vyāptam devakula ādau kārya tvam pramāṇataḥ pratisiddham yat ca kṣiti ādau asiddham yat ca kṣiti ādau na anaikāntikam na tatas abhimata sādhya siddhiḥ 
TBV_8.9^1	 nanu etat kāryasamam nāma jāti uttaram tathā hi kṛtaka tvāt anityaḥ śabdhaḥ iti ukte jāti vādī atra api prerayati kim idam ghaṭa ādi gatam kṛtaka tvam hetu tvena upanyastam kim vā śabda gatam atha ubhaya gatam iti ādye pakṣe hetoḥ asiddhiḥ na hi anya dharmaḥ anyatra vartate dvitīya api sādhana vikalaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ tṛtīye api etau eva doṣau iti 
TBV_8.9^2	 etat ca kāryasamam nāma jāti uttaram iti pratipāditam yathā uktam kāryatva anyatva leśena yat sādhya asiddhi darśanam tat kārya samam iti kāryatva sāmānyasya anitya tva sādhaka tvena upanyāse abhyupagate dharmi bhedena vikalpana vat buddhimat kāraṇa tve kṣiti ādeḥ kāryatva mātreṇa sādhye abhīṣṭe dharmi bhedena kārya tva ādeḥ vikalpanāt asat etat yatas sāmānyena kāryatva anitya tvayoḥ viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇa balāt vyāpti siddhau kāryatva sāmānyam śabda ādau dharmiṇī upalabhyamānam anitya tvam sādhayati iti kāryatva mātrasya eva tatra hetu tvena upanyāse dharma vikalpanam yat tatra kriyeta tat sarva anumāna ucchedaka tvena kārya sama jāti uttara tām āsādayate na tu evam kṣiti ādeḥ buddhimat kāraṇa tve sādhye kāryatva sāmānyam hetu tvena sambhavati tasya viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇa abhāvāt sandigdha vipakṣa vyāvṛttika tvena a= aikāntika tvāt yat ca buddhimat kāraṇa pūrvaka tvena vyāptam devakula ādau kārya tvam pratipannam yat akriyā darśinaḥ api jīrṇa prāsāda ādau kṛtabuddhim utpādayati tat tatra asiddham iti pratipāditam 
TBV_8.10^1	 api ca yadi atra vyāpaka nitya eka buddhimat kāraṇam kṣiti ādeḥ kāraṇa tvena abhipretam kāryatva lakṣaṇāt dhetoḥ tathā sati ghaṭa ādau dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇi tad pūrvaka tvena kāryatvasya aniścayāt sādhya vikalaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ viruddhaḥ ca hetuḥ syāt anitya buddhi ādhāra avyāpaka aneka kartṛ pūrvaka tvena vyāptasya kāryatvasya ghaṭa ādau niścayāt atha buddhimat kāraṇa tva mātram sādhya tvena abhipretam kṣiti ādau tarhi nitya buddhi ādhāra vyāpaka eka kartṛ pūrvakatva lakṣaṇasya vśeṣasya kṣiti ādau asiddheḥ na īśvara siddhiḥ 
TBV_8.10^2–8.11	 atha buddhimat kāraṇa tva sāmānyam eva kṣiti ādau sādhyate tat ca pakṣa dharma tā balāt viśiṣṭa viśeṣa ādhāram sidhyati nirviśeṣasya sāmānyasya asambhavāt anitya jñānavataḥ śarīriṇaḥ kṣiti ādi vinirmāṇa sāmarthya rahita tvena ghaṭa ādau= upalabdhasya viśeṣasya buddhimat kāraṇa tva sāmānya ādhārasya tatra asambhavāt nanu evam sāmānya āśraya tvena yat ghaṭa ādau vyakti svarūpam pratipannam tasya kṣiti ādau asambhavāt anyasya ca vyakti svarūpasya vivakṣita sāmānya āśraya tvena aprasiddha tvāt nirādhārasya ca sāmānyasya asambhavāt buddhimat kāraṇa tva sāmānyasya eva kṣiti ādau na siddhiḥ syāt na hi kvacid go tva ādhārasya khaṇḍa ādi vyakti viśeṣasya asambhave a nya rūpa mahiṣī ādi vyakti samāśritam go tvam kutaścid dhetoḥ siddhim āsādayati 
TBV_8.12^1	 atha kāryatvasya kṣiti ādau buddhimat kāraṇa tva abhāve abhava prasaṅgāt vilakṣaṇa vyakti āśritasya api tad sāmānyasya tatra siddhiḥ bhavati eva yathā mahānasa vilakṣaṇa giri śikhara ādi ādhārasya agni sāmānyasya dhūmāt prasidhiḥ syāt etat yadi adhūma vyāvṛttam dhūmātram anagni vyāvṛttena agninā vyāptam yathā pratyakṣa anupalambha lakṣanāt pramāṇāt prasiddham tathā atra api abhuddhimat kāraṇa vyāvṛttena buddhimat kāraṇa tva mātreṇa ākāra vyāvṛttasya kārya mātrasya kutaścid pramāṇāt vyāptiḥ sarva upasaṃhāreṇa niścitā syāt yāvatā sā eva na siddhāḥ atha yathā karya dharma anuvṛtteḥ kāryam hutabhujaḥ dhūmaḥ sa tad abhāve api abhavan hetumat tām vilaṅghayet iti na agni vyatirekeṇa dhūmasya sadbhāvaḥ iti sarva upasaṃhāreṇa vyāpti siddhiḥ tathā atra api bhūdhara ādi kārya dharma anuvṛttitaḥ buddhimat kāraṇa kāryam tad abhāve tat bhavat nirhetukam syāt iti sarva upasaṃhāreṇa vyāpti siddhiḥ 
TBV_8.12^2	 nanu ghaṭa ādi lakṣaṇaḥ kārya viśeṣaḥ buddhimat anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyī ya upalabhyamānaḥ tad samāneṣu padārtheṣu akriyā darśinaḥ api kṛta buddhim utpādayati saḥ eva buddhimat kāraṇa kārya tvāt tad abhāve bhavat nirhetukaḥ syāt iti vaktum śākyam na punar kāryatva mātram kāraṇa mātra hetukam buddhimat kāraṇa abhāve bhavat nirhetukam āsajyate tat dhi kāraṇa mātra abhāve bhavat nirhetukam syāt na ca kārya viśeṣaḥ kartāram antareṇa na upalabdhaḥ iti kāryatva mātram api kartṛ viśeṣa anumāpakam iti nyāya vidā vaktum yuktam anyathā dhūma viśeṣaḥ tad kāla vahni avyabhicaritaḥ mahānasa ādau upalabdha iti dhūpa ghaṭikā ādau dhūma mātram api tad kāla vahni anumāpakam syāt 
TBV_8.12^3	 atha tatra tad kāla vahni anumāne tatas pratyakṣa avirodhaḥ sa tarhi bhūruha ādau api akṛṣṭa jāte kartṛ anumāne kāryatva lakṣaṇāt dhetoḥ samānaḥ atha tad kartuḥ atīndriya tva abhyupagamāt na pratyakṣa virodhaḥ dhūpa ghaṭikā ādau api vahneḥ atīndriya tva abhyupagame kaḥ doṣaḥ yeva pratyakṣa virodhaḥ udbhāvyeta mahānasa ādau tathābhūtasya eva tasya darśanāt iti ced nanu evam bhūruha ādau api yadi kartā syāt tadā śarīravān dṛśyaḥ eva syāt ghaṭa ādau kartuḥ tathābhūtasya eva tasya upalambhāt iti samānam paśyāmaḥ 
TBV_8.13^1	 atha vṛkṣa śākhā bhaṅga ādi kāryasya adṛśyaḥ piśāca ādiḥ kartā yathā abhyupagataḥ sva śarīra avayavānām vā apara śarīra vyatirekeṇa api yathā vā prerakaḥ devadatta ādiḥ tathā bhūruha ādi kārya kartā adṛśyaḥ śarīra ādi rahitaḥ ca yadi syāt kaḥ doṣaḥ na kaścid dṛṣṭa vyatikrama vyatirekeṇa tathā hi devadatta ādeḥ api sva śarīra avayava preraka tvam viśiṣṭa śarīra sambandha vyatirekeṇa na upalabdham iti etāvat mātram eva tatra tasya kartṛ tva nibandhanam na apara śarīra sambaddhaḥ tatra tasya upayogī iti bhūruha ādi kartuḥ api śarīra sambaddhasya eva kārya karaṇe vyāpāraḥ yuktaḥ na anyathā 
TBV_8.13^2	 tad sambandhaḥ ca tasya yadi tad kṛtaḥ abhyupagamyate tadā śarīsa sambandha rahitasya tad akaraṇa sāmarthyam iti apara śarīra sambandhaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ anyathā śarīra sambandha rahitasya katham prastuta kārya karaṇam tathā tad abhyupagame vyāpara apara śarīra nirvartane kṣīṇa vyāpāra tvāt īśasya na bhūruha ādi kārya nirvartavam atha tad anirvartitam tat śarīram tadā atra api vaktavyam kim tat kāryam uta nityam iti yadi ādyaḥ pakṣaḥ tadā tasya kāryatve sati api na kartṛ pūrvaka tvam tatas tena eva kāryatva lakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ vyabhicārī atha nityam tadā yathā tat śarīrasya śarīra tve sati api nitya tva lakṣaṇaḥ svabhāva atikramaḥ abhyupagamyate tathā bhūruha ādeḥ kāryatve sati api akartṛ pūrvaka tvam anabhyupagantavyam iti punar api taiḥ hetuḥ vyabhicārī prakṛtaḥ 
TBV_8.14	 piśāca ādeḥ tu śarīra sambandha rahitasya kārya kartṛ tvam mukta ātmanaḥ iva anupapannam atha asti eva tasya śarīra sambandhaḥ kintu adṛśya śarīra sambandhāt asau adṛśyaḥ kartā abhyupagamyate nanu kulāla ādeḥ api śarīra sambandhaḥ eva dṛśya tvam na aparam svarūpeṇa ātmanaḥ adṛṣṭya tvam na aparam svarūpeṇa ātmanaḥ adṛśya tvāt atha dṛśya śarīra sambandhāt tasya dṛṣya tvam nanu piśāca ādi śarīrasya śarīra tve sati api katham adṛśya tvam 
TBV_8.15	 asmad ādi cakṣuḥ vyāpāreṇa tasya anupalambhāt iti ced nanu yathā śarīra tve sati api asmad ādi śarīra vilakṣaṇam piśāca ādi lakṣaṇam śarīram anupalabhya tvena abhyupagamyate tathā ghaṭa ādi vilakṣaṇam bhūruha ādi kāryatve sati api akartṛka tvena kim na abhyupagamyate tathā abhyupagame ca punar api prakṛtaḥ hetuḥ vyabhicārī tat evam asiddha tva anaikāntika tva viruddha tva doṣa diṣṭa tvāt na asmāt dhetoḥ prastuta sādhya siddhiḥ tena yat uktam pṛthivī ādi gatasya kāryatvasya apratipatteḥ na tasmāt īśvara avagamaḥ iti tat yuktam eva uktam 
TBV_8.16	 yat tu uktan pṛthivī ādīnām bauddhaiḥ kāryatvam abhyupagatam te katham evam vadeyuḥ iti tat asāram prakṛta sādhya siddhi nibandhanasya kāryatvasya teṣu asiddhatva pratipādanāt yat ca abhāṣi ye api cārvākaḥ teṣām kārya tvam na icchanti teṣām api viśiṣṭa saṃsthāna yuktānām katham kārya tā iti tas api ayuktam saṃsthāna yukta tvasya asiddha tva ādi doṣa duṣṭa tva pratipādanāt yat ca saṃsthāna śabda vācya tvam kevalam ghaṭa ādibhiḥ sāmānyam pṛthivī ādīnām na tu arthaḥ kaścid dvayoḥ anigataḥ samānaḥ vidyate tat evam eva yat tu uktam dhūma ādau api pūrva apara vyakti gataḥ na eva kaścid anugataḥ arthaḥ samānaḥ asti ityādi tat asaṅgatam ghaṭa ādi saṃsthānebhyaḥ pṛthivī ādi saṃsthānasya vailakṣaṇyena hetoḥ asiddha tva pratipādanāt 
TBV_8.17^1	 yat api uktam vyutpannānām asti eva pṛthivī ādi samsthānavattva kārya tva ādeḥ hetoḥ dharmi dharma tā avagamaḥ avyutpannānām tu prasiddha anumāne dhūma ādau api na asti iti tat api acāru yatas yadi anumāna nimitta hetu pakṣa dharma tva pratibandha lakṣaṇām vyutpattim āśritya vyutpannā abhidhīyate tadā pṛthivī ādi gata saṃsthāna kārya tva ādau ghaṭa ādi saṃsthāna vailakṣaṇye prakṛta sādhya sādhake vyutpattuḥ na keṣāñcid api bhavati yathā ukta sādhya vyāptasya pṛthivī ādau saṃsthāna ādeḥ abhāvāt bhāve vā śarīra ādimataḥ asmad ādi indriya grāhyasya anitya buddhayā ādi dharma kalāpa upetasya ghaṭa ādau saṃsthāna ādi hetu vyāpaka tvena pratipannasya kartuḥ pṛthivī ādau tatas pratipattiḥ syāt na hi hetu vyāpakam apahāya avyāpakasya viruddha dharma ākrāntasya aparasya sādhya dharmasya pratipattiḥ sādhya dharmiṇi yathā ukta lakṣana lakṣita hetu bala samutthā iti anumāna vidām vyavahāraḥ 
TBV_8.17^2	 kāraṇa mātra pratipattau tu tatas tatra na vipratipattiḥ iti siddha sādhya tā atha hetu lakṣaṇa vyutpatti vyatiriktām vyutpattim āśritya vyutpannānām iti ucyate tadā kenacid sraṣṭrā jagat sṛṣṭam iti nirmūla durāgamāhita vāsanānām asti eva pṛthivī ādi saṃsthānavattva kārya tva ādeḥ hetoḥ dharmi dharma tā avagama ādiḥ na ca tathābhūta dharmi dharmatā ādi avagamāt sādhya siddhiḥ vede mīmāṃsakasya asmaryamāṇa kartṛka tva ādeḥ dharmi dharma tā avagama ādeḥ yathāpauruṣeya tvasya avyutpannānām tu pratisiddha anumāne dhūma ādau api na asti iti yuktam eva asmābhiḥ api abhyupagamyāt 
TBV_8.18^1	 yat tu prāsāda ādi saṃsthāna ādeḥ vailakṣaṇye api pṛthivī ādi saṃsthāna ādeḥ kāryatva ādi pṛthivī ādīnām iṣyate kāryam ca kartṛ karaṇa karma pūrvakam dṛṣṭam ityādi tat api asaṅgatam yatas yatas nāma ghaṭa ādeḥ viśiṣṭa kāryasya kartṛ pūrvaka tvam upalabdham na etāvatā viśiṣṭasya api bhūruha ādi kāryasya kartṛ pūrvaka tvam abhyupagantum yuktam anyathā pṛthivī lakṣaṇasya kāryasya rūpa rasa gandha sparśa guṇa yogi tvam upalabdham bhūta tve sati vāyoḥ api tad yogi tvam abhyupagamanīyam syāt tattvāt eva atha atra pratyakṣa ādi bādhaḥ sa bhūruha ādi kāryeṣu api samānaḥ iti prāk pratipāditam 
TBV_8.18^2–8.19	 yat tu uktam kartṛ pūrvakasya kārya tva ādeḥ tad vailakṣaṇyāt na tatas sādhya avagamaḥ ityādi tat satyam eva tad vailakṣaṇyasya prasādhita tvāt atas iva siddham yādṛś adhiṣṭhātṛ bhāva abhāva anuvṛttimat sanniveśa ādi ityādi grantha pratipāditasya dūṣaṇasya kāryatva ādau sarvasmin īśvara sādhake hetau samāna tvāt na kasyacid tad sādhaka tā yadi evam anumāna uccheda prasaṅgaḥ dhūma ādi yathāvidham agni ādi sāmagrī bhāva abhāva anuvṛttimat tathāvidham etat yadi parvata upari bhavet syāt tatas vahni ādi avagamaḥ iti ādikaḥ tu pūrva pakṣa granthaḥ pūrvam eva vihita uttaraḥ yathā yathābhūtaḥ adhūma vyāvṛttaḥ dhūmaḥ anagni vyāvṛttena agninā vyāptaḥ viparyaye bādhaka pramāna balāt avasitaḥ giri śikhara ādau upalabhyamānaḥ tad deśam agni sāmānyam aniyata tā arṇa pārṇa ādi agni vyakti samāśritam anumāpayati 
TBV_8.20^1	 na evam karyatva mātram buddhimat kāraṇa tva sāmānyena vyāptam viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇa balāt niścitam kintu kāraṇa tva mātreṇa vyāptam tat tad balāt niścitam tat ca upalabhyamānam kṣiti ādau kāraṇa mātram anumāpayati yathā giri śikhara ādau= upalabhyamānaḥ dhūmaḥ tad sambaddham agni mātram aniyata vyakti niṣṭham tena pṛthivī ādi gata kārya tva darśanāt kartṛ adarśinaḥ tad apratipatti vat śikharī ādi gata vahni ādi adarśinām dhūmāt api tad pratipattiḥ astu iti kaḥ anyaḥ anumāna svarūpa vidaḥ bhavataḥ vaktum kṣamaḥ yadi hi kārya viśeṣāt dhūma lakṣaṇāt upalabhyamānāt gṛhīta avinābhāvasya puṃsaḥ agni lakṣaṇa kāraṇa viśeṣa pratipattiḥ giri śikhara ādau bhavati tadā kārya mātrāt pṛthivī ādau upalabhyamānāt buddhimat kāraṇa viśeṣasya tatra pratipattau kim āyātam 
TBV_8.20^2	 kāraṇa mātra pratipattiḥ tu tatas tatra bhavati eva su vivecitam kāryam kāraṇam na vyabhicarati iti nyāyāt atas eva anyasya sambaddhasya anyatas pratipattau kārya kāraṇa avagama ādau prayatnaḥ kāryaḥ anyathā tad uttha pramāṇasya pramāṇa ābhāsa tā syāt yat tu na ca atra śabda sāmānyam vastu anugamaḥ na asti iti yuktam vaktum dhūma ādau api śabda sāmānyasya vaktum śakya tvāt iti tat api asaṅgatam dhūma ādi vailakṣaṇyena pṛthivī ādau kāryatvasya buddhimat kāraṇa tva avyāpteḥ śabda sāmānyasya sādhita tvāt 
TBV_8.21	 yat ca ghaṭa ādi vat pṛthivī ādi sva avayava saṃyogaiḥ ārabdham avaśyam tad viśleṣāt vināśam anubhaviṣyati ityādi tat api asaṅgatam avayava saṃyoga vat tad viśleṣasya api vibhāga lakṣaṇasya vināśam prati hetu tvena upanyastasya asiddhi tvāt tat asiddha tvam ca samyoga vat vaktavyam evam vināśāt vā sambhāvitāt kāryatva anumānam racanā svabhāva tvāt vā ityādi sarvam nirastam draṣṭavyam yat tu cārvākam prati kāryatva sādhanāya uktam yathā laukika vaidikyaḥ racanayoḥ aviśeṣāt kartṛ pūrvaka tvam tathā prāsāda ādi pṛthivī ādi samsthānayoḥ api tad rūpa tāḥ tu aviśeṣāt tat api acāru tad viśeṣasya pratipādita tvāt na hi kevalāt pakṣa dharmāt vyāpti śūnyāt sādhya avagamaḥ tat satyam eva vyāpti rahitāt dhetoḥ sādhya siddheḥ asambhavāt 
TBV_8.22	 yat ca ghaṭa ādau kartṛ pūrvaka tvena kāryatva avagame api keṣāñcid kāryāṇām akartṛ pūrva kāṇām kāryatva darśanāt na sarvam kartṛ pūrvakam yathā vaneṣu vanaspati ādīnām iti tat api satyam eva tasmāt na īśvara siddhau kaścid dhetuḥ avyabhicāri asti iti etat paryantam yat api uktam na ākṛṣṭa jātaiḥ sthāvara ādibhiḥ vyabhicāraḥ vyāpti abhāvaḥ vā sādhya abhāve hetuḥ vartamānaḥ vyabhicārī ucyate teṣu kartṛ a grahaṇam na kartṛ abhāva niścayaḥ iti tat api asāram sarva pramāṇa viṣaya tve api yadi sthāvara ādiṣu kartṛ abhāva niścayaḥ na bhavati tathā sati ākāśa ādau rūpa ādi abhāva niścayaḥ mā bhūt atha tatra rūpa ādi sadbhāva bādhaka pramāṇa sadbhāvāt tad abhāva niścayaḥ saḥ atra api samānaḥ tat ca pramāṇam pradarśayiṣyāmaḥ ananantaram eva 
TBV_8.23	 yat tu uktam kṣiti ādi anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāna darśanāt teṣām tad atiriktasya karyaṇa tva kalpane ati prasaṅga koṣaḥ iti etasyām kalpanāyām dharma adharmayoḥ api na kāraṇa tā bhavet ityādi tat ayuktam dharma adharma ādeḥ kārana tvam jagat vaicitryāni atha anupapattyā vyavasthāpyate tathā hi sarvān utpattimataḥ prati bhūmi ādeḥ sādhāraṇa tvāt tad anya adṛṣṭa ākhya vicitra kāraṇa kṛtam kārya vaicitryam na ca evam īśvarasya kāraṇa tva parikalpanāyām kiñcid nimittam sambhavati tad vyatirekeṇa kasyacid arthasya anupapadyamānasya adṛṣṭeḥ na ca cetanam kartāram vinā akārya svarūpa anupapattiḥ iti śakyam vaktum dṛṣṭasya eva sugata sutaiḥ caitanyasya jagat vaicitrya kartṛka tvena abhyupagamāt tadā tad vyatirikta anyeśvarasya kalpanāyām nimitta abhāvāt 
TBV_8.24	 na ca adṛṣṭasya cetaneṣu api sakala jagat upādāna upakaraṇa sampradāna ādi abhijñātā na sambhavati iti tad vyatiriktaḥ aparaḥ maheśaḥ tad jñaḥ kalpanīyaḥ iti vaktum yuktam tat jñānavat tvena tasya api asiddheḥ na ca sakala jagat kartṛ tva siddhiḥ tad siddhau ca tasya tad abhijña tva siddhiḥ iti vyaktam itaretara āśraya tvam 
TBV_8.25	 atha yat yat karyam tat tat upadāna ādi abhijña kartṛ pūrvakam upalabdham ghaṭa ādi vat pṛthivī ādi api kāryam tena tat api tad abhijña kartṛ pūrvakam yuktam iti na itaretara āśraya doṣaḥ nanu ghaṭa ādi kārya kartuḥ api kulāla ādeḥ yat api sarvathā ghaṭa ādi upādāna ādi abhijña tvam siddham syāt tadā yujyeta api etat vaktum na ca tasya api ghaṭa ādi upādāna upakaraṇa ādeḥ parimāṇa avayava saṅkhyeya tva ādi aneka dharma sākṣāt karaṇa jñānam asti tattvam siddham kim cit mātra parijñānam tu cetana tve adṛṣṭasya api tad ādhārasya vā sattvasya tad dṛṣṭa nirvartita phala upabhoktuḥ pratiniyata śarīra adhiṣṭhāyakasya vidyate iti vyartham vyatiriktā apara jñānavataḥ maheśasya parikalpanam na ca ayam ekāntaḥ sarvam kāryam tad upādāna ādi abhijñena eva kartrā nirvartyate iti svāpa mada avasthāyām śarīra ādi avayava preraṇasya kāryasya tad upādāna abhijñāna abhāve api tad kṛta tvena upalabdheḥ 
TBV_8.26	 yat ca uktam na ca ākṛṣṭa jāteṣu sthāvara ādiṣu tasya agrahaṇena pratikṣepaḥ anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta tvāt adṛṣṭa vat iti tat api acāru yatas yadi tasya śarīra sambandha rahitasya kartṛ tvam abhyupeyate tat na yukti saṅgatam tad sambandha rahitasya mukta ātmanaḥ akartṛ tvam na punar śarīra sambandha abhāvāt iti viṣamaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ tat ayuktam jñāna ādi samavāyasya kartṛ tvena abhyupagatasya tatra api niṣiddha tvāt tasmāt śarīra sambandhāt eva tasya jagat kartṛ tvam abhyupagantavyam kulālasya iva ghaṭa kartṛ tvam tad sambandhaḥ ced abhyupagamyate katham na tasya upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta tvam kulāla ādeḥ api śarīra sambandhāt eva upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptam na punar tad sambandha rahitasya ātmanaḥ dṛśya tvam tat ca īśvare api śarīra sambandhi tvam kartṛ tvāt abhyupagantavyam iti upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupalabdheḥ tad kartuḥ sthāvara ādiṣu abhāvaḥ siddhaḥ iti katham na taiḥ kāryatva lakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ vyabhicārī 
TBV_8.27^1	 atha adṛśyam tat śarīram atas tatra sat api na upalabhyate iti ayam adoṣah nanu evam api asmin sati idam sthāvara ādikam jātam iti pratipattiḥ me bhūt tathā anya kāraṇa bhave api yathā atīndriyasya indriyasya abhāve rūpa ādi jñānam na upajāyate tathā pṛthivī ādi karaṇa sākalye api kadācid tad śarīra virahe tad sthāvara ādi kāryam na upajāyate iti vyatirekāt pratītiḥ kim na syāt yadā yatra tat śarīram niyamena sannihitam iti ca ayam doṣaḥ tarhi yugapad bhāviṣu triloka adhikaraṇeṣu bhāveṣu kā vārtā na hi ekasya mūrtasya sāvayavasya maheśvara vapuṣaḥ api yugapad sakala vyāptiḥ sambhavati 
TBV_8.27^2	 amūrva tve niraṃśa prasaṅgāt ākāśam eva tat śarīram tasya tad śarīra tvena adya api asiddha tvāt atha yāvanti krama bhāvīni aṅkura ādi kāryāṇi tavanti tathāvidhāni tad śarīrāṇi kalpyante tarhi tad śarīraiḥ sakalam jagat āpūritam iti na aṅkura ādi kāryaiḥ utpattavyam tad utpatti deśa abhāvāt na api māheśvaraiḥ kvacid pravartitavyam kutaścid vā nivartitavyam tad śarīrāṇām pāda ādi abhighāta bhayāt api ca tāni api kāryāṇi sāvayava tvāt kumbha vat tatas tad karaṇe tāvānti eva aparāṇi tasya śarīrāṇi kalpanīyāni punar tad karaṇe api iti na anavasthātaḥ muktiḥ tat na śarīra vyāpāra sahāyaḥ api asau sthāvara ādi kāryam karoti iti kalpayitum yuktam aneka doṣa prasaṅgāt 
TBV_8.28–8.29	 na api sattā mātreṇa asau sva kāryamm karoti iti kalpayitum yuktam śarīra kalpana vaii arthya prasaṅgāt atha sarva utpattimatām īśvaraḥ nimitta kāraṇam tasya tad kāraṇa tvam sakala kārya kāraṇa parijñāne na anyathā tad parijñānam ca anityasya indriya śarīram antareṇa anupapatteḥ atas tad artham tat parikalpanam iti ced na sakala hetu phala viṣayam tasya anityam sa indriya śarīra jam jñānam na sambhavati indriyāṇām yugapad sarva artha sannikarṣa abhāvāt indriya artha sannikarṣa jam ca naiyāyikaiḥ pratyakṣam abhyupagamyate tat uktam indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam jñānam avyapadeśyam avyabhicāri vyavasāya ātmakam pratyakṣam 
TBV_8.30	 sāmagrī phala svarūpa viśeṣaṇa pakṣa traye api indriya artha sannikarśa jasya tasya prāmāṇya abhyupagamāt tathā pramāṇataḥ artha pratipattau pravṛtti sāmarthyāt arthavat pramāṇam iti atra bhāṣye pramātṛ prameyābhyām artha antaram pramiti lakṣaṇe phale sādhakatama vat iti arthaḥ sahakāri pramāṇam pratipāditam sahakāri tvam ca arthasya pramāṇasya phala janane vyāpriyamānasya phala janaka tvena tasya api sahāya bhāvaḥ saha karoti iti sahakāri iti vyutpatteḥ na ca asat nihitasya arthasya atītasya anāgatasya vā pramiti lakṣaṇa phala jananam prati vyāpāraḥ sambhavati na ca pramityajanakaḥ arthaḥ tat abhyupagame na pramāṇa viṣaya tā iti atas sa indriya śarīra janita pratyakṣa jñāna vat tva abhyupagame maheśasya na sakala kārya kāraṇa viṣaya jñāna sambhavaḥ iti śarīra sambandhāt tasya jagat kartṛ tva abhyupagame tat akartṛ tvam eva prasaktam iti na tasya adṛśya śarīra sambandhaḥ abhyupagantum yuktaḥ 
TBV_8.31^1	 api ca ghaṭa ādi kāryam dṛśya śarīra sambaddha puruṣa pūrvakam upalabdham iti aṅkura ādi kāryam api tathā kalpanīyam atha tad parikalpane pratyakṣa bādha anava stha ādi doṣāt aṅkura ādi kāryasya kartṛ pūrvaka tā eva viśīryate iti na tathā akalpanam nanu tad viśareṇe kaḥ doṣaḥ atha aṅkura ādeḥ kārya tā aneka karaṇa mātra abhāve samupajāyamānasya tasya akārya tā prasaktiḥ na punar kartṛ bhāve anyathā gopāla ghaṭikā ādau tad kāla agni abhāve dhūmasya api abhāva prasaktiḥ na punar kartṛ bhāveṇa anala pūrvaka tvam vyāpti grahaṇa kāle dhūmasya pratipannam tena tatas tatra tad kāraṇam anala anumānam 
TBV_8.31^2	 nanu evam kārya mātram kāraṇa mātra pūrvaka tvena vyāptam vyāpti grahaṇa kāle pratipannam aṅkura ādau upalabhyamānam kāraṇa mātram idam anumāpayatu na punar buddhimat kāraṇa viśeṣam tena kārya mātrasya vyāpteḥ niścayāt na ca dṛśya śarīra sambaddha buddhimat kāraṇa pūrvaka tvam kārya viśeṣasya upalabdham aṅkura ādau tu kāryatvam upalabhyamānam tathābhūta kartṛ pūrvakatva anumāne tatra pratyakṣa virodhaḥ iti adṛśya sambaddha śarīra kartṛ pūrvaka tvam anumāpayati iti vaktum śakyam tathā abhyupagame gopāla ghaṭikā ādau api tad kāla adṛśya anala anumāpakaḥ dhūmaḥ kim na syāt 
TBV_8.31^3	 na ca vahniḥ adṛśyaḥ na sambhavati iti vaktum śakyam na ayana raśmiṣu adṛśyasya tasya sadbhāva abhyupagamāt atha avyavahita rūpa upalabdhi anyathā anupapattyā tasya tathābhūtasya parikalpanam nanu evam dhūma sadbhāvāni atha anupapattyā tatra tasya tathābhūtasya kim na parikalpanam api ca yathā analasya bhāsva rūpa sambandhi tve sati api tasya udbhūta tvān udbhūta tvābhyām dṛśya tvādṛśya tve parikalpyete tathā prāsāda aṅkura ādīnām kāryatve kim na parikalpyete nyāyasya samāna tvāt tat na adṛśya śarīra sambandhāt tasya aṅkura ādi kārya utpādaka tvam yuktam dṛśya śarīra sambandhāt tad kartṛ tve upalabhya anupalambhāt katham tasya na abhāvaḥ yat tu uktam na ca sarvā karaṇa sāmagrī upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptāḥ ityādi tat satyam eva idam tu asatyam īśvarasya kāraṇa tve api na tad svarūpa grahaṇam pratyakseṇa adṛṣṭa vat kārya dvāreṇa tad pratipatteḥ iti adṛṣṭa pratipattau iva īśvara pratipattau kārya tva ādeḥ hetoḥ nirdoṣasya asambhavāt iti pratipādita tvāt 
TBV_8.32	 yat tu uktam sthāvareṣu kartṛ a grahaṇam kartṛ abhāvāt āhosvit vidyamāna tve api tasya agrahaṇam anupalabhya svabhāva tvena evam sandigdha vyatirikta tve na kaścid dhetuḥ gamakaḥ dhūma ādeḥ api sakala vyakti ākṣepeṇa vyāpti upalambha kāle na sakalāḥ vahni vyaktayo dṛśyāḥ ityādi yāvat sarvam utpattimat kartṛ karaṇa pūrvakam dṛṣṭam tasya sakṛt api tathā adarśanāt tad janya tā svabhāvaḥ tasya evam svabhāva niścitau anyatama abhāve api katham svabhāvaḥ iti tat api asaṅgatam yatas yādṛś bhūtam iva ghaṭa ādi kāryam tat pūrvakam upalabdham tasya sakṛt api tathā adarśanāt tat janyaḥ svabhāvaḥ vyavasthitaḥ iti tad anyatama abhāve api tasya bvhāve sakṛt api tad sadbhāvaḥ na syāt iti yuktam ca vaktum na punar tad vilakṣaṇam bhūruha ādikam kartṛ karaṇa pūrvakam kadācana api upalabdham kintu kāraṇa mātra pūrvakam atas tad abhāve tasya bhavataḥ ahetuka tva prāpteḥ tat eve tat gamayati iti asakṛt āveditam 
TBV_8.33	 yat ca anupalabhyamāna kartṛkeṣu sthāvareṣu kartuḥ anupalambhaḥ śarīra ādi a bhāvāt na tu asattvāt ityādi tat api pratikṣiptam ukta uttara tvāt yat api uktam caitanya mātreṇa upādāna ādi adhiṣṭhānāt katham pratyakṣa vyāpṛtiḥ tat asaṅgatam tathā upādāna ādi adhiṣṭhāyaka tvasya kvacid api adarśanāt adṛṣṭasya api tasya kalpane buddhi anadhiṣṭhitasya api bhūruha ādi upādānasya tad kartṛ tvam kim na kalpyate adarśana aviśeṣāt 
TBV_8.34^1	 yat ca abhyadhāyi kāryasya śarīreṇa saha vyabhicāraḥ dṛśyate sva śarīra avayavānām hi śarīra antaram antareṇa api pravṛtti nivṛttī kevalaḥ vidadhāti iti tat api ayuktam yatas śarīra sambandha vyatirekeṇa cetanasya sva śarīra avayaveṣu anyatra vā kārya nirvartaka tvam na dṛṣṭam iti na yatra api tat tasya na kalpanīyam iti etāvat mātram eva pratipādyate na tu apara śarīra sambandha parikalpanam atra upayogi yadi ca śarīra rahitasya api tasya bhūruha ādi kārye vyāpāraḥ parikalpyate tahri muktasya api tad antareṇa jñāna samavāyi kāraṇa tva parikalpanam kim na kriyate tathā abhyupagame na jñāna sukha ādi guṇa rahita ātma svarūpa avasthitiḥ muktiḥ sambhavati iti tad artham īśvara ārādhanam asaṅgatam āsajyeta 
TBV_8.34^2	 yat api kāryam śarīreṇa vinā karoti iti naḥ sādhyam tat sva śarīra gatam anya gatam na iti na anena kiñcid iti tat api asāram śarīra vyatirekeṇa kārya karaṇa adarśanāt sva śarīra pravṛtti svarūpe api kārye tad śarīra sambaddhasya eva vyāpārāt atas acetanaḥ katham bhāvaḥ tad icchām anuvartate iti dūṣaṇam vyavasthitam eva acetanasya śarīra ādeḥ śarīra asambaddha icchā mātra anuvartana adarśanāt tad asambaddhasya icchāyāḥ api abhāvāt muktasya iva kutas tad anuvartanam acetana kāryeṇa 
TBV_8.34^3	 atha adṛṣṭā api icchā aśarīrasya sthāṇoḥ parikalpyate kim iti bhūruha ādikam kāryam kartṛ vikalam sṛṣṭam pai na kalpyate etena īśvarasya api prayatna sadbhāve na kācid kṣatiḥ iti nirastam śarīra abhāve mukta ātmanaḥ iva prayatna asambhavāt apara śarīra rahita sva śarīra avayava preraṇa prayatna sadbhāvaḥ api na śarīra abhāve prayatna sadbhāvā vedakaḥ sarvathā śarīra rahitasya tasya kvacid api adarśanāt dṛṣṭa anusāriṇyaḥ ca kalpanāḥ bhavanti tatas sthāvareṣu śarīra abhāvāt na tad kartuḥ anupalabdhiḥ kintu kartuḥ abhāvāt iti katham na taiḥ kārya tva ādeḥ hetoḥ vyabhicāraḥ 
TBV_8.35^1	 na ca yathādṛṣṭasya indriyasya ca anvaya vyatirekayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva vyavasthāpakayoḥ abhāve api kāraṇa tva siddhiḥ vyatireka mātrāt tathā maheśvarasya api tatas tad siddhiḥ tasya nitya vyāpaka tva abhyupagamena vyatireka asambhavāt atas na vyāpti siddhiḥ kāryatva ādeḥ tad sādhaka tvena upanyastasya hetoḥ atas eva na sat pratipakṣatā api na ekasmin sādhya anvite hetau sthite dvitīyasya tathāvidhasya tatra avakāśaḥ iti satyam kintu sthāṇu sādhakasya karyatva ādeḥ sādhya anvita tvam eva na sambhavati iti pratipāditam yat ca uktam na api bādhā abuddhimat kāraṇa pūrvakatvasya pramāṇena agrahaṇāt iti tat asāmpratam buddhimat kāraṇa pūrvaka tva abhāva pratipādakasya pramāṇasya aṅkura ādau akṛṣṭa utpattau sadbhāvāt 
TBV_8.35^2	 atha aṅkura ādi kartuḥ atīndriya tvāt na pratyakṣāt tad abhāva siddhiḥ na pratyakṣāt tad abhāva asiddhau api anumānasya tatra tad abhāva grāhakasya bhāvāt tathā hi yat yasya anvaya vyatirekau na anuvidhatte na tat tad kāraṇam yathā na paṭa ādayaḥ kulāla kāraṇāḥ na anuvidadhati ca aṅkura ādayaḥ buddhimat kāraṇa anvaya vyatirekau iti vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ yat ca yat kāraṇam tat tasya anvaya vyatirekau anuvidhatte yathā ghaṭa ādayaḥ kulālasya na ca upalabdhimat kāraṇa sannidhāne prāc anupalabdhasya aṅkura ādeḥ upalambhaḥ tad abhāve ca apara kāraṇa sākalye api tasya anupalambhaḥ iti anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānam aṅkura ādi kāryāṇām 
TBV_8.36	 atha aṅkura ādi kartuḥ upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta tvasya abhāvāt na pratyakṣeṇa sa bhāva abhāva pratītiḥ iti na aṅkuradeḥ tad anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānasya upalabdhiḥ yuktāḥ nanu mā bhūt tad anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāna upalabdhiḥ vyatireka anuvidhāna upalabdhiḥ tu yuktāḥ yathā rūpa āloka manaskāra sākalye api kadācid vijñāna kārya anutpattyā kāraṇa antarasya api tatra sāmarthyam avasīyate yat ca tad kāraṇa antaram sā indriya śaktiḥ tad abhāvāt rūpa jñānam na san jātam iti anupalabhya svabhāvasya api kāraṇasya vyatirekaḥ kāryeṇa anuvidhīyamānaḥ upalabhyate 
TBV_8.37	 na deha upalabdhimat kāraṇasya vyatirekaḥ aṅkura ādi kāryeṇa anuvidhīyamānaḥ upalabhyate buddhimat kāraṇa vyatirikta pṛthivī ādi sāmagrī sākalye aṅkura ādeḥ avāśya aṃbhāva darśanāt indriya śakteḥ anitya tva avyāpaka tvena vyatireka sambhavāt tad vyatireka anuvidhānasya upalabdhiḥ yuktāḥ na buddhimat kāraṇa vyatireka anuvidhānasya tasya nitya tva vyāpaka tvena vyatireka anuvidhāna abhāvāt iti ced astu nāma evam tathā api īśvarasya jñāna prayatna cikīrṣā samavāyaḥ aṅkura ādi kārya karaṇe vyāparaḥ tasya sarvadā sarvatra abhāvāt tad anuvidhānam syāt 
TBV_8.38^1	 atha tad samavāyasya api sarvatra sarvadā bhāvāt na ayam doṣaḥ na tasya nitya tva vyāpaka tve sati api tad viśeṣaṇānām īśvara jñāna prayatna cikīrṣā ādīnām anitya tvāt avyāpaka tvāt ca vyatireka anuvidhānam upalabhyeta atha tad jñāna ādeḥ api nitya tvāt na ayam doṣaḥ sarvadā tarhi aṅkura ādi kārya utpattiḥ syāt sarvadā sahakāriṇām asannidhānāt na iti ced nanu te api tat jñāna ādi āyatta janmānaḥ kim na sarvadā sannidhīyante atha na eva te tad āyatta utpattayaḥ tarhi taiḥ eva kāryatva ādi hetuḥ anaikāntikaḥ tad sahakāriṇām api sarvadā sva utpatti hetūnām sa kāryāṇām asannidhānāt na sarvadā utpadyante iti ced anavasthā tathā ca apara apara sahakāri pratīkṣāyām eva upakṣīṇa śakti tvāt tad jñāna ādeḥ prakṛta kārya kartṛ tvam na kadācid api syāt atas su dūram api gatvā kvacid avasthām icchatā nitya tvam sahakāriṇām atadāyatta utpattika tvam vā abhyupagamanīyam tad āyatta utpatti kāryasya api tad jñāna ādi vyatirekeṇa api utpattiḥ abhyupagantavyāḥ iti vṛthā tad parikalpanā 
TBV_8.38^2	 nitya tve vā punar api sahakāriṇām tad jñāna ādīnām ca nitya tvāt sarvadā kārya utpatti prasaṅgaḥ tat evam tad jñāna ādīnām ca nitya tvāt sarvadā kāryasya utpattiḥ anutpattiḥ vā syāt iti anityāḥ tat jñāna ādayaḥ abhyupagantavyāḥ tathā ca sati tad anya sāmagrī sākalye api aṅkura ādi anutpattiḥ kadācid syāt sakala tad anya sāmagrī sannidhāna anantaram eva tad jñāna ādi utpattiḥ syāt te tu sahakāriṇaḥ tad jñāna ādya preritāḥ eva tad jñāna ādi janayantaḥ aṅkura ādi janayanti kim antarga ḍuta jñāna ādi kalpanayā tad jñāna ādi saha kṛtāḥ eva tad jñāna ādikam janayanti iti abhyupagame tad jñāna ādi antaram sahakāri kāraṇa janyam ajanya tvāt tad anantaram anutpadyamānam kāryam api tad jñāna ādikam tad anantaram na utpādayati iti āyātaḥ saḥ eva kāraṇa antara sākalye api aṅkura ādi kārya ādi anutpatti prasaṅgaḥ saha kāribhyaḥ tad jñāna ādi antara utpattau saḥ eva prasaṅgaḥ anavasthā ca 
TBV_8.38^3	 tasyām ca apara apara jñāna utpādanaḥ iva sahakāriṇām sarvadā upayogāt na kārye kadācid api upayogaḥ bhavet saha kāribhiḥ saha tad jñāna ādikam niyamena utpattimat iti ced tarhi sahakāriṇām tad jñāna ādeḥ ca eka sāmagrī adhīna tvam abhyupagantavyam anyathā sahabhāvāt tathā eka sāmagrī lakṣaṇam kāraṇam tad jñāna ādibhiḥ anyaiḥ janitam ajanitam vā tat janayati na ca ajanitam tathā eva kārya tva ādeḥ hetoḥ vyabhicāri tva prasaṅgāt janitam tad jñāna ādikam abhyupagantavyam tat ca tena janyena saha niyamena utpadyamānam tad eka sāmagrī adhīna tvam abhyupanantaram sāmagrī adhīnam syāt sā ca sāmagrī tad jñāna antareṇa utpāditā ca iti vikalya dvaye pūrva ukta doṣa dvaya prasaṅgaḥ 
TBV_8.38^4–8.39	 prāk anantara utpatti niyama abhyupagame sahakāri hetubhiḥ eka sāmagrī adhīna tayā syāt tatra api sā ekasāmagrī tad jñāna ādi antareṇa preritā janayati iti abhyupeyam anyathā acetanasya acetana anadhiṣṭitasya vā asya ādeḥ iva janakatvā sambhavāt jñāna ādi antaram ca preryāt sāmagrī viśeṣāt prāc antaram niyamena utpadyamānam tat hetubhiḥ eka sāmagrī adhīnam syāt anyathā prāk anantaram niyamena utpattiḥ na syāt sāmagryantaram ca preritam apreritam vā janayati iti vikalpa dvaye doṣa dvasya prasaṅgaḥ tena imam doṣam parijihīrṣatā na tad jñāna ādi utpattiḥ tad anantaram saha prāk vā anantaram abhyupagantavyā tad anantaram saha prāk vā anantaram utpatti niyama abhāve api ca aṅkura ādi kāryasya tad vyatireka anuvidhānam upalabhyeta na ca upalabhyate kṣiti udaka bīja ādi kāraṇa sāmagrī sannidhāne pratibandhe ca asati aṅkura ādi kāryasya avaśyaṃbhāva darśanāt atas tad jñāna ādi anuvidhānasya tad kāraṇa tva vyāpakasya anupalambhāt tad kāraṇa tva abhāvaḥ aṅkura ādi kāryasya anumīyate atas bādhā vyāpaka an upalabdhyā buddhimat kāraṇa anumānasya 
TBV_8.40^1	 buddhimat kāraṇa anumānena eva vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ kasmāt na bādhyate lohalekyam vajram pārthiva tvāt kāṣṭha vat iti anumānena pratyakṣam tasya tad alekhya tva grāhakam kim na bādhyate iti samānam pratyakṣeṇa tad viṣayasya bādhita tvāt na tena tat bādhyate iti ced buddhimat kāraṇa tva anumānasya api tarhi vyāpaka anupalabdhyā viṣayasya bādhita tvāt katham tat bhādhaka tvam buddhimat kāraṇa tva anumānena eva vyāpaka anupalabdheḥ viṣayasya bādhita tvāt na tat bādhaka tvam iti ced na pārthiva tva anumānena tad lekhya tva grāhakasya pratyakṣasya bādhita viṣaya tvāt na tat bādhaka tvam iti api vaktum śakya tvāt atha tad anumānasya tad ābhāsa tvāt na prakṛta pratyakṣa viṣaya bādhaka tvam na etat itaretara āśraya doṣa prasaṅgāt tathā hi pratyakṣa bādhita viṣaya tvāt tad anumānasya tad ābhāsa tvam tasya tad ābhāsa tvāt pratyakṣasya tad abādhita viṣaya tvena atad ābhāsa tvāt tad viṣaya bādhaka tvam iti vyaktam itaretara āśraya tvam 
TBV_8.40^2	 atha anumāna ābādhita viṣaya tva nibandhanam na tad pratyakṣasya atad ābhāsa tvam kim tarhi sva paricchedya avyabhicāra nibandhanam nanu evam anumānasya api sva sādhya avyabhicāra nibandhanam kim na atad ābhāsa tvam api abhyupagama viṣayaḥ atha ābādhita viṣaya tve sati tasya tat eva sva sādhya avyabhicāri tvam parisamāpyate nanu evam abādhita viṣaya tvasya pratipattum aśakteḥ na kvacid api sva sādhya avyabhicāritvasya anumāne atad ābhāsa tva nibandhanasya prasiddhiḥ na hi bādha anupalambhāt bādhā bhāvaḥ tasya vidyamāna bādhakeṣu api anutpanna bādhaka pratipattiṣu bhāvāt atha yatra bādhaka sadbhāvaḥ tatra prāk bādhaka anupalambhe api uttara kālam avaśyaṃbhāvinī bādhaka upalabdhiḥ yatra tu na kadācid bādhaka upalabdhiḥ tatra na tad bhāvaḥ asat etat na hi arvāk dṛśā bādhaka anupalambha mātreṇa na kadācana api atra bādhaka upalabdhiḥ bhaviṣyati iti jñātum śakyam sva sambandhinaḥ anupalambhasya anaikāntika tvāt sarva sambandhinaḥ asiddha tvāt na hi asarva vid sarveṇa api atra bādhakam na upalabhyate upalapsyate vā iti avasātum kṣamaḥ 
TBV_8.40^3	 na api bādhaka abhāvaḥ abhāva grāhi pramāṇa avaseyaḥ tasya niṣiddha tvāt niṣetsyamāna tvāt ca na ca ajñātaḥ bādhaka abhāvaḥ anumāna aṅgam pakṣa dharma tva ādi vat na ca sva sādhya avyabhicāri tva niścayāt eva bādhaka abhāva niścayaḥ tat niścayam antareṇa tvad abhiprāyeṇa sva sādhya avyabhicāri tvasya aparisamāpta tvena niścaya ayogāt tasmāt pakṣa dharma tva anvaya vyatireka niścaya lakṣaṇa svasādhya avinābhāvi tvasya prakṛta anumāne api sadbhāvāt pratyakṣa vat na tasya api tad ābhāsa tvam atha viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇa abhāvāt pārthiva tva anumānasya na antar vyāptiḥ iti tad ābhāsa tvam evam tarhi kāryatva anumāne api viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇa abhāvāt vyāpti abhāvataḥ tad ābhāsa tvam iti na vyāpaka anupalabdhi viṣaya bādhaka tā 
TBV_8.40^4	 atha pratyakṣam na anumānena bādhyate iti loha lekhya tva anumānasya na tad lekhya tva grāhaka pratyakṣa bādhaka tā katham tarhi diśa antara prāpti liṅga janita anumānena sthira candra arka grāhi pratyakṣasya bādhā atha tasya pratyakṣa ābhāsa tvāt anumānena bādhā nanu kutas tasya tad ābhāsaḥ tvam anumānena bādhita viṣaya tvāt iti ced nanu tat eva itaretara āśraya tvam anumānena bādhita viṣaya tvāt tasya tad ābhāsa tvam tasya tad ābhāsa tve ca tena abhādhita viṣaya tvāt anumānasya atad ābhāsa tvena tad viṣaya bādhaka tvam iti vyaktam itaretara āśraya tvam tasmāt sva grāhya avyabhicāraḥ eva sarvatra prāmāṇya nibandhanam sa ca vyāpaka anupalabdhau pakṣa dharma anvaya vyatireka svarūpaḥ pramāṇa pariniścitaḥ vidyate iti tasyāḥ eva sva sādhya pratipādaka tvena prāmāṇyam na punar buddhimat kāraṇa anumānasya tatra sva sādhya avyabhicāra abhāvasya pradarśita tvāt 
TBV_8.41	 na ca vyāpaka anupalabdhau api pakṣa dharma tva anvaya vyatireka niścayasya sva sādhya avyabhicāri tva niścaya lakṣaṇasya abhāvaḥ iti vaktum yuktam yatas vyāpaka anupalabdheḥ tāvat pakṣa vyāpaka tva niścayaḥ prāk eva uktaḥ vipakṣe bādhaka pramāṇa sadbhāvāt anvaya vyatirekau api tatra avagamyete tad kāraṇeṣu hi kumbha ādiṣu tata nvaya vyatireka anuvidhānasya upalabdhiḥ tat anupalabdheḥ bādhakam pramāṇam atha vā tad kāraṇa tvam tad anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānena vyāptam tad abhāve tad kāraṇatva asambhavāt tad abhāve api bhavataḥ tad kāraṇa tve sarvam sarvasya kāryam kāraṇam ca syāt na kvacid kārya kāraṇa bhāva vyavasthā 
TBV_8.42	 anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānam hi kārya kāraṇa bhāva vyavasthā nibandhanam tad abhāve api kārya kāraṇa bhāvam kalpayataḥ kim anyat tad vyavasthā nibandhanam syāt iti atas ati vyāpti parihāreṇa kvacid eva kārya kāryaṇa bhāva vyavasthām icchatā tad abhāve kārya kāryaṇa bhāvaḥ na abhyupagantavyaḥ iti anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānena kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ vyāptaḥ sa yatra upalabhyate tatra anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāna sannidhāpanena tad abhāvam bādhataḥ iti anumana siddhaḥ vyatirekaḥ tad siddheḥ ca anvayaḥ api siddhaḥ tathā hi yaḥ eva sarvatra sādhya abhāve sādhana abhāva lakṣaṇaḥ vyatirekaḥ saḥ eva sādhana sadbhāve avaśya tayā sādhya sadbhāva svarūpaḥ anvayaḥ iti vyāpaka anupalabdheḥ pakṣa dharma tva anvaya vyatireka lakṣaṇaḥ sādhya avyabhicāraḥ pramāṇataḥ siddhaḥ na ca evam kāryatva ādeḥ ayam avinā abhavaḥ sambhavati pakṣa vyāpaka tve sati anvaya vyatirekayoḥ abhāvasya viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇa abhāvataḥ pratipādita tvāt 
TBV_8.43^1	 api ca buddhimat kāraṇa tve tanu ādīnām sādhye tad viparyayaḥ abuddhimat kāraṇāḥ paramāṇu ādayaḥ na ca tebhyaḥ buddhimat kāraṇa sādhya vyāvṛtti nimitta kārya tva ādi vivṛtti pratipādaka pramāṇa pravṛttiḥ siddhāḥ ghaṭa ādeḥ avayavi tu a nirākaraṇena viśiṣṭa avasthā prāpta paramāṇu rūpa tvāt na ca tebhyaḥ buddhimat kāraṇa vyāvṛtti kṛtā kāryatva vyāvṛttiḥ pratyakṣatas siddhāḥ buddhimat kāraṇa nimitta kāryatva grāhaka tvena pratyakṣasya pratyakṣa anupalambha śabda vācyasya tatra pravṛtteḥ paramāṇu antarā saṃsṛṣṭa paramāṇūnām ca pratyakṣa buddhau apratibhāsanān na tatas sādhya vyāvṛtti prayuktā sādhana vyāvṛtti pratipattiḥ 
TBV_8.43^2	 na api abuddhimat kāraṇeṣu kārya tva ādeḥ adarśanāt sa akalpena tatas vyatireka siddhiḥ dvasambandhinaḥ adarśanasya para cetaḥ vṛtti viśeṣaiḥ anaikāntika tvāt sarva sambandhinaḥ asiddha tvāt na tatas vipakṣāt dhetoḥ vyāptyā vyatireka siddhiḥ na api paramāṇu ādīnām anumānāt nitya tva siddheḥ kāryatvasya karyatva viruddhasya teṣu sat bhavāt tatas vyāvartamānaḥ kāryatva lakṣaṇaḥ hetu buddhimat kāraṇa tvena anvitaḥ sidhyati kāryatvasya abuddhimat kāraṇa tvena virodha asiddheḥ aṅkura ādiṣu abuddhimat kāraṇa niṣpādyeṣu api tasya sambhavāt atha nityebhyaḥ akṛta tvāt eva kārya tvam vyāvṛttam utpattimatām sa aṅkura ādīnām buddhimat kāraṇa pūrvaka tvea pakṣīkṛta tvāt na taiḥ hetoḥ vyabhicāra āśaṅkanīyaḥ iti teṣu vartamānaḥ kāryatva lakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ buddhimat kāraṇa tvena anvitaḥ sidhhaḥ 
TBV_8.43^3	 syāt etat yadi pakṣīkaraṇa mātreṇa envābuddhimat kāraṇa tva abhāvaḥ teṣu siddhaḥ syāṭ tathā abhyupagame vā pakṣīkaraṇāt eva sādhya siddheḥ hetu upādānam vyartham atha tad sahitāt sādhya nirdeśāt tad abhāva siddhiḥ katham sākalyena aniścita vyatirekāt kāryatvāt nitya vyatiriktānām sarveṣām aṅkura ādīnām abuddhimat kāraṇa tva abhāva siddhiḥ tad abhāva asiddhau ca na sākalyena vyatireka niścayaḥ iti itaretara āśraya doṣaḥ katham na syāt tat evam vyāptyā vyatireka asiddhau na sākalyena anvaya siddhiḥ tad asiddhau ca na vyatireka sidhdiḥ iti na kāryatva ādeḥ hetoḥ prakṛta sādhya sādhaka tvam 
TBV_8.43^4	 na ca sarva anumāṇeṣu eṣa doṣaḥ samānaḥ anyatra viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇa balāt anvaya vyatireka siddheḥ na ca prakṛte hetau tat asti iti asat kṛt āveditam tena sādhya abhāve hetoḥ abhāvaḥ sva sādhya vyāpta tvāt eva siddhaḥ iti nirastam yathā ukta prakāreṇa sva sādhya vyāpta tvasya prakṛta hetoḥ asambhavāt na api dharmya siddha tā iti etat api nirastam dharmya siddha tvasya prāk pratipādita tvāt kārya kāraṇa saṅghāt iti ādikaḥ tu granthaḥ ayukta tvena pratipāditaḥ atas eva īśvara avagame pramāṇa abhāvaḥ tad pratipādaka pramāṇasya samāna doṣa tvena anyasya api acetana upādāna tva ādeḥ nirākṛta tvāt 
TBV_8.44	 yat ca uktam na api hetoḥ viśeṣa viruddha tā ityādi tat api asaṅgatam yatas yadi kārya mātrāt kāraṇa mātram tanu ādeḥ sādhyate tadā vyāpti sidhheḥ na viruddha avakāśaḥ atha buddhimat kāraṇa pūrvaka tvam sādhyate tadā tatra vyāpteḥ asiddha tvam pratipāditam eva yadi punar ghaṭa ādau kārya tvam buddhimat kāraṇa sahacaritam upalabdham iti pṛthivī ādau api tat sādhyate tathā sati dṛṣṭānte anīṣu arā sarvajña kṛtrima jñāna śarīra sambandhi kartṛ pūrvaka tvam kāryatvasya upalabdham iti tatas tādṛś bhūtam eva kṣiti ādau sidhim āsādayati na tu tad sahacarita tvena adṛṣṭam īśvara tva ādi viruddha dharma kalāpa upeta buddhimat kāraṇa pūrvaka tvam na hi mahānasa pradeśe agni sahacaritam upalabdham dhūma mātram giri śikhara ādau= upalabhyamānam agni viruddha dharma adhyāsita udaka gamakam yuktam atiprasaṅgāt 
TBV_8.45^1	 yat ca uktam pūrva ukta viśeṣaṇānām dharmi viśeṣa rūpāṇām vyabhicārāt ityādi tat api asaṅgatam yādṛś bhūtam hi kārya tvam ghaṭa ādau anīśvara ādi dharma upeta buddhimat kāraṇa tvena vyāptam upalabdham tādṛś bhūtam tat anyatra api jīrṇa prāsāda ādau upalabhyamānam akriyā darśinaḥ api tathābhūta kartṛ pūrvakatva pratipattim janyati na ca tatra kenacid anīśvara tva ādi dharmeṇa vyabhicāraḥ kadācid kena api upalabhyate tathābhūta sādhyavyāpta hetu upalambhaḥ eva tatra tat avyabhicāraḥ sa ced asti katham anīśvara tva ādi dharmāṇām vyabhicārāt asādhya tvam sacetasā vaktum yuktam anyathā dhūmāt agni pratipattau api bhāsvara rūpa sambandha ādi dharmāṇām vyabhicārāt tathābhūtasya agneḥ asādhya tvam syāt 
TBV_8.45^2	 etena pūrvasmāt dhetoḥ sva sādhya siddhau uttareṇa pūrva siddhasya eva sādhyasya kim viśeṣaḥ sādhyate āhosvit pūrva hetoḥ sva sādhya sidddhi pratibandhaḥ kriyate ityādi sarvam nirastam yatas yadi kāryatva mātram hetu tvena kṣityā asau sādhya sādhaka tvena upādīyate tadā tasya sandhigdha vipakṣa vyāvṛttika tvena buddhimat kāraṇa pūrvakatva asādhaka tvam atha ghaṭa ādau buddhimat kāraṇa tvena vyāptam yat kārya tvam tat tatra hetu tvena upādīyate tat tatra asiddham iti katham tat tatra buddhimat kāraṇa tvasya api gamakam iti aviśiṣṭasya kāryatvasya vyāpti abhāvāt eva apara viśiṣṭa sādhaka hetu vyāpāram antareṇa api kāryatvasya hetoḥ sva sādhya sādhaka tva vyāghātaḥ sambhavati eva kāryatva viśeṣasya tu tatra asiddha tvāt eva sādhya asiddhi lakṣaṇaḥ tad vighātaḥ 
TBV_8.46^1	 yat tu śabdasya kṛtaka tvāt anitya tva siddhau hetu antareṇa guṇa tva siddhau api na pūrvasya kṣatiḥ iti tat api acāru guṇa tvam hi dravya āśrita tva ādi dharma yukta tvam ucyate tat ced śabde siddhim āsādayati tadā pūrva hetu sādhitam anitya tvam tatra vyāhanyate eva na hi anutpannasya tasya asattvāt eva dravya āśrita tvam guṇa tva samavāyaḥ vā sambhavati utpannasya api utpatti anantara dhvaṃsi tvena tat na sambhavati na ca tad āśritasya utpatti ādikam eva tat khara viśāṇa ādeḥ api tattva prasaṅgāt ityādi āśraya ādau asiddhatvam hetoḥ pratipādayadbhiḥ nirṇītam iti na punar ucyate sarvathā utpādaka kāraṇa vyakti vyatiriktasya kṣaṇa mātra sthiteḥ guṇa tvam na sambhavati tad sambhave ca kṣaṇika tvam vyāhanyate iti pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ 
TBV_8.46^2	 dvitīye tu vikalpe na ca dharmi viśeṣa viparyaya udbhāvanena kasyacid api rūpasya abhāvaḥ kathyate iti yat uktam tat api asaṅgatam yatas yadi anyādṛśasya dharmiṇaḥ kutaścid dhetoḥ kṣityā asau siddhiḥ syāt tadā yujyeta api vaktum dharmi viśeṣa viparyaya udbhāvanena na kasyacid dhetu rūpasya abhavaḥ iti tathābhūtasya tu dharmiṇaḥ na prakṛta sādhanāt avagamaḥ iti pratipāditam atas eva āgamāt hetu antarāt vā na tatra viśeṣa siddhiḥ buddhimat kāraṇasya eva dharmiṇaḥ kṣiti ādi kartṛ tvena asiddhatvāt tatas tat ca anvaya vyatireki pūrvam kevala vyatireki saṃjñakam tat eva ca anvaya vyatireki lakṣaṇam pakṣa dharma tā prasādāt viśeṣa sādhanam iti pratipādanam dūra apāstam dharmya siddhau tad viśeṣa siddheḥ dūra utsārita tvāt atas eva yaḥ itthambhūtasya pṛthivī ādeḥ kartā niyamena asau akṛtrima jñāna sambandhī śarīra rahitaḥ sarvajña ekaḥ iti evam yadā viśeṣa siddhiḥ tadā na viśeṣa viruddhānām avakāśaḥ iti niḥsāra tayā vyavasthitam 
TBV_8.47–8.48^1	 yat tu uktam śarīra sambandhasya tāvat vyāpti abhāvena tatra nirākṛtiḥ śarīra antara rahitasya api ātmanaḥ śarīra dhāraṇa preraṇa kriyāsu yathā vyāpāraḥ tathā īśvarasya api kṣiti ādi kārye iti tat api ayuktam apara śarīra rahita tve api ātmanaḥ śarīra sambaddhasya eva tad dhāraṇa ādi kartṛ tva upalabdheḥ īśvarasya api śarīra sambaddhasya eva kārya kartṛ tvam abhyupagantavyam iti pratipādita tvāt yadi ca śarīra sambandha abhāve api tasya kṣiti ādi kārya kartṛ tvam tadā vaktavyam kim punar tat tatra jñāna cikīrṣā prayatnānām samavāyaḥ tat tatra uktam eva iti ced na samavāyasya niṣiddha tvāt 
TBV_8.47–8.48^2	 na ca kumbhakāra ādau śarīra sambandha vyatirekeṇa anyat kartṛ tvam upalabdham iti īśvare api tat eva parikalpanīyam dṛṣṭa anusāri tvāt kalpanāyāḥ na ca śarīra vyatirekeṇa jñāna cikīrṣā prayatnānām api sadbhāvaḥ kvacid api upalabdhaḥ iti na īśvare api tad abhāve asau abhyupagantavyaḥ tathā hi jñāna ādīnām utpattau ātmā samavāyi kāraṇam ātma manaḥ saṃyogaḥ asamavāyi kāraṇam śarīra ādi nimitta kāraṇam na ca kāraṇa traya abhāve pareṇa kārya utpattiḥ abhyupagamyate na ca asamavāyi kāraṇa ātma manaḥ saṃyoga ādi sadbhāvaḥ īśvare abhyupagataḥ iti na jñāna ādeḥ api tatra bhāvaḥ 
TBV_8.49	 atha asamavāyi kāraṇa ādeḥ abhāve api tatraḥ jñāna vyutpattiḥ tarhi nimitta kāraṇa īśvara vyatirekeṇa aṅkura ādeḥ kim iti na utpattiḥ yuktāḥ atha jñāna ādi abhāve tad anadhiṣṭhitānām katham acetanānām tad upādāna ādīnām pravṛṭtiḥ vā asya ādi vat acetanasya cetanā anadhiṣṭhitasya pravṛtti adarśanāt pravṛttau api nirabhiprāyāṇām deśa kāla ākāra niyamaḥ na syāt tat adhiṣṭhitasya eva tasya tat niyata tva darśanāt nanu evam cetanasya api cetanā antara anadhiṣṭhitasya karmakara ādeḥ iva svāmi anadhiṣṭhitasya katham pravṛttiḥ atha svāminaḥ eva anya an adhiṣṭhitasya cetanasya pravṛttiḥ upalabhyate kim aṅkura ādeḥ kṛṣṭa utpatteḥ upādānasya tad anadhiṣṭhitasya sā na upalabhyate atha ghaṭa ādeḥ upādānasya tad karaṇe pravṛttiḥ na upalabhyate iti aṅkura ādi upādānasya api tat adhiṣṭhitasya eva sā prasādhyate tarhi karmakara ādeḥ api svāmi anadhiṣṭhitasya sā na upalahyate iti svāminaḥ api apara cetana antara adhiṣṭhitasya sā sādhyatām yadi punar svāminaḥ api adhiṣṭātā cetanaḥ maheśaḥ parikalpyate tarhi tasya api aparaḥ iti anavasthā 
TBV_8.50^1	 na ca cetanasya api apara cetana adhiṣṭhitasya pravṛtti abhyupagame acetanam cetanā adhiṣṭitam iti prayoge acetanam iti dharmi viśeṣaṇasya acetana tva ādeḥ iti hetoḥ ca avyartham upādānam acetana vat cetanasya api cetanā adhiṣṭhitasya pravṛtti abhyupagame vyvacchedya abhāvāt na ca acetanānām api sva hetu sannidhi samāsādita utpattīnām cetanā adhiṣṭātṛ vyatirekeṇa api deśa kāla ākāra niyamaḥ anupapannah tat niyamasya sa hetu bala āyāta tvāt anyathā adhiṣṭhātṛ jñāna kṛtaḥ api sa na syāt 
TBV_8.50^2	 tat jñānasya sarva acetana adhiṣṭhāyaka tve kṣaṇika tve ca tat jñeya tvam eva tat adhiṣṭhita tvam teṣām sarva kāla bhāvi kārye tadā eva pravṛttiḥ iti eka kṣaṇaḥ eva uttara kāla bhāvi kārya utpatti prasaṅgaḥ aparakṣaṇe api tathābhūta tad jñāna sadbhāve punar api anantara kāla kārya utpattiḥ sadā eva iti yaḥ ayam krameṇa aṅkura ādi kārya sadbhāvaḥ sa viśīryeta katipaya acetana viṣaya tve ca tad jñāna ādeḥ tad aviṣayāṇām sva kārye pravṛttiḥ na syāt iti tad kārya śūnyaḥ sakalaḥ saṃsāraḥ prasaktaḥ na hi tad jñāna ādi viṣaya tva vyatirekeṇa aparam teṣām tat adhiṣṭhita tvam pareṇa abhyupagamyate atha nityam tad jñāna ādi nanu evam kṣaṇikam jñānam asmad ādi pratyakṣa tve sati vibhu dravya viśeṣa guṇa tvāt śabda vat iti atra prayoge maheśa jñānena hetoḥ vyabhicāraḥ 
TBV_8.51	 atha tad jñāna ādi vyatireke sati iti viśeṣaṇāt na ayam doṣaḥ na vipakṣa viruddha viśeṣaṇam hetoḥ tatas vyāvartakam bhavati anyathā tad vyāvartaka tva ayogāt na ca akṣaṇika tvena tad vyatirikta tvam viruddham dvi vidhyasya api virodhasya anayoḥ asiddheḥ na ca nipakṣa aviruddha viśeṣaṇa upādāna mātreṇa hetoḥ vyabhicāra parihāraḥ anyathā na kaścid hetuḥ vyabhicārī syāt sarvatra vyahicāra viṣaye etad vyatirikta tve sati iti viśeṣaṇasya upādātum śakya tvāt na ca naiyāyika matena akṣaṇikam jñānam sambhavati arthavat pramāṇam iti vacanāt artha kāryam jñānam tad viṣayam abhyupagatam arthaḥ ca krama bhāvī atītaḥ anāgataḥ ca yat ca kramavat jñeya viṣayam jñānam tat krama bhāvi yathā devadatta ādi jñānam jvālā ādi gocaram kramavat vijñeya viṣayam ca īśvara jñanam iti svabhāva hetuḥ 
TBV_8.52	 prasasṅga sādhanam ca idam tena āśraya asiddha tā hetoḥ na aśaṅkanīyāḥ na ca viparyae bādhaka pramāṇa abhāvāt vyāpya vyāpaka bhāva asiddheḥ na prasaṅga sādhana avakāśaḥ atra iti vaktavyam tasya bhāvāt tathā hi yadi kramavatā viṣayeṇa tat īśvara jñānam sva nirbhāsam janyate tadā siddham eva kramitvam atha na janyate tadā pratyāsatti nibandhana abhāvāt na tat jānīyāt viṣayam antareṇa api ca bhavataḥ prāmāṇyam abhyupagatam hīyeta atīta anāgate viṣaye nirviṣaya tu a prasaṅgāt iti viparyaya bādhaka sadbhāvaḥ siddhaḥ 
TBV_8.53	 tad jñāna ādeḥ ca nitya tve tad viṣaya tvam antareṇa aparasya cetana adhiṣṭhita tvasya abhāvāt avikala kāraṇasya jagataḥ yugapad utpatti prasaṅgaḥ tathā hi yat avikala kāraṇam tat bhavati eva yathā antya avasthā prāptāyāḥ sāmagryāḥ avikala kāraṇaḥ bhavan aṅkuraḥ avikala kāraṇam ca sarvadā sarvam īśvara jñāna ādi hetukam jagat iti yugapad bhavet 
TBV_8.54^1	 syāt etat na īśvara buddhi ādikam eva kevalam kāraṇam api tu dharma adharma ādi sahakari kāraṇam apekṣya tat tat karoti nimitta kāraṇa tvāt īśvara buddhi ādeḥ atas dharma ādiḥ sahakāri kāraṇasya vaikalyāt avikala kāraṇa tvam asiddham asat etat yadi hi tasya saha kāribhiḥ kaścid upakāraḥ kriyeta tadā syāt sahakāri savyapekṣata yāvatā nitya tvāt paraiḥ anādheya atiśayasya na kaścid tasya sahakāribhyaḥ prāptavyam asti kim iti tat tathābhūtān anupakāriṇaḥ apekṣeta kiñca te api sahakāriṇaḥ kim iti satatam na sannihitāḥ bhavanti yadi tad janyāḥ 
TBV_8.54^2	 apara sva sannidhi hetu saha kāri vaikalyāt iti na uttaram teṣām api tad sannidhi sahakāriṇām tadā ayāt ta utpattīnām tadā eva sannidhi prasakteḥ katham asiddha tā hetoḥ atha nitya tve tad buddhi ādikam sahakāri karaṇam utpādya paścāt aṅkura ādi kāryam upajanayati iti abhyupagamaḥ tarhi apara apara sahakāri janane eva upakṣīṇa śakti tvāt tasya na aṅkura ādi kārya jananam atha atat janyāḥ eva dharma adharma ādi sahakāriṇaḥ atas ayam adoṣaḥ nanu evam taiḥ eva acetana upādāna tvāt iti hetuḥ anaikāntikaḥ syāt atas tad āyatta sannidhayaḥ dharma ādi sahakāriṇaḥ iti na avikala kāraṇa tva ākhyaḥ hetuḥ asiddhaḥ
