TBV_8.55^1	 na ca anaikānntikaḥ api avikala kāraṇa tva hāni prasaṅgāt avikala kāraṇasya api anutpattau sarva dā eva anutpatti prasaṅgāt ca viśeṣa abhāvāt etena yat api udyota kareṇa uktam yadi api nityam īśvara ākhyam kāraṇam avikalam bhāvānām sannihitam tathā api na yugapad utpattiḥ īśvarasya buddhi pūrva kāri tvāt yadi hi īśvaraḥ sattā mātreṇa eva abuddhi pūrvam bhāvānām utpādakaḥ syāṭ tadā syāt etat codyam yadā tu buddhi pūrvam karoti tadā na doṣaḥ tasya sva icchayā kāryeṣu pravṛtteḥ atas anaikāntika tāiva hetoḥ iti tat api nirastam na hi kāryāṇām kāraṇasya icchā bhāva abhāva apekṣayā pravṛtti nivṛttī bhavataḥ yena apratibaddha sāmarthye api īśvara ākhye kāraṇe sadā sannihite tadīya it chā bhāvāt na pravarteran kim tarhi kāraṇa gata sāmarthya bhāva abhāva anuvidhāyinaḥ bhāvāḥ 
TBV_8.55^2	 tathā hi icchāvataḥ api kara caraṇa ādi vyāpāra akṣamāt kulāla ādeḥ asamarthāt na utpadyante ghaṭa ādayaḥ bhāvāḥ samarthāt ca bīja ādeḥ anicchāvataḥ api samutpadyamānāḥ upalabhyante aṅkura ādayaḥ tatra yat īśvara ākhyam kāraṇam kārya utpāda kāla vat apratihata śakti sadā eva avasthitam bhāvānām tat kim iti tadīyām anupakāriṇīm tām icchām apekṣante yena utpāda kāla vat yugapad na eva utpadyeran evam hi taiḥ avikala kāraṇa tvam ātmanaḥ darśitam bhavet yadi yugapad bhaveyuḥ na ca api īśvarasya paraiḥ anupakāryasya kācid apekṣā asti yena ucchām apekṣeta na ca buddhi viśeṣa vyatirekeṇa aparā icchā tasya sambhavati 
TBV_8.56^1	 buddhiḥ ca īśvarasya yadi nityā vyāpikā ekā ca abhyupagamyeta tadā sā eva acetana padārtha adhiṣṭhātrī bhaviśyati iti kim apara tad ādhāra īśvara ātma parikalpanayā atha anāśritam tajñānam na sambhavati iti tad ātma parikalpanā nanu tad ā ātmā api anāśritaḥ na sambhavati iti apara apara āśraya parikalpanayā ananteśvara prasaṅgaḥ atha dravya tvāt tasya anāśritasya api sadbhāvaḥ na buddheḥ guṇa tvāt iti na ayam doṣaḥ nanu kutas tasyāḥ guṇa tvam tatra samaveta tvāt iti na uttaram taysā eva aniścayāt tad ādheya tvāt tasyāḥ tad samaveta tvam iti ced nanu kena etat pratīyate 
TBV_8.56^2	 na tāvat īśvareṇa tena ātmanaḥ jñānasya ca agrahaṇāt idam atra samavetam iti tasya pratīteḥ ayogāt tat jñānasya tatra samaveta tvam eva tad grahaṇam iti api na uttaram anyonya saṃśrayāt siddhe hi idam atra iti grahaṇe tatra samaveta tva siddhiḥ asyāḥ ca tad grahaṇa siddhiḥ iti anyonya āśrayaḥ tat na īśvaraḥ tat jñānam ātmani samavetam avaiti yaḥ ca ātmīyam api jñānam ātmani vyavasthitam na vetti sa sarva jagat upādāna sahakāri kāraṇa ādikam avagamayiṣyati iti kaḥ śraddhātum arhati 
TBV_8.56^3	 na api tat jñānam avaiti sthāṇau aham samavetam iti tena ātmanaḥ avedanāt ādhārasya ca na ca tad grahaṇe idam mama rūpam atra sthitam iti pratītiḥ sambhavati na ca tat ātmānam api avaiti asva saṃvidita tva abhyupagamāt na ca aparam tat grāhakam nityam jñānam tasya īśvarasya api sambhavati yena ekena sakalam padārtha jātam avagamayati apariṇa tu tat jñānam samāna kālam yāvat dravya bhāvi sajātīya guṇa dvayasya anyatra anupalabdheḥ tatra api tad kalpanā sambhavāt tad kalpane vā kartṛkam aṅkura ādi kāryam kim na kalpyeta 
TBV_8.56^4	 astu vā tatra yathoktam jñāna dvayam tathā api tayoḥ jñānayoḥ anyatareṇa sva grahaṇa vidhureṇa na sva ādhārasya na sahacarasya jñānasya na api anyasya gocarasya grahaṇam tathā hi yat sva grahaṇa vidhuram tat na anya grahaṇam yathā ghaṭa ādi sva grahaṇa vidhuram ca prakṛtam jñānam tatas anena sahacarasya agrahaṇāt katham tena asya grahaṇam tena api grahaṇa virahitena asya vedane tat eva vaktavyam iti na kasyacid grahaṇam iti na tad samaveta tvena tad buddheḥ guṇa tvam na api tad ādhārasya dravya tvam siddhim upagacchati 
TBV_8.57	 tasmāt nitya buddhi pūrvaka tve aṅkura ādīnām kim iti yugapad utpādaḥ na bavet īśvara vat tad buddheḥ api sadā sannihita tvāt anitya buddhi savyapekṣasya api īśvarasya acetana adhiṣṭhāyaka tvena jagat vidhātṛ tve tasya nitya tvena tad buddheḥ api sadā sannihita tvam avikala kāraṇayoḥ sarvadā sannihita tvāt yugapad aṅkura ādi kārya utpatti prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt buddhimat tvāt iti viśeṣaṇam akiñcitkaram eva iti na anā ekāntika tā hetoḥ 
TBV_8.58	 na ca api viruddha tā sa pakṣe bhāvāt na ca evam bhavati tasmāt viparyaya prayogaḥ yat yadā na bhavati na tat tadānīm avikala kāraṇam yathā kuśūla avasthita bīja avasthāyām anupajāyamānaḥ aṅkuraḥ na bhavati ca eka padārtha utpātti kāle sarvam viśvam iti vyāpakanupalabdhiḥ na ca siddha sādhya tā īśvarasya tat jñāna ādeḥ vā kāraṇa tve vikala kāraṇa tva anupapatteḥ prasādhita tvāt tat na nitya jñāna prayatna cikīrṣāṇām tad samavāyasya vā nityasya kartṛ tvam yuktam 
TBV_8.59^1	 tasmāt śarīra sambandhasya eva kumbhakāra ādau kartṛ tva vyāpaka tvena pratīteḥ tad abhāve kartṛ tvasya api vyāpyasya abhāva prasaṅgaḥ tat ca kvacid kara ādi vyāpāreṇa karaka prayoktṛ tva lakṣaṇam yathā kumbhakārasya daṇḍa ādi kāraṇa prayoktṛ tvam aparam vāc vyāpāreṇa yathā svāminaḥ karmakara ādi prayoktṛ tva svarūpam anyat ca prayatna vyāpāreṇa yathā jāgrataḥ sva śarīra avayava preraka tva svabhāvam kiñcid ca nidrā mada pramāda viśeṣeṇa tālu ādi kara ādi preraka tvam sarvathā śārīra sambandhaḥ eva kartṛ tvasya vyāpakaḥ sa ced īśvarāt nivartate sva vyāpyam api kartṛ tvam ādāya nivartate iti na tasya kartṛ tvam abhyupagantavyam iti prasaṅgaḥ 
TBV_8.59^2	 atha tasya jagat kartṛ tvam abhyupagamyate tadā śarīra sambandhaḥ kartṛ tva vyāpakaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ iti prasaṅga viparyayaḥ na ca kāraka śakti parijñāna lakṣaṇam tasya kartṛ tvam yena prasaṅga viparyayayoḥ vyāptya siddheḥ abhāvaḥ syāt kumbhakāra ādau mṛd daṇḍa ādi kāraka śakti parijñāne api śarīra vyāpāra abhāve ghaṭa ādi kārya kartṛ tva adarśanāt supta pramatta ādau ca tālu ādi kāraṇa parijñāna abhāve api tad vyāpāre prayatna lakṣaṇe sati tad preraṇa kārya karśanāt yat api abhidhāna mātreṇa viṣa apahāra ādi kārya kartṛ tvam tat api na jñāna mātra nibandhanam kintu śarīra sambandha avinābhūta viśiṣṭa ātma prayatna hetukam eva 
TBV_8.60–8.62^1	 api ca viśiṣṭa dharma adharma ādi upadeśa vidhāy īśvaraḥ sarvajña tvena mumukṣubhiḥ upāsyaḥ anyathaḥ ajña upadeśa anuṣṭhāne teṣām vipralambha śaṅkyā tatra pravṛttiḥ na syāt tat uktam jñānavān mṛgyate kaścid tad ukta pratipattaye ajña upadeśa karaṇe vipralambhana śaṅkibhiḥ tasya ca sarvajña tve sati api aśarīriṇaḥ vaktra abhāvāt upadeṣṭṛtvā sambhavaḥ iti tad kṛta tvena tad upadeśasya prāmāṇya āsidder na mumikṣūṇām tatra pravṛttiḥ syāt iti upadeśa kartṛ tve tasya śarīra sambandhaḥ api avaśyam abhyupagntavyaḥ vyāpya abhyupagamasya vyāpaka abhyupagamana antarīyaka tvāt śarīra sambandha abhāve tu vyāpyasya api upadeśa nidhātṛ tvasya abhāvaḥ iti prasaṅga viparyayau vyāpya vyāpaka bhāva prasādhakam ca pramāṇam tālu ādi vyāpāra abhāve api upadeśasya sadbhāve tasya tad hetuka tvam na syāt iti kārya kāaṇa bhāva prasādhakam prāk eva pradarśitam iti na punar ucyate 
TBV_8.62^2	 tat sthitam etat na śarīra abhāve maheśasya kartṛ tvam iti tena śarīra manaḥ sambandha abhāve prayatna buddhi ādeḥ abhāvāt īśvara sattā eva asiddhāḥ atas tad abhāve kasya viśeṣaḥ śarīra ādi yoga lakṣaṇaḥ sādhyate ityādi pūrva pakṣa vacanam niḥsāra tayā vyavasthitam prasaṅga viparyayoḥ nimitta bhūta vyāpti pradarśanasya vaihita tvāt yat api uktam jñāna cikīrśā prayatnānām samavāyaḥ asti īśvare te tu jñānāt asya tatra nityāḥ iti tat api ayukta tvena pratipāditam yat ca uktam tatra śarīra sambandhasya vyāpti abhāvāt asiddhiḥ tat api asat śarīra sambandhasya kartṛ tva vyāpaka tva pratipādanāt 
TBV_8.63	 yat api uktam na api asarvajña tvam viśeṣaḥ kulāla ādiṣu dṛṣṭaḥ tatra sādhyate ityādi tat api ayuktam kulāla ādeḥ ghaṭa ādi kāryasya upāsāna ādi abhijña tve karma ādi nimitta kāraṇa abhijñā tva prāpteḥ sarvajña ta prasaktiḥ iti vyartham apara īśvara sarvajña parikalpanam tad nirvartaka ati indriya adṛṣṭa parijñāna vat tasya api sakala padārtha parijñāna prasakteḥ atha adṛṣṭa aparijñāne api kulālaḥ mṛd piṇḍa daṇḍa ādi kati paya kāraka śakti parijñānāt eva ghaṭāḍi lakṣāṇam sva kāryam nirvartayati iti na sakala kārya kartṛ tva anyathā anupapattyā tasya atīndriya ādi aśeṣa padārtha jñātva lakṣaṇa sarvajña tva siddhiḥ 
TBV_8.64^1	 yat ca uktam kṣetrajñānām niyata artha viṣaya grahaṇam sarva vid adhiṣṭhitānām yathā pratiniyata śabda ādi viṣaya grāhakāṇām aniyata viṣaya sarva vid adhiṣṭhitānām jīvat śarīre ityādi tat api asaṅgatam yatas śabdha ādi viṣaya grāhakāṇām iti dṛṣṭānta tvena upanyāsaḥ yadi indriyāṇām tadā teṣām karaṇa tvāt vedana lakṣaṇa kriyā anāśraya tvcāt katham niyata śabda ādi viṣaya grahaṇam atha grahaṇa ādhāra tvena na teṣām niyata śabda ādi viṣaya grahaṇam kintu karaṇa tvena nanu evam kṣetrajñānām api viṣaya grahaṇe karaṇa tvam na kartṛ tvam iti ghaṭa ādi kulāla akartṛkam tad kāraṇa śakti parijñānena na siddham iti kutas tat dṛṣṭāntāt kṣiti ādeḥ jñāna ādhāra kartṛka tvam siddhim upagacchati 
TBV_8.64^2	 yadi punar jñāna samavāyā iva cakṣuḥ āḍīnām niyata viṣayāṇām kartṛ tve api aniyata viṣaya apara kṣetrajña kartṛ adhiṣṭhita tvam aṅgīkriyate tarhi cetanānām api kṣetrajñānām niyata viṣāyāṇām yathā paraḥ aniyata viṣayaḥ cetanaḥ adhiṣṭhātā tathā tasya api pratiniyata viṣaya tva kalpanāyām aparaḥ aniyata viṣayaḥ tad adhiṣṭhāta abhyupagantavyaḥ tasya api aparaḥ iti anavasthā prasaktiḥ tathā cetanānām api kṣetrajñānām yadā cetanaḥ adhiṣṭhātā abhyupagamyate tadā acetanam cetanā adhiṣṭhitam pravartate avetana tvāt vā asya ādi vat iti prayoge acetana grahaṇam dharmi hetu viśeṣaṇam na upādeyam syāt vyavacchedya abhāvāt 
TBV_8.65^1	 yat tu uktam bhavatu aniṣṭhā yadi tad prasādhakam pramāṇam kiñcid asti tāvataḥ eva anumāna siddha tvāt iti tat api asaṅgatam yatas pramāṇam antareṇa hetvābhāsāt yadi ekasya siddhiḥ abhyupagamyate aparasya api tatas eva sā kim na abhyupagamyate pramāṇa siddha tvam tu tāvataḥ api na asti aniṣṭhayā tad prasādhakasya pramāṇasya aprāmāṇyā saṃjanāt yat api uktam āgamaḥ api asmin vastuni vidyate ityādi tat api ayuktam āgamasya tad praṇīta tvena prāmāṇyam tad prāmāṇyāt ca tatas tad siddhiḥ iti itaretara āśraya prasakteḥ nityasya tu āgamasya prāmāṇyam vaiśeṣaiḥ na abhyupagatam īśvara kalpa nā vaii arthya prasaṅgāt na api anyeśvara kṛta tad āgamāt tad siddhiḥ tatra api tad kṛta tvena prāṃāṇye itaretara āśraya doṣāt apara īśvara praṇīta aparāgama kalpane api tat eva vaktavyam iti aniṣṭhā prasaktiḥ tat evam svarūpe arthe āgamasya prāmāṇye api na tatas īśvara siddhiḥ 
TBV_8.65^2	 yat tu uktam tasya ca sattā mātreṇa sva viṣaya grahaṇa pravṛttānām kṣetrajñānām adhiṣṭhāyaka tā yathā sphaṭika ādīnām upadhāna ākāra grahaṇa pravṛttānām savitṛ prakāśaḥ tat ayuktam sattā mātreṇa savitṛ prakāśasya api sphaṭika ādi adhiṣṭhāyaka tva asambhavāt tat asambhavaḥ ca ākāśa ādeḥ api sattā mātrasya sadbhāvāt tad adhiṣṭhāyaka tā syāt kintu savitṛ prakāśasya tad viśiṣṭa avasthā janaka tvena tat adhiṣṭhāyaka tvam tat ced kṣetrajñeṣu īśvarasya parikalpyate tadā teṣām tad kāryatā prasaktiḥ tathā ca yathā kṣetrajñānām ātma tve aviśiṣṭe api kārya tā tathā īśvarasya ātma tva aviśeṣāt kāryatā iti tad adhiṣṭhāyakaḥ aparaḥ tad kartrā abhyupagantavyaḥ tatra api aparaḥ iti anavasthā atha tasya kāryatve sati api anadhiṣṭhitasya eva sva kārye pravṛttiḥ tarhi jagat upādāna ādeḥ api tad anadhiṣṭhitasya pravṛttiḥ iti vyabhicārī adhiṣṭhātṛ sādhaka tvena upanyasyamānaḥ tena eva hetuḥ 
TBV_8.66^1	 api ca sattā mātreṇa tasya tad adhiṣṭhāyaka tve gaganasya iva na sarvajña tvam iti sarvajña tva sādhaka hetoḥ tad viparyaya sādhanāt viruddha tvam na ca sarva viṣaya jñāna samavāyāt tatra tasya eva sarvajña tvam na ākāśa ādeḥ iti vaktum yuktam samavāyasya niṣiddha tvāt sattve api nitya vyāpaka tvena akāṣa ādau api bhāva prasaṅgāt na ca samavāya aviśeṣe api samavāyinoḥ viśeṣaḥ iti vaktum śakyam tad viśeṣasya eva asiddhatvāt siddha tve api samavāya parikalpanā vaiyarthya prasaṅgāt iti pratipādayiṣyamāṇa tvāt na ca sattā mātreṇa tasya tad adhiṣṭhāyaka tve jñāna mātram api upayogi āstām sakala padārtha sārtha kāraka parijñānam 
TBV_8.66^2	 yat api uktam jñānasya svaviṣaya sadartha prakāśa tvam nāma svabhāvaḥ tasya anyathā bhāvaḥ kutas cit doṣa sadbhāvāt tat satyam eva yat ca uktam yat punar cakṣuḥ ādi anāśritam jñānam parasya siddham tad siddhau cakṣuḥ ādi anāśritasya jñānasya iva sukhasya api siddheḥ ānanda rūpa tā katham muktānām na saṅgacchate yena sukha ādi guṇa rahitam ātmanaḥ svarūpam muktiḥ iti abhyupagamam śobheta na ca rāga ādeḥ āvaraṇasya abhāvaḥ maheśe siddhaḥ yena tat jñānam anāvṛtam aśeṣa padārtha viṣayam tatra siddhim upagacchet tad svarūpasya eva asiddhatvāt tatra rāga ādi abhāva pratipādakasya avyabhicaritasya hetoḥ tvad abhyupagama vicāraṇayā dūra apāsta tvāt ca 
TBV_8.67^1	 yat tu uktam viparyāsa kāraṇāḥ rāga ādyayaḥ viparyāsaḥ ca adharma nimittaḥ na ca bhagavati adharmaḥ iti tat api asāram adharma vat dharmasya api tad hetoḥ ca samyak jñāna ādeḥ tatra asambhavasya pratipādita tvāt yat ca uktam rāga ādayaḥ iṣṭa aniṣṭa sādhdhaneṣu viṣayeṣu upajāyamānāḥ dṛṣṭāḥ na ca bhagavataḥ kaścid iṣṭa aniṣṭa asādhanaḥ viṣayaḥ avāpta kāma tvāt iti tat api asāram yatas yadi iṣṭa aniṣṭa sādhanaḥ na tasya kaścid viṣayaḥ katham tarhi asau iṣṭa aniṣṭa upādāna parivarjana artham pravartate buddhi pūrvikāyāḥ pravṛtteḥ heya upādeya jihāsā upāditsā pūrvaka tvena vyāpta tvāt tad abhāve api pravṛttau unmattaka pravṛtti vat na buddhi pūrvikeśvara pravṛttiḥ syāt heya upādeya jihāsā upāditse api anāpta kāma tvena vyāpte avāpta kāmasya heya upādeya jihāsā upāditsā anupapatteh 
TBV_8.67^2	 anāpta kāma tvam api anīśvara tvena vyāptam īśvarasya anāpta kāma tva ayogāt iti yatra buddhi pūrvikā pravṛttiḥ iṣyate tatra heya upādeya jihāsā upāditse avaśyam aṅgikartavye yatra ca te tatra anāpta kāma tvam yatra ca tat tatra anīśvara tvam iti prasaṅga sādhanam īśvara tve ca avāpta kāma tvam avāpta kāma tvāt ca na heya upādeya viṣaye tad dhāna upādāna icchā tad abhāve na buddhi pūrvikā pravṛttiḥ iti prasaṅga viparyayaḥ atas eva svatantra sādhana pakṣe yat āśraya asiddha tva ādi hetu doṣa udbhāvanam tat asaṅgatam vyāpti prasiddhi mātrasya eva atra upayogāt sā ca pratipāditā yā tu pravṛttiḥ śarīra ādi sarge sā krīḍā arthāḥ avāpta kāmānām eva ca krīḍā bhavati iti yat uktam tat asaṅgatam ratim avindatām eva krīḍā bhavati na ca rati arthī bhagavān duḥkha abhāvāt iti vārttika kṛtā eva pratipādita tvāt yat ca uktam na hi duḥkhitāḥ krīḍāsu pravartante iti tat prakrama anapekṣam vacanam duḥkha abhāve api krīḍāvatām rāga ādi āsakti nimitta iṣṭa sādhana viṣaya vyatirekeṇa tasya asambhavāt 
TBV_8.68^1	 yat ca kāruṇyāt tasya tatra pravṛttiḥ ityādi tat api anālocita abhidhanam na hi karuṇāvatām yātanā śarīra utpādaka tvena prāṇī gaṇa duḥkha utpādaka tvam yuktam na ca tathābhūta karma savyapekṣaḥ tathā teṣām duḥkha utpādakaḥ asau nimitta kāraṇa tvāt tasya iti vaktum yuktam tad karmaṇām īśvarān āyatta tve kāryatve ca tena eva kāryatva lakṣaṇasya hetoḥ vyahicāri tva prasaṅgāt tad kṛta tve vā karmaṇaḥ abhyupagamyamāne prathamam karma prāṇinām vidhāya punar tad upabhoga dvāreṇa tasya eva ksayam vidadhataḥ maheśasya aprekṣā kāritā prasaktiḥ na hi prekṣā pūrva kāriṇaḥ gopāla ādayaḥ api prayojana śūnyam vidhāya vastu dhvaṃsayanti tat na karuṇā pravṛttasya karma savyapekṣasya api prāṇi duḥkha utpādaka tvam yuktam kiñca prāṇi karma savyapekṣaḥ yadi asau prāṇinām duḥkha utpādakaḥ iti na kṛpālu tva vyāghātaḥ tarhi karma paratantrasya prāṇi śarīra utpādaka tve tasya abhyupagamyamāne varam tad phala upabhoktṛ sattvasya tad sa vyapekṣasya tad utpādaka tvam ahi upagantavyam evam adṛṣṭa īśvara parikalpanā parihṛtā bhavati 
TBV_8.68^2	 yathā prabhuḥ sevā bheda anurodhāt phala pradaḥ na aprabhuḥ tathā maheśvaraḥ api karma apekṣa phala pradaḥ na aprabhuḥ iti api ayuktam yatas yathā rājñaḥ sevā āyatta phala pradasya rāga ādi yogaḥ nairghṛṇyam sevā āyatta tā ca pratītā tathā īśasyā api etat sarvam abhyupagamanīyam anyathā bhūtasya anya parihāreṇa kvacid eva sevake sukha ādi pradatva anupapatteḥ tat evam karma paratantra tve tasya anīśa tvam karuṇā preritasya kartṛ tve sṛjet ca śubham eva saḥ iti vārttika kārīyat ūṣaṇasya vyavasthita tvam 
TBV_8.68^3	 yat ca nāraka tiryak ādi sargaḥ api akṛta prāyad śittānām tatratya duḥkha anubhave punar viśiṣṭa sthāna avāptau abhyudaya hetuḥ iti siddham duḥkhi prāṇi sṛṣṭau api karuṇayā pravartanam īśasya iti tat api prativihitam eva yatas karma prāṇinām duḥkha pradam vidhāya tad phala upabhoga vidhāna dvāreṇa kṣaya nimittam prāṇinām abhyudayam vidadhataḥ tasya aśuci sthāna patita gṛhīta prakṣālitam odaka tyāga vidhāyinaḥ na samāna buddhi tva prasaktiḥ api ca yadi prānikarma paravaśaḥ teṣām duḥkha ādikam tad kṣaya nimitta prāyaścitta kalpam upajanayati iti abhyupagamaḥ tadā tad karma kārya tvam tasya prasaktam tad kṛta upakāra abhāve tat apekṣyāḥ ayogāt upakārasya ca tad kṛtasya tad bhede tena sambandha ayogāt abhinnasya tad karane tasya eva karaṇam iti katham na tad kārya tvam 
TBV_8.69	 atha yat yadā yatra karma ādikam sahakāri kāraṇam āsādayati tena saha sambhūya tat tadā tatra sukha ādikam kāryam janayati eka kārya kāri tvam eva sahakāri tvam iti na kāryatva lakṣaṇaḥ tasya doṣaḥ nanu karma ādi sahakāri savyapekṣāḥ kārya janana svabhāvaḥ tasya karma ādi sahakāri sannidhānāt yadi prāk api asti tadā sahakāri sannidhāne api sva rūpeṇa eva asau kāryam nirvartayati 
TBV_8.70^1	 para rūpeṇa janaka tve sarvasya sva rūpeṇa ajanaka tvāt kārya anutpāda prasaṅgaḥ tasya ca avikalasya tad janana svabhāvasya bhāvāt uttara kāla bhāvi samasta kārya utpattiḥ tadā eva syāt tathā hi yat yadā yat janana samartham tat tadā tat janayati eva yathā antya avasthā prāptam bījam aṅkuram ajanane vā tadā tasya tad janana svabhāvam eva na syāt tad janana svabhāvaḥ ca karma ādi sāmagrya sannidhāne api eka svabhāva tayā abhyupagamyamānaḥ maheśaḥ iti svabhāva hetuḥ atha karma ādi sāmagrya bhāve tad svabhāvaḥ api asau vivakṣita kāryam na janayati na tarhi tad janaka svabhāvaḥ yaḥ hi yadā yat na janayati sa tad janaka svabhāvaḥ na bhavati yathā śāli bījam yava aṅkurasya atajjanakasya api tad svabhāva tve ati prasaṅgaḥ na janayati ca karma ādi sāmagrya bhāve vivakṣitam kāryam īśaḥ iti vyāpaka anupalabhdiḥ 
TBV_8.70^2	 atha karma ādi sāmagrya bhāve sa svabhāvaḥ tad apekṣa kārya janakatva lakṣaṇaḥ na asti tarhi svabhāva bhedāt katham na tasya bhedaḥ aparasya tad nibandhanasya abhāvāt tathā ca krama varti anekam aṅkura ādi kāryam na akrama eka īśvara vihitam iti na ekatvam tasya sidddhim āsādayati tat na sarvajña tva aśarīritvā eka tva ādi dharma yogaḥ tasya siddhim upaḍhaukate na api kṛtrima jñāna sambandhi tvam tat jñānasya pratyartha niyama abhāvāt ityādi yat uktam tat api nirastam nitya sarva padārtha viṣaya jñāna sambandhi tvasya tatra pratiṣiddha tvāt 
TBV_8.71^1	 yat ca yathā sthapati ādīnām mahā prāsāda ādi karaṇe eka abhiprāya niyamitānām aikamatyam tadvat atra api yadi kṣiti ādi aneka kārya karaṇe bahūnām niyāmakaḥ kaścid ekaḥ asti saḥ eva īśvaraḥ iti uktam tat api asaṅgatam yatas na hi ayam niyamaḥ ekena eva sarvam kāryam nirvartanīyam eka niyamitaiḥ vā bahubhiḥ iti anekadhā kārya kartṛ tva darśanāt tathā hi kvacid ekaḥ eva eka kāryasya vidhātā upalabhyate yathā kuvindaḥ kaścid ekasya paṭasya kvacid ekaḥ eva bahūnām kāryām yathā ghaṭa śarāva udañcanānām ekaḥ kulādaḥ kvacid anekaḥ api anekasya yathā ghaṭa paṭa śakaṭa ādīnām kulāla ādiḥ kvacid anekaḥ api ekasya yathā śibikā udvahana ādeḥ anekaḥ puruṣa saṅghātaḥ na ca prāsāda ādi lakṣaṇe api aneka sthapati ādi nirvartye avaśyaṃtaya eka sūtra dhāra niyamitānām teṣām tatra vyāpāraḥ upalabdhaḥ pratiniyata abhiprāyānām api eka sūtra dhārā niyamitānām tad karaṇa avirodhāt iti na ekaḥ kartā kṣiti ādīnām siddhim āsādayati 
TBV_8.71^2	 atas eva na tad nibandhanā sarvajña tva siddhiḥ api tasya yuktāḥ tat evam nitya tva ādi viśeṣa sākalya sādhaka anumāna asambhavāt tad viparyaya sādhakasya ca prasaṅga sādhanasya tatra bhāvāt katham na viśeṣa viruddha avakāśaḥ atha śarīra ādimat buddhimat kāraṇa tva vyāptam yadi kṣiti ādau kāryatvam upalabhyeta tadā tatas tatra tat siddhim āsādayat tathābhūtam eva sidhyet iti bhavet kāryatva ādeḥ viruddha tvam sādhya viparyaya sādhanāt na ca tathābhūta tat tatra vidyate iti katham viruddha tā na para prasiddha pakṣa dharma tvam viparyaya vyāptim na āśritya viruddha tā abhidhānāt paramārthataḥ tu kāryatva viśeṣasya kṣiti ādau asiddhatvam tad sāmānyasya tu anaikāntika tvam iti pratipāditam sarveṣu ca īśvara sādhanāya upanyasteṣu anumāneṣu asiddha tva ādi doṣaḥ samānaḥ iti karyatva dūṣaṇena eva tāni api dūṣitāni iti na pratyuccārya dūṣyante maheśvarasya ca nitya tvam tad vādibhiḥ abhyupagamyate na ca akṣaṇikasya sattvam sambhavati iti pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ 
TBV_8.72^1	 yat ca pṛthivī ādi mahābhūtāni svāsu kriyāsu buddhimat kāraṇa adhiṣṭhitāni pravartante anitya tvāt vā asya ādi vat iti tatra kulāla ādi buddhau api anitya tva lakṣaṇasya hetoḥ sadbhāvāt tatra api apara buddhimat kāraṇa adhiṣṭhita tva prasaktiḥ tathā abhyupagame maheśa buddheḥ api anitya tvasya prasādhanāt tasya api apara buddhimat adhiṣṭhita tvam tat buddhau api evam iti anavasthā atha buddheḥ anitya tve sati api na buddhimat adhiṣṭhita tvam tadā vyabhicārī hetuḥ aparam ca atra prativihita tvāt na āśaṅkyate 
TBV_8.72^2	 yat ca kāryatva hetoḥ dūṣanam asiddha tva ādi tat atra api samānam tathā hi yādṛśam anitya tvam buddhimat adhiṣṭhitam vā asya ādau siddham tādṛśam tanu ādiṣu asiddham anitya tva mātrasya pratibandhā siddheḥ vyabhicāraḥ pratibandha abhyupagame sati iṣṭa viparīta sādhanāt viruddha tvam sādharmya dṛṣṭāntasya sādhya vikalatā nitya eka buddhimat adhiṣṭhita tvena sādhya dharmeṇa anvaya asiddheḥ sāmānyena sādhye siddha sādhya tā viśeṣeṇa vyabhicāraḥ ghaṭa ādiṣu anyathā darśanāt iti evam sarvasu prakṛta sādhya sādhanāya upanyasteṣu hetuṣu yojyam 
TBV_8.73^1	 yat ca sthitvā pravṛtteḥ iti sādhanam uktam tatra anyat api dūṣaṇam vācyam sarva bhāvānām udaya sam anantara apavargi tayā kṣaṇa mātram api na sthitiḥ asti iti kutas sthitvā pravṛttiḥ tasmāt prativādya siddhaḥ hetuḥ anaikāntikaḥ ca īśvareṇa eva yatas saḥ api kramavatsu kāryeṣu sthitvā pravartate atha ca na asau cetanāvata adhiṣṭhitaḥ anavasthā prasaṅgāt atha acetana tve sati iti sa viśeṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ upādīyate yathā praśasta m atinā upanyasta s tathā api sandigdha vipakṣa vyāvṛrttika tayā anaikāntika tvam anivāryam yat eva hi viśeṣaṇam vipakṣāt dhetum nivartayati tat eva nyāyyam yat punar vipakṣe sandeham na vyāvartayati tad upādānam api asat kalpam pūrva uktaḥ ca asiddhatā doṣaḥ sa viśeṣaṇa tve api tad avasthaḥ eva 
TBV_8.73^2	 yat ca uktam sarga ādau vyavahāraḥ ca ityādi tatra api uttara kālam prabuddhānām iti etat viśeṣaṇam asiddham tathā hi na asmad mate pralaya kāle pralupta jñāna smṛtayaḥ vitanu karaṇāḥ puruṣāḥ santiṣṭhante kintu ābhāsvara ādiṣu spaṣṭa jñāna atiśaya yogiṣu deva nikāyeṣu upadyante ye tu pratiniyata niraya ādi vipāka saṃvartanīya karmāṇaḥ te lokadhātu antareṣu utpadyante iti matam vivartakāle api tatas eva ābhāsvarā ādeḥ cyutvā iha ālupta jñāna smṛtayaḥ eva sambhavanti tasmāt uttara kālam prabuddhānām iti viśeṣaṇam asiddham anaikāntikaḥ ca hetuḥ sandigdha vipakṣa vyāvṛttika tvāt 
TBV_8.74^1	 kiñca anya upadeśa pūrvakatva mātre sādhye siddha sādhya tā anādeḥ vyavahārasya sarveṣām eva anya upadeśa pūrvaka tvasya iṣṭa tvāt atha īśvara lakṣaṇa puruṣa upadeśa pūrvaka tvam sādhyate tadā anaikāntika tā anyathā api vyavahāra sambhavāt dṛṣṭāntasya ca sādhya vikalatā etat ca anya hetu sāmānyam dūṣaṇam pūrvam uktam viruddhaḥ ca hetuḥ abhyupeta bādhā ca pratijñāyāḥ nirmukhasya upadeṣṭṛtvā sambhavāt yadi īśvara upadeśa pūrvaka tvam vyavahāṛasya sambhavet tadā syāt aviruddha tā hetoḥ yāvatā asau vigata mukha tvāt upadeṣṭā na yuktaḥ tat ca vimukha tvam vitanu tvena tat api dharma adharma virahāt tathā ca uddyota kareṇa uktam yathā buddhi mat tāyām īśvarasya pramāṇa sambhavaḥ na evam dharma ādi nitya tve pramāṇam asti iti tasmāt īśvarasya upadeṣṭṛtva asambhavāt tad upadeśa pūrvaka tvam vyavahārasya na siddhyati kintu īśvara vyatirikta anya puruṣa upadeśa pūrvaka tvam atas iṣṭa vidhātakāri tvāt viruddhaḥ hetuḥ 
TBV_8.74^2	 atha īśvarasya upadeṣṭṛ tvam aṅgīkriyate tadā vimukha tvam abhyupetam hīyate iti abhyupeta bādhaḥ evam anyeṣu api sarvajña tva ādi tad viśeṣa sādhakeṣu hetuṣu asiddha tva anaikānitka tva viruddha tva ādi doṣa jālam sva matya abhyūhyam diś mātra darśana paratvāt prayāsasya atha eva sapta bhuvanāni ekabuddhi nirmitāni  eka vastu antargata tvāt eka āvasatha antargatān eka apavaraka vat yathā eka āvasatha antargatānām apavarakāṇām sūtra dhāra eka buddhi nirmita tvam dṛṣṭam tathā ekasmin eva bhuvane antargatāni sapta bhuvanāni tasmāt teṣām api ekabuddhi nimita tvam niścīyate yat buddhi nirmitāni ca etāni sa bhagavān maheśvaraḥ sakala bhuvana eka sūtra dhāraḥ iti ādikāḥ prayogāḥ praśastam ati prabhṛtibhiḥ upanyastāḥ teśu api hetuḥ asiddhaḥ na hi ekam bhuvanam āvasatha ādiḥ vā asti vyavahāra lāghava artham bahuṣu iyam saṃjñā kṛtā atas eva dṛṣṭāntaḥ api sādhana vikalaḥ eka saudha ādi antargatānām apavaraka ādīnām eka sūtra dhāra ghaṭita tva darśanāt ca anaikāntikaḥ hetuḥ 
TBV_8.75^1	 yat ca eka adhiṣṭhānāḥ brahma ādayaḥ piśāca antāḥ paraspara atiśaya vṛtti tvāt iha yeṣām paraspara atiśaya vṛtti tvam teṣām eka āyattatā dṛṣṭāḥ yathā iha loke gṛha grāma nagara deśa adhipatīnām ekasmin sārvabhauma narapatau tathā ca bhujaga rakṣaḥ yakṣa prabhṛtīnām paraspara atiśaya vṛtti tvam etena manyāmahe teṣām api ekasmin īśvare pāratantryam iti tat etat yadi īśvarādhyena adhiṣṭhāyakena eka adhiṣṭhānāḥ iti ayam arthaḥ sādhayitum iṣṭaḥ tathā anaikāntika tā hetoḥ viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇa abhāvāt pratibandha asiddheḥ dṛṣṭāntasya ca sādhya vikalatā 
TBV_8.75^2	 atha adhiṣṭhāyaka mātreṇa sa adhiṣṭhānāḥ iti sādhyate tadā siddha sādhya tā yatas iṣyate eva sugata sutaiḥ bhagavatā sambuddhena sakala loka cūḍāmaṇinā sarvam eva jagat karuṇā vaśāt adhiṣṭhitam yad prabhāvāt adya api abhyudaya niḥśreyasa sampadam āsādayanti sādhu jana sārthāḥ sarveṣu api ca sarvajña sādhaneṣu para upanyasteṣu yadi sāmānyena kaścid sarvajñaḥ iti sādhyam abhipretam tadā na asmān prati bhavatām idam sādhanam rājate siddha sādhya tā doṣāt kintu ye sarvajña apavādinaḥ jaiminīyāḥ cārvākāḥ vā teṣu eva śobhate 
TBV_8.76	 atha īśva rādhyaḥ sarvajñaḥ sādhyeta tadā ukta prakāreṇa pratibandha asiddheḥ hetūnām anaikāntika tā dṛṣṭāntasya ca sādhya vikalatā iti śeṣaḥ tu pūrva paksa granthaḥ niḥsāra tayā upeksitaḥ atas īśvara sādhakasya tat nitya tva ādi dharma sādhakasya ca pramāṇasya abhāvāt kleśa karma vipāka āśayaiḥ aparāmṛṣṭaḥ puruṣa viśeṣaḥ īśvaraḥ ityādi sarvam ayukta tayā sthitam atas bhava hetu rāga ādi jayāt śāsana praṇetāraḥ jināḥ siddhāḥ atas su vyavasthitam etat bhava jinānām śāsanam iti 
TBV_8.77^1	 nanu yadi teṣām bhava nibandha rāga ādi jetṛ tvam tadā śāsana praṇetṛ tva anupapattiḥ tad jaya anantaram eva apavarga prāpteḥ śarīra abhāve vaktṛ tva asambhavāt atha rāga ādi kṣaya anantaram na apavarga prāptiḥ tarhi rāga ādi jayaḥ na bhava kṣaya lakṣaṇa apavarga prāpti kāraṇam na hi yasmin sati api yat na bhavati tat tad avikala kāraṇam vyavasthāpayitum śakyam yava bījam iva śāli aṅkurasya atha niravaśeṣa rāga ādyajayāt apavarga prāpteḥ prāk eva tad praṇetṛ tvāt adoṣaḥ nanu enam tat śāsanasya rāga śleśa āśliṣṭa puruṣa praṇīta tvena na aikāntikam prāmāṇyam kapila ādi puruṣa praṇītasya iva iti āśaṅkya āha sūriḥ ṭhāṇam aṇovama suham uvagayāṇam iti asya abhiprāyaḥ yadi api sarvajña tā pratibandhi ghāti karma catuṣṭa ya kṣāya avibhūta kevala jñāna sampadaḥ jināḥ tathā api bhava upagrāhi śarīra nibandhanasya karmanaḥ sadbhāvāt alpa sthitikasya na śarīra ādi a bhāvāt śāsana pranetṛtva anupapattiḥ na api rāga ādi leśa sadbhāvāt tad praṇīta āgamasya aprāmāṇyam viparyāsa hetoḥ ghātikarmaṇaḥ atyanta kṣayāt 
TBV_8.77^2	 na ca karma kṣayāt aparasya apravṛtti nimitta tvam bhava upagrāhiṇaḥ adya api sāmastyena akṣayāt tad kṣaye ca apavargasya anantara bhāvi tvāt karma kṣayasya eva apavarga prāptau avikala kāraṇa tvāt iti avayava arthaḥ tu tiṣṭhanti sakala karma kṣaya avāpta ananta jñāna sukha rūpa adhyāsitāḥ śuddha ātmanaḥ asmin iti sthānām loka agra lakṣaṇam viśiṣṭa kṣetram na vidyate upamā svābhāvika ātyantika tvena sakala vyābādhā rahita tvena ca sarva sukha atiśāyi tvāt yasya tat sukham ānanda rūpam yasmin tat tathā tat upa iti kāla sāmīpyena gatānām prāptānām yat vā upa iti upasargaḥ prakarṣe api upalabhyate yathā upoḍha rāgeṇa iti tena sthānam anupama sukham prakarṣeṇa gatānām iti para arthe prayujyamānāḥ śābdāḥ vatim antareṇa api tam artham gamayanti iti nyāyāt anubhūyamāna tīrtha kṛnnām karma leśa sadbhāve api tat gatāḥ iva gatāḥ iti uktāḥ tena śāsana praṇetṛ tvam tasyām avasthāyām teṣām upapannam eva 
TBV_8.78–8.79	 yat vā muktāḥ sarvatra niṣṭhanti vyoma vat tāpa varjitāḥ iti etasya durnayasya nirāsa artham āha sūriḥ ṭhāṇam aṇovama suham uvagayāṇam atra ca sthānam anupama sukham prakarṣeṇa apunarāvṛttyā gatānām upagatānām iti vyākhyeyam atha vā buddhi ādīnām navānām viśeṣa guṇānām ātyantikaḥ kṣayaḥ ātmanaḥ muktiḥ iti mata vyavaccheda artham ācāryeṇa ṭāṇam aṇovama suham uvagayāṇam iti sūtram upanystam asya ca ayam arthaḥ sthitiḥ sthānam svarūpa prāptiḥ tat anupama sukham upa iti sakala karma kṣaya anantaram avyavadhānena gatānām prāptānām śaileśya vasthā caram asamayā upādeya bhūtam ananta sukha svabhāvam ātmanaḥ kathaṃcid ananya bhūtam svarūpam prāptānām iti yāvat
